SURAH AL HIJR (15)

           *25th Muharram 1443*

 *4th September 2021, Saturday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦️ SURAH AL-HIJR♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1747)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الۤرۚ تِلۡكَ ءَایَـٰتُ ٱلۡكِتَـٰبِ وَقُرۡءَانࣲ مُّبِینࣲ.*

"Alif Laam Raa. Ye Ki Kitab e Ilahi aur Qur'an e Mubeen ki Ayaat hain."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 1)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📖

Aaj se Surah Al-Hijr ka aghaaz kiya ja raha hai.

📚

Is Surah mein Allah Ta'ala ne apne Habib (saww) ko tasalli di hai ke Mazaaq udane walon ki parwa na karen. Jo log Qur'an Majeed ke khilaf bol rahe hain un se hargiz ma'roob na hon. Rasool ka Mojeza Qur'an aur Aap (saww) Nabuwwat ta Qayamat baqi rahegi. Pichhle Rasoolon ki Ummat ne bhi Mazaaq udaya tha magar woh tabah o barbad hi gaye. Kafir chahe kitne Mojize dekh le phir bhi Islam qubool nahi karenge.

Aasmaan mein Khuda ne Burj banaye aur Shaayateen se inki Hifazat ka intezam kiya. Khuda ne Zameen bichhayi, Rizq ka Intezam kiya, Hawa ko baese Barkat rakha. Khuda agle pichhle tamam logon ko jaanta hai.

Is Surah ke doosre Topic hain: Takhleeq e Adam (as), Inkaare Iblis, Jannat ke 7 Darwaze. Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke Mehmano ka Qissa, Qaum e Lut ki barbadi, Ashaabul Aika ki tabahi, Zameen o Aasmaan ki Takhleeq ka maqsad, Surah Fateh ki Azmat waghaira. Ye sab is surah ke ahm Mauzoo hain jo tafseel se bayan honge.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*

🙇 📚

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jo shakhs Namaz ki do Rakat ada kare aur Pehli Rakat mein Surah Fateha ke baad Surah Ibrahim aur doosri Rakat mein Surah Al-Hijr padhe to woh kabhi Muflis (Poor) na hoga aur woh kabhi Pagal na hoga aur us par koi Azmaish nahi aayegi."

(Kitab Sawabul Amaal, Noorus Saqlain)

📚

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Jo shakhs Surah Al-Hijr padhe to woh kabhi Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki Zindagi mein jitne Muhajir o Ansar the aur jin logon ne AanHazrat (saww) ka Mazaaq udaya tha un sab ki tadaad se 10 guna zyada Allah Ta'ala use Nekiyan ata karega."

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Aaqa! Is chahnewale ka Adaab qubool kijiye jo Aapke Gham mein nidhaal, behaal o bechain hai.

Aaqa! Is Jaanisar ka Hadiya e Salam qubool kijiye. Jo agar Karbala mein Aapke saath hota to Aapki hifazat ke liye Talwaaron se takra kar apni Jaan ki baazi laga deta. Dilo Jaan se Aap par fida hone ke liye Maut se Panja Azmayi karta, Aapke saamne Jang o Jihad ke johar dikhata, Aapke khilaf baghawat karne walon ke muqabile mein Aapki madad karta aur anjamkar apna Jism o Jaan, Rooh o Maal aur Aal Aulaad sab kuchh aap par qurban kar deta....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

*EVENT OF THE DAY:*

😭😢

Imam Sadiq (as):

Imam Baqir (as) ne farmaya:

"Jab mere Pidar e Buzurgwaar *Imam Zainul Abedin (as)* ka waqt e Shahadat aaya to aap ne farmaya, "Aye Farzand! Ye wo shab hai jis shab mera Waada e Wafaat hai. Mere Naaqe (oo'nttni) ko uski jagah baandh do aur kuchh chaara uske aage daal do". Jab *Imam Sajjad (as)* ko dafn kiya gaya to Naaqa apni rassi tod-ke bhaaga aur Qabr ke nazdeek ja kar apna Mun'h unki Qabr ke upar rakhta aur faryaad aur naala karta tha, Aa'nkho'n se Aa'nsu jaari the. Jab ye khabar Imam Baqir (as) ko pahu'nchi to wo us Naaqe ke paas aaye aur farmaya, "Chup reh aur phir ja. Khuda tujhe Barkat de". Ye sun kar Naaqa apni jagah chala gaya. Phir thode arse ke baad doosri martaba Qabr e Shareef ke paas aa kar Naala o Iztiraab karta aur rota tha. Is martaba jo uska haal logo'n ne Imam se bayaan kiya to unhone farmaya, "Usko uske haal par chhor do, wo bahut betaab hai". Phir 3 din baad wo Naaqa shaheed ho gaya. *Imam Sajjad (as)* ne us Naaqe par 22 Hajj kiye the aur Taziyana (whip/koda) bhi nahi maara tha."

(Jila ul Uyoon - Allamah Majlisi, v2, p368; 14 Sitaarey, p307; Tehzeeb ul Islam, p377)

   ♦️ KAFIRON KA PASTAWA♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1748)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*رُّبَمَا یَوَدُّ ٱلَّذِینَ كَفَرُوا۟ لَوۡ كَانُوا۟ مُسۡلِمِینَ * ذَرۡهُمۡ یَأۡكُلُوا۟ وَیَتَمَتَّعُوا۟ وَیُلۡهِهِمُ ٱلۡأَمَلُۖ فَسَوۡفَ یَعۡلَمُونَ.*

"Ek Din wo aanewala hai jab Kuffar bhi ye tamanna karenge ke kaash woh bhi Musalman hote."

"(Ay Rasool) Aap unhe unke haal par chhod den, khayen, piyen, maze karen aur Ummeeden unhe bhulawe mein dale rakhen. Anqareeb unhe sab kuchh maloom ho jayega."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 2 - 3)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:  

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

😕

Imam Baqir (as):

"Qayamat ke Din ek Munadi Nida karega jise tamam Ahle Mehshar sunenge. Woh kahega ke Jannat mein sirf Muslim hi dakhil ho sakta hai. Us waqt tamam Kuffar hasrat se is Khwahish ka izhaar karenge ke kaash woh bhi Muslim hote."

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤔

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Gunehgar Dozakh mein jayenge. Un mein kuchh Gunehgar Ahle Qibla bhi shamil honge. Dozakh mein Kuffar Musalmano se kahenge ke kya Musalman nahi the? Woh kahenge: 'Ji haan, ham Musalman the. Kafir kahenge, lekin tumhare Islam ne tumhe koi fayda nahi diya, tum bhi to hamare saath Dozakh mein ho."

"Musalman kahenge, 'Hamne Zindagi mein Gunah kiye the jiski wajah se Khuda ne hamari giraftar kiya hai. Jab Allah Ta'ala ye Guftagu sunega to Woh Hukm jaari karega ke tamam Musalmano ko Dozakh se nikaal lo. (Us waqt Musalman Dozakh se nikaal liye jayenge.) Us waqt Kafir Hasrat se kahenge, 'Kash ham bhi Musalman hote.'"

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

😔

Riwayaat ke mutabiq is tarah Dushmanan Vilayat bhi is tarah ki hasrat karenge jab Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ko Hauz e Kausar par Qaseem e Jannat o Naar ke taur par dekhenge ke kaash mein bhi Ahle Vilayat mein se hota.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hamari Wilayat Amal se milti hai. Beshak roz e Qayamat sab se zyada woh aadmi hasrat karega, jo Adaalat ki riayat (insaaf ka paalan) to karta ho, lekin uske Amal aur qaul mein tazaad (conflict/takrao) ho."

(Mafaatih al Hayaat, p479)

📖

Hikaayat (Anecdote):

Umr bin Lais jo Khurasan ke Sultan mein se tha aur bada pehelwaan aur qawi Daulatmand tha aur bahut badi fauj rakhta tha. Jab woh mar gaya to logo'n ne use khwaab mein bahut achche haal mein dekha to puchha ke tumhari bakshish ka kya sabab hua? Usne kaha, "Ek din main ek pahaad par tha aur apni be-shumaar fauj ka mulaheza kar raha tha. Unki kasrat (zyadati) par khushi ke saath us waqt mujhe hasrat hui ke kaash main apni is fauj ke saath Sayyadus Shohada (as) ke muhaarbe ke din (Aashur ke Din) Imam (as) ke paas hota to Imam (as) ke Dushmano'n se khoob muqabla karta aur un paleedo'n ko khoob maarta-koott'ta. Pus, isi hasrat ki ba-daulat Allah Ta'ala ne mujhe baksh diya aur mujhe Jannat naseeb hui."

(Kitaab Waseelatun Najaat, Isbaat e Azadari, p24)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Aaqa! Is Jaanisar ka Salam qubool kijiye jiski Rooh par fida aur uske Ahlo Ayaal Aapke Ahl o Ayaal par tasadduq.

Maula! Mein Waqae Shahadat ke baad paida hua, apni qismat ke sabab mein Huzoor ki Nusrat se mehroom raha, Aapke saamne Maidan e Karzar mein utarne walon mein shamil na ho saka, aur na hi mein Aapke Dushmanon se nabrdaazma (no fight) ho saka. Lehaza ab mein Kamale Hasrat o ando ke saath Aap par tootne wale Masaeb o Aalaam par afsos o malaal aur tapish e ranj o gham ke sabab Subah o Shaam musalsal girya o zari karta rahunga. Nez Aapke Khoon ki jagah is qadar Khoon ke Aansu bahahunga ke anjaamkar gham o Andoh ki bhatti aur Musibaton ke lapakte hue sholon mein jal kar khaakstar ho jaon aur yun Aapke Huzoor apni Jaan ka nazrana pesh kar dun....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔹🔹🔹🔹﷽🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

         *27th Muharram 1441*

  *6th September 2021, Monday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

           ♦ AZAAB-E-ILAHI ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1749)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَاۤ أَهۡلَكۡنَا مِن قَرۡیَةٍ إِلَّا وَلَهَا كِتَابࣱ مَّعۡلُومࣱ * مَّا تَسۡبِقُ مِنۡ أُمَّةٍ أَجَلَهَا وَمَا یَسۡتَـٔۡخِرُونَ*  

"Hamne jis bhi Basti ko Halaak kiya hai, uske liye ek khaas Mohlat e Amal likhi ja chuki thi. Koi Qaum na apne Waqt e muqarrar se pehle Halaak ho sakti hai aur na uske baad chhoot sakti hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 4 - 9)

**********************************

"Hamne tumse pehli Aqwaam (Tribes, Groups) ko halaak kar diya jab unhone Zulm ki rawish apnayi aur unke Rasool unke paas khuli Nishaniyan le kar aaye magar woh Imaan laanewale na the. Ham isi tarah se Mujrim ko Badla diya karte hain. Iske baad Hamne tumko Zameen par unka Janasheen bana diya taake Ham ye dekhen ke tum kaise Amal karte ho?"

(Surah Yunus: 13 - 14)

📚📖 🌵

👉 Tafseer:

Isse milti julti doosri Ayaton ka zikr guzishta Messages mein ho chuka hai. Mufhoom same hai isliye phir se repeat kar rahe hain:

*أَلَمْ يَرَوْا كَمْ أَهْلَكْنَا.........*

"Kiya unhone nahi dekha ke Hamne unse qabl kitni aisi qaumon ko halak kiya hai jinhen Hamne Zameen mein aisa Aqdaar diya tha ke is jaisa Aqdaar tumhe nahi diya. Hamne un par Aasmaan se khoob Baarish barsayen aur Hamne unke neeche Nehren baha di thi. Akhirkar Hamne unhein Gunahon ki padaash mein halaak kar diya aur unki jagah doosri qaumon ko le aye."

(Surah An'am: 6)

👥👉🏻

Zajaj ka kahna hai ke Qarn *قرن* ka itlaq us muddat ke logon par hota hai jin mein koi Nabi ho ya Ahle Ilm ka koi tabqa ho aur is mein kam saal ya zyada saal ho isse koi farq nahi padta kiyonki Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya:

*خيركم قرني ثم الذين يلونهم.*

"Mera daur sab se behtar hai. Phir un logon ka daur behtar hai jo iske baad ayenge."

(Tafseer Majmaul Bayan)

🐲

Allah ne Guroor o Takabbur karne wale, Sarkash, Zalim logon par etaab ki barish barsa kar halaak kar diya. Ye sabaq ainda qaumon ke liye hai ke sarkashi ka natija kiya hota hai.

Aaj kal bhi aap log dekhte honge ke kahin Selaab, to kahin Zalzala to kahin bijli ka girna wa bhari barsat hona jiske natije mein sekdon ya hazaron log halaak ho jaate hain. Allah Zalim nahi, Woh zulm nahi karta lekin Zalim ko kadi se kadi saza bhi deta hai. Ye sab hadsaat o waqeat doosron logon ke liye sabaq hote hain taake woh hoshiyar ho jayen.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 🌵🐲

Ameerul Mo'meneen Imam Ali (as)

"Tajjub hai aur mujhe kaise tajjub na ho un giroho'n ki khataao'n par jinhone apne Deen ki Hujjato'n mein ikhtelaaf paida kar rakhe hain. Jo na Nabi ke naqsh e qadam par chalte hain, na Wasi ke amal ki pairavi karte hain, na Gaib par Imaan laate hain, na Aib se daaman bachaate hain. Maskook (doubtful) cheezo'n par amal karte hain aur apni khwaisho'n (ki duniya) mein chalte phirte hain. Unke nazdeek bus wohi cheez achchi hai jisko wo achcha samajhte hain aur wohi cheez buri hai jisko wo bura jaante hain. Mushkil gutthiyo'n ko suljhaane ke liye unhone apne Nafso'n par etemaad kar liya hai aur mushtaba (Doubtful) cheezo'n mein apni raai par bharosa kar liya hai, goya unme se har shakhs apna Imam hai aur usne apni jagah jo faisla apni raai se kar liya hai uske baare mein ye khayaal karta hai ke ise qaabil e itminaan zariyo'n se haasil kiya hai."

(Gorar ul Hakam, Vol 2, p494, Nahjul Balagah, Khutba 88 (Jisme Logo'n Ki Halaakat Ke Asbaab Bayaan Kiye Gaye Hain)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"Aaqa! Mein Shahadat deta hun ke: 'Aapne Namaz qayem karne ka Haq ada farmaya, Zakat ada ki, Neki ka hukm diya, aur Burai aur Dushmani se roka, Dil o Jaan se Allah ki Ita'at ki. Pal bhar ke liye bhi Uski Nafarmani nahi ki. Allah aur Uski Rassi se yun wabasta rahe ke Uski Reza hasil kar li. Hamesha Uske Ahkam ki nigehdasht o paasbani karte rahe, Uski Awaaz par Labbaik kahi. Uski Sutoon (pillers) ko qayem ki......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

           ♦ HATDHARMI ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1750)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَّوۡ مَا تَأۡتِینَا بِٱلۡمَلَـٰۤىِٕكَةِ إِن كُنتَ مِنَ ٱلصَّـٰدِقِینَ * مَا نُنَزِّلُ ٱلۡمَلَـٰۤىِٕكَةَ إِلَّا بِٱلۡحَقِّ وَمَا كَانُوۤا۟ إِذࣰا مُّنظَرِینَ.*

"(Unhone kaha:) Agar tu apne daawe mein sachcha hai to hamare paas Farishte kyon nahi le aata. Ham Farishton ko (yun hi nahi nazil karte, jab woh nazil hote hain to) Haq ke Faisle ke saath bheja karte hain. Phir logon ko Mohlat nahi di jati."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 7 - 8)

**********************************

"Aur agar Ham unki taraf Farishton ko nazil karte aur Murde unse kalam karte aur Ham har cheez unki Ankhon ke saamne jama kar dete tab bhi ye Imaan na laate. Albatta Mashiyat e Ilahi isse mustashna (exception) hai. Lekin unki aksariyat Jihalat mein mubtila hai."

(Surah An'am: 111)

📚📖 🌵

👉 Tafseer:*

Isse milti julti doosri Ayaton ka zikr bhi guzishta Messages mein ho chuka hai.

Guzishta Ayat mein Azab e Ilahi ka zikr hua. In Ayaton mein Kafiron aur Mushrekin ki hatdharmiyan ko zahir kiya gaya hai. Jaisa ke unhone bahut se taqaze kiye jaise Allah ko dekhna, koi Mo'jeza dekhana waghaira. Balke woh Qasmen bhi khaate the ke woh Imaan le ayenge lekin Khuda ne is ayat bata diya ke agar unke saamne Farishta bhi aa jaye, ya unse ek Murda bhi bolne lage tab bhi ye Imaan nahi layenge.

Iski wajah unki Jihalat hai. Jaisa ke pahle bhi explain kar chuke hain, agar Allah chahta to apni Qudrat se sab ko Momin bana deta lekin ye Uski Adalat ke khilaf hota. Isko aisa samjha ja sakta ke ek Teacher apne Student se exam le aur wohi usko copy karne de, to exam meaningless ho jayega, ye Student ke saath ghair insaafi hogi, kyonki woh jahil ka jahil hi rahega.

Isliye Allah ne iska Natija bhi bata diya ke agar Mo'jeza/Farishte dekh kar bhi na maana to phir koi Mohlat nahi di jayegi aur un par Azaab hatmi aa kar rahega.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 🌵🐲

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Reza (as):

"Kya tu nahi jaanta ke Allah ne apni Zameen ko Nabi ya Imam se khali nahi chhoda aur Nabi ya Imam ka talluq Insaano ki sinf (type) se hi hota hai jaisa ke Allah Ta'ala ne Farmaya: (12:109) Allah Ta'ala ne Zameen par Malaika ko kabhi Imam aur Haakim bana kar nahi bheja. Malaika ki duty ye hai ke woh Khuda ka Paigham Anbiya tak pahunchayen."

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Kazim (as):

"Kul (tamaam) aadmiyo'n par Allah ki 2 Hujjaten hain, ek Hujjat e Zaahiri aur ek Hujjat e Baatini. Hujjat e Zaahiri to Rasool aur Anbiya aur Aimma e Masumeen (as) hain aur Hujjat e Baatini (inner) khud unki (aadmiyo'n) ki Aql hai."

(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p74)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".......Fitno ki bhadakti hui Aag ko bujhaya. Logon ko Haq o Hidayat ki taraf bulaya, unke liye Hidayat ke Raaston ko Roshan o Munawwar karke wazeh kiya. Nez Aapne Allah ke Raaste mein Jihad karne ka Haq ada kar diya.

Aaqa! Mein Dilo Jaan se Gawahi deta hun ke: Aap hamesha Dil se Allah ke Farmabardar rahe. Aapne hamesha apne Jadd e Amjad (saww) ki itteba aur pairavi ki, Apne Walid e Majid ke Irshadaat ko suna aur us par amal kiya. Bhai ki Wasiyyat ki tezi se takmeel ki. Deem ke Sutoon (pillers) ko buland kiya. Baghawaton ka qila qama kiya, nez Sarkashon aur Baghiyon ki sarkoobi ki....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

   ♦️ QUR'AN MEIN TEHREEF? ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1751)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالُوا۟ یَـٰۤأَیُّهَا ٱلَّذِی نُزِّلَ عَلَیۡهِ ٱلذِّكۡرُ إِنَّكَ لَمَجۡنُونࣱ*

 *إِنَّا نَحۡنُ نَزَّلۡنَا ٱلذِّكۡرَ وَإِنَّا لَهُۥ لَحَـٰفِظُونَ.*

"Un logon ne kaha: 'Aye woh Shakhs jis par Zikr (Qur'an) nazil kiya gaya hai, tu Diwana hai."

"Hamne hi Zikr (Qur'an) ko Nazil kiya aur Ham hi iski Hifazat Karnewale hain."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 6 & 9)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Aaj se Qur'an ki Tehreef ke mauzoo par tazkara hoga. Kyunki is mein bahut si ghalaf fehmiyan payi jati hain.

📚

Kaffiron ne us Zaat ki mazaq udayi jis par Allah ka Kalam Qur'an e Karim nazil hua, jis mein Duniya ki har khusk o tar maujood hai. Aur ye kehte hain: 'tu pagal hai kya?' Pagal to ye kafir hain.

Kuffar ne Qur'an Majeed ko Lafz "Az-Zikr" se tabeer kiya hai. Allah Ta'ala ne is Zikr yaani Qur'an Majeed ki Hifazat ki zimmedari Apne Zimme li hai aur is Zimmedari ka Ailaan kiya hai.

Qur'an e Karim ki ye Ayat is Amr par dalalat karti hai ke Qur'an har tarah ki Tehreef (Modification) se Mehfooz hai, kyonki woh Allah ka Nazil kardah Zikr hai aur wo hamesha zinda o paindah rehnewala Zikr hai. Aur Zikr ke liye shart ye hai ke Baatil ki har qism ki amezish (milawat) se Paak ho. (41:41-42)

Is maqam par ye keh dena ke Zikr se Rasoole Khuda (saww) murad hain aur Allah ne unki Hifazat ka Ailaan kiya hai, sarasar ghalat aur sayaq e Qur'an ke khilaf hai. Maktabe Tashayyo (Shia) ke Muhaqqeqin ka hamesha ye Nazariya hai ke Qur'an e Hakim har tarah ki Tehreef se Paak hai, jaisa ke Shaikh Sadooq, Syed Murtaza, Shaikh Tusi aur Mufassir Tabarsi (ar) ne isi mauzoo par Millat e Jafariya ke Aqeede ko wazeh kiya hai aur Shaikh Sadooq ke Nazariye ke mutabiq is par Imamiya Ulama o Mujtahedin ka Ijma hai. Chunache Shaikh Sadooq (ar) likhte hain:

"Qur'an Majeed ke bare mein hamara Aqeeda ye hai ke Allah ne jo Qur'an Apne Paighambar par Nazil kiya hai wohi hai jo do Daftiyon yani do Gatton ke darmiyan maujood aur logon ke haath mein hai.' Isse zyada nahi hai aur jo shakhs hamari taraf se is baat ki nisbat deta hai ke ham ye kehte hain ke Qur'an isse zyada hai to woh Jhoota hai."

(Eteqadaat e Sadooq)

(To be Cont'd......)

   ♦️ QUR'AN MEIN TEHREEF?♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1752)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالُوا۟ یَـٰۤأَیُّهَا ٱلَّذِی نُزِّلَ عَلَیۡهِ ٱلذِّكۡرُ إِنَّكَ لَمَجۡنُونࣱ*

 *إِنَّا نَحۡنُ نَزَّلۡنَا ٱلذِّكۡرَ وَإِنَّا لَهُۥ لَحَـٰفِظُونَ.*

"Un logon ne kaha: 'Aye woh Shakhs jis par Zikr (Qur'an) nazil kiya gaya hai, tu Diwana hai."

"Hamne hi Zikr (Qur'an) ko Nazil kiya aur Ham hi iski Hifazat Karnewale hain."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 6 & 9)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Tehreef e Qur'an ke mutalliq Zikr jari hai.

Ulama ka moqif is tarah hai:

Shaikh Tusi (ar):

"Rahi ye baat ke Qur'an mein kisi qism ki kami beshi hai to ye ek aisi baat hai jise bayan karne ki zaroorat nahi hai. Is mein beshi aur izaafe ke mutalliq poore Alam e Islam ka Ijma hai ke Qur'an mein koi izafi lafz nahi hai aur kami ke mutalliq bhi Ulama e Islam ka Ijma hai ke is mein koi kami nahi hai aur yahi baat hamare Mazhab e Imamiya ke ain mutabiq hai."

Syed Murtaza (ar) ka bhi yehi muqif hai.

📚

Mufassir Tabarsi (ar):

"Qur'an mein kisi tarah ke izaafe ki baat to ijmayi taur par baatil hai albatta Ulama e Shia aur Sunni mein baaz hazrat is tarah ki Riwayaat naql ki hain jin se ye ishara milta hai ke Quran mein kami waqe hui hai. Is silsile mein hamare Ulama ka sahih moqif ye hai ke Qur'an mein koi kami nahi hui. Qur'an e Karim ki sehet e naql ke bare mein is qadr Ilm o yaqeen hai jis qadr Mulkon, Shehron, bade bade Waqea'at, Azeem Hawadis, Mashhoor Kitab aur Tehreer shuda Asha'ar ke bar mein Ilm o Yaqeen hai. Qur'an e Karim Nabi e Akram (saww) ki Nabuwwat ka Mo'jeza hai aur Uloom e Shar'iyyah aur Ahkam e Deeniyah ka Maakhaz (Source) hai aur Ummat e Islamiyah ke Ulama ne iski hifazat o hirasat mein apni akheri koshish tak sarf ki hain yahan tak ke unhone iske Eraab, Qara'at aur Huroof o Ayaat mein jo Ikhtilafat dekha use bhi bayan kiya hai to phir is qade shahdeed tawajjoh aur sachchi koshishon ke hote hue is mein tabdeeli o taghayyur ya kami beshi kaise ho sakti hai."

"Syed Murtaza (ar) ne zikr kiya hai ke is bare mein jo shakhs ikhtilaf kare khwa uska talluq Imamiya se ho ya doore Awamun Nas se to unke in ikhtilaf ki tarf tawajjoh nahi ki jayegi aur ise ahmiyyat ke layeq nahi samjha jayega. Albatta baaz Muhaddesin ne Zaeef Riwayaat ka sahara liya hai aur inhe naql kar ke ye samajh liya hai ke ye sahih Ahadis hain."

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

📚

Lekin Allama Majlis ka moqif kuchh mukhtalif hai jo riwayaat ke mutabiq hai. Is link mein unka moqif darj hai (English):

https://al-mumtahana.blogspot.com/2021/04/majlisi-revived-my-people-part-1.html?m=1

  ♦️ QUR'AN MEIN TEHREEF?♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1753)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالُوا۟ یَـٰۤأَیُّهَا ٱلَّذِی نُزِّلَ عَلَیۡهِ ٱلذِّكۡرُ إِنَّكَ لَمَجۡنُونࣱ*

 *إِنَّا نَحۡنُ نَزَّلۡنَا ٱلذِّكۡرَ وَإِنَّا لَهُۥ لَحَـٰفِظُونَ.*

"Un logon ne kaha: 'Aye woh Shakhs jis par Zikr (Qur'an) nazil kiya gaya hai, tu Diwana hai."

"Hamne hi Zikr (Qur'an) ko Nazil kiya aur Ham hi iski Hifazat Karnewale hain."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 6 & 9)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 _*Tafseer:*_  (Cont'd)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Tehreef e Qur'an ke mutalliq Zikr jari hai.

📚📖

Ye Ayat (15:9) Qur'an e Majeed ke Ghair Muharrif hone ki badi Daleel hai.

Zara sochye Allah ne kis Hifazat ki Zimmedari li hai. Agar Qur'an e Karim ko Paani mein dala jaye to doob jata hai. Agar kisi Ghar mein Qur'an e Hakim maujood ho aur ittifaq se us Ghar mein Aag lag jaye to Qur'an Majeed bhi nazar e Aatish ho jata hai. Agar koi badbakht Qur'an e Karim ko phaadna chahe to wo phat jata hai magar iske bawajood Allah ne iski Hifazat ko Zimmedari Apne Zimme ki hai. Maloom hota hai ke Allah ne jis Hifazat ka Wada kiya hai uska talluq kami beshi ya taghayyur o tabdeel se hai. Allah ne ye Zimmedari li hai ke Mein ia mein kisi tarah ki kami beshi nahi hone dunga.

Iske alawa Qur'an e Karim Risaalat e Muhammadiya (saww) ka Azeem Mo'jeza hai. Agar Risaalat Ma'ab ka ye Azeem Mo'jeza bhi logon ke daste tasarruf se Mehfooz na rahe to Risaalat e Muhammadiya ki Gawahi mutassir hoti hai.

📚

https://al-mumtahana.blogspot.com/2021/04/majlisi-revived-my-people-part-1.html?m=1

  ♦️ QUR'AN MEIN TEHREEF?♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1754)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالُوا۟ یَـٰۤأَیُّهَا ٱلَّذِی نُزِّلَ عَلَیۡهِ ٱلذِّكۡرُ إِنَّكَ لَمَجۡنُونࣱ*

 *إِنَّا نَحۡنُ نَزَّلۡنَا ٱلذِّكۡرَ وَإِنَّا لَهُۥ لَحَـٰفِظُونَ.*

"Un logon ne kaha: 'Aye woh Shakhs jis par Zikr (Qur'an) nazil kiya gaya hai, tu Diwana hai."

"Hamne hi Zikr (Qur'an) ko Nazil kiya aur Ham hi iski Hifazat Karnewale hain."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 6 & 9)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Tehreef e Qur'an ke mutalliq Zikr jari hai.

📚📖

Khuda Wande Alam ka ye Usool raha hai ke jis bhi Kitab mein Tehreef hui Allah ne uski jagah naya Rasool bheja aur nayi Kitab bheji. Agar Khuda na khwasta Qur'an mein bhi Tehreef ka imkaan hota to Allah Haamil e Qur'an ko Khatimul Anbiya na banata aur Qur'an ko Akheri Ilhaami Kitab na banata.

📚

Islami Ahkam ke do hi Sarchashme (Sources) hain. Pehle Source ka naam Qur'an hai aur doosre Source ka naam Hadis hai. Hadis ke liye shart ye hai ke wo Qur'an ke mutabiq ho. Agar Khuda na khwasta Qur'an hi mein Tehreef aa jaye to Hadis ki Mutabiqat kis cheez se ki jayegi kyonki agar Mizaan (Criteria, Scale) hi sire se ghalat ho to us par se etemad uth jayega aur jo cheez Mizaan par toli jayegi uska koi aitbar nahi hoga. Lehaza Tehreef e Qur'an ke Aqeede se Islami Ahkam ki Buniyad hi mashkook (doubtful) ho jati hai Islami Ahkam ki Asaas (buniyad) kp sahih maanne ke liye zaroori hai ke Qur'an ko Ghair Muharrif (Unchanged) tasleem kiya jaye.

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

(Al Kaafi, v5, p284)

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"Maula! Aapki Shaan o Sifaat ye hain ke: Zimmedariyon ko poora karnewale, Sahebe Ausaaf e Hameeda, Jood o Karam mein mashoor, Shab ki Tareekiyon mein Tahajjud guzar, Mazboot tareeqon ko ikhtiyar karnewale, Khalqe Khuda mein sab se zyada Khoobiyon ke Malik, Azeem Maazi ke haamil, Aala Hasab o Nasab wale, Buland martabon aur be panaah Manaqib ka Markaz, Pasandeeda Namuna e Amal ke khaaliq, Misaali Zindagi basar karnewale, Bawaqar, Burdbar, Buland Martaba, Daryadil, Dana wa Beena, Sahebe Azm o Jazm, Khuda Shanaas Rehbar, Khauf o Khashiyyat aur Soz o Tapish rakhne wale, Khuda ke chahne aur nez Uski Bargah mein Sar newdanewale. Aap Rasool e Akram (saww) ke Farzand, Qur'an ke bachanewale, Ummat ke Madadgar, Ita'at e Ilahi mein jafa kash, Ahd o Misaaq ke paband o Muhafiz, Fasiqon ke Raaston se door rehnewale, husool e Maqsad ke liye Dil o Jaan ki baazi laganewale, aur toolani Ruku o Sujood ada karnewale....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  ♦️ QUR'AN MEIN TEHREEF?♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1755)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالُوا۟ یَـٰۤأَیُّهَا ٱلَّذِی نُزِّلَ عَلَیۡهِ ٱلذِّكۡرُ إِنَّكَ لَمَجۡنُونࣱ*

 *إِنَّا نَحۡنُ نَزَّلۡنَا ٱلذِّكۡرَ وَإِنَّا لَهُۥ لَحَـٰفِظُونَ.*

"Un logon ne kaha: 'Aye woh Shakhs jis par Zikr (Qur'an) nazil kiya gaya hai, tu Diwana hai."

"Hamne hi Zikr (Qur'an) ko Nazil kiya aur Ham hi iski Hifazat Karnewale hain."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 6 & 9)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Tehreef e Qur'an ke mutalliq Zikr jari hai.

📚📖

Qur'an e Karim ke Ghair Muharrif hone ki azeem Daleel Hadis e Saqlain hai. Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne apni Zindagi mein mutaddid maqamat par farmaya:

*إِنِّی تَارِک فِیکمْ الثَّقَلَینِ کتَابَ اللَّهِ وَ عِتْرَتِی أَهْلَ بَیتِی فَاِن تَمَسَّكتُم بِهِمَا لَنْ تَضِلُّوا بَعدِى اَبَدًا.*

"Mein tumhare darmiyan do giraan qadr cheezen chhod kar ja raha hun aur wo hain Qur'an aur meri Itrat Ahle Bait (as), jab tak tum in dono se tamassuk (touch mein) rahoge to mere baad harguz Gumrah na hoge."

Ahlebait (as) se har Syed murad nahi hai balke Aimma e Huda (as) murad hain jinke pehle fard Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) aur Akheri fard Hazrat Imam e Zamana (atfs) hain. Imam e Zamana (atfs) Ghaibat e Kubra ke Parde mein hain aur jab Khuda ka Hukm hoga to woh Zahoor farmayenge. Ab Amali taur par (practically) Ahlebait (as) se istefada ka darwaza band hai. Ab sirf Qur'an e Majeed hi baqi reh jata hai. Woh Hazraat jo chand ghair sahih riwayaat maan kar Tehreef e Qur'an ka isbaat karte hain ham unse poochhne mein haq bajanib hain ke silsila e Nabuwwat to ek taweel arse se munqata ho chuka hai aur silsila e Imamat se Amali taur par Ghaibat e Kubra ke ayyam mein istefada mushkil hai. Agar Khuda na khwasta Qur'an e Karim mein bhi Tehreef waaqe ho chuki to unke paas apne Islam ka kya jawaz hai kyonki na to unki nazar mein Qur'an sahih hai aur nahi Aimma e Huda (as) se direct contact hai jabke Gumrahi se bachane wale Aawamil (Factors) to sirf yehi the aur dono se mehroom ho chuke hain. Phir iske bawajood woh agar Musalman hain to kis buniyad par Musalman hain?

Iske alawa Ahlebait e Taherin (as) apni poori zindagi mein apne maanne walon ko Qur'an e Karim ki taraf rujoo ka hukm diya tha. Agar Khuda na khwasta Qur'an mein koi Tehreef hoti to Aimma e Huda (as) Qur'an ki taraf rujoo karne ka hukm kyon dete.

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Quran Allah Ta'ala ki Saamit (silent / khamosh) Kitaab hai aur main Kitaab e Naatiq (bolti Kitaab) hun."

(Maula Ali (as) Ki Shaan Mein 1000 Ahadees, p65)

📚

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Ali (as) Qur'an ke saath hai aur Qur'an Ali (as) ke saath hai. Wo Hauz e Kausar tak ek doosre se juda nahi honge."

(Sawaaiq Muharriqah, p11)

🤲🏻

*Imam Husain (as) & Duniya:*

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"Aapne Duniya se is tarah Munh moda aur yun be etenai dikhayi jaise Duniya se hamesha ke liye kooch karnewale karte hain, Duniya se khaufzada log ise dekhte hain. Aapki Tamannayen aur Arzuen Duniya se hati hui thi. Aapki Himmat o koshish iski zeenaton se beniyaz thi aur aur Aapne to Duniya ke chehre ki taraf kabhi uchatti hui nigah bhi na dali. Albatta, Akherat mein Aapki dilchaspi Shohra e Afaq (famous) hai......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  ♦️ QUR'AN MEIN TEHREEF? ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1756)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالُوا۟ یَـٰۤأَیُّهَا ٱلَّذِی نُزِّلَ عَلَیۡهِ ٱلذِّكۡرُ إِنَّكَ لَمَجۡنُونࣱ*

 *إِنَّا نَحۡنُ نَزَّلۡنَا ٱلذِّكۡرَ وَإِنَّا لَهُۥ لَحَـٰفِظُونَ.*

"Un logon ne kaha: 'Aye woh Shakhs jis par Zikr (Qur'an) nazil kiya gaya hai, tu Diwana hai."

"Hamne hi Zikr (Qur'an) ko Nazil kiya aur Ham hi iski Hifazat Karnewale hain."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 6 & 9)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Tehreef e Qur'an ke mutalliq Zikr jari hai.

📚📖

Islam ke ibtidai zamane mein Musalman mukhtalif Qara'aton mein padha karte the ya Hifz rakhte the. Ye padhna sirf padhna hi nahi tha balke tashrihi bhi tha, jis mein alfaaz lehje ke mutabiq badalte the.

San 1500 mein poore Middle-east mein Usmani Hukumat thi. Bahut si Qira'aton mein se Hukumat ne 'Asim' se 'Hafs' Qira'at ko raaej kiya. Isliye poore Middle-east mein ye Qira'at raaej ho gayi aur doosri Qira'aten ahista ahista khatm hoti gayi.

Isi tarah Shiyon ke muqaddas Shehron par bhi Usmani Hukumat ka ghalba tha. Kuchh jagah kabhi Safavi to kabhi Usmani Hukumat mein rahi, is tarah Safavi ilaqon mein bhi yehi Qira'at raaej ho gayi.

📚

Allama Majlisi (ar) ke mutabiq hamen yehi maqbool Qur'an ki Tilawat karni hai lekin yehi bhi dhyan rahe ke 'Hafs' ya koi aur Mukhalifin ki Qara'at zaroori nahi ke original Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki Qira'at ho.

Kuchh Ayaat ki taraf nazar karte hain jahan Qira'at ke farq se matalib bhi badal jate hain:

*فَمَا ٱسۡتَمۡتَعۡتُم بِهِۦ مِنۡهُنَّ فَـَٔاتُوهُنَّ أُجُورَهُنَّ فَرِیضَةࣰۚ*(4:24)

Ibne Abbas ki Qara'at, Sunni Book Tafsir Al-Tabari

Habib Ibne Thabit ne kaha:

"Ibne Ibbas ne mujhe jo mushaf diya woh Ubayy ki Qara'at ke hain, us mein aisa likha tha:

فَمَا ٱسۡتَمۡتَعۡتُم بِهِۦ *اِلٰی اَجَلٍ مُسَمّٰی* مِنۡهُنَّ فَـَٔاتُوهُنَّ أُجُورَهُنَّ فَرِیضَةࣰۚ

Ye mutah ki Ayat hai. Is mein ye alfaz nahi hain *اِلٰی اَجَلٍ مُسَمّٰی*

📚

Imam Sadiq (as):

*فما استمتعتم به منهن إلى أجَلٍ مُسَمّٰى فآتوهن أجورهنفريضة " فهذه الآية دليل على المتعة*

"Ek muqarrar muddat ke liye jo kuchh tumne unse hasil kiya hai, phir unhe unki ujrat bataur Farz ada karo.' Ye Ayat Mutah ki Daleel hai

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi)

📚

Isse wazeh hota hai ke kuchh missing hai, lekin majmui maana mein koi tabdeeli nahi aati.

قَالَ تَٱللَّهِ إِن كِدتَّ *لَتُرۡدِینِ.*

Is Ayat (37:56) mein لَتُرۡدِینِ ko Sanaa Mushaf mein is tarah likha hai: لَتُغوِینِ

Thoda sa badal hai lekin mafhoom mein tabdili nahi aati. Jaise yaha 'tum barbad kar dete' ya 'tum dhoka dete.'

(To be Cont'd ......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Qur'an! , Allah ke baad, har shay se Afzal hai. Jisne Qur'an ki izzat ki goya usne Allah ki izzat ki aur jisne Qur'an ki izzat na ki goya usne Allah ki tauheen ki."

(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v9, p27)

🤲🏻

*Imam Husain (as) nargha e Aada mein:*

Imam Mahdi:

"Yahan tak ke wo waqt aa gaya jab Jor o Sitam ne lambe lambe dig bhar kar Sarkashi shuru kar di. Zulm tamam tar Hathyar jama kar ke sakht Jang ke liye amada ho gaya. Aur Baghiyon ne apne tamam saathiyon ko bula bheja. Us waqt Aap apne Jadd ke Haram mein panah gazen, Zalimon se alag thalag, Masjid o Mehrab ke saaye mein Lazzat o Khwahishat se bezaar baithe the. Aap apni taqat aur imkanat ke mutabiq Dilo Zaban ke zariye Buraiyyon se nafrat ka izhar karte aur logon ko Buraiyyon se rokte the. Magar, phir Aapke Ilm ka taqaza hua ke Aap khullam khulla Bai'at se inkar karen aur Fujjar ke khilaf Jihad ke liye uth khade hon......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

  ♦️ QUR'AN MEIN TEHREEF? ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1757)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالُوا۟ یَـٰۤأَیُّهَا ٱلَّذِی نُزِّلَ عَلَیۡهِ ٱلذِّكۡرُ إِنَّكَ لَمَجۡنُونࣱ*

 *إِنَّا نَحۡنُ نَزَّلۡنَا ٱلذِّكۡرَ وَإِنَّا لَهُۥ لَحَـٰفِظُونَ.*

"Un logon ne kaha: 'Aye woh Shakhs jis par Zikr (Qur'an) nazil kiya gaya hai, tu Diwana hai."

"Hamne hi Zikr (Qur'an) ko Nazil kiya aur Ham hi iski Hifazat Karnewale hain."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 6 & 9)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Tehreef e Qur'an ke mutalliq Zikr jari hai.

📚📖

Allama Majlisi kehte hain ke is *نقص و تغيير* (Changes) ye sirf ek mushaheda hai.

Isse ye sabit nahi hota ke ham Qur'an ka inkaar karte hain. Jabke sabhi Ahkam ham Qur'an se hi istefada karte hain.

📚

Ek Ayat ki misal aur hai: (4:64)

*وَلَوۡ أَنَّهُمۡ إِذ ظَّلَمُوۤا۟ أَنفُسَهُمۡ جَاۤءُوكَ فَٱسۡتَغۡفَرُوا۟ ٱللَّهَ...*

Riwayat mein is tarah hai:

عن أبي جعفر عليه السلام قال: "ولو أنهم إذ ظلموا أنفسهم جاءوك " *يا علي*" فاستغفروا الله واستغفر لهم الرسول لوجدوا الله توابارحيما " هكذا نزلت.  

Yani is mein 'Ya Ali' hai.

(Bihar, Vol-94, P-36, H-1467)

📚

Ek aur Ayat

*سَلَـٰمٌ عَلَىٰۤ إِلۡ یَاسِینَ.*

[As-Saaffat 130]

Riwayat mein ye is tarah hai:

*سَلَـٰمٌ عَلَىٰۤ آلِۡ یَاسِینَ.*

'Yasin' Rasoole Khuda (saww) ka Laqab hai.

*قَالَ هَـٰذَا صِرَ ٰ⁠طٌ عَلَیَّ مُسۡتَقِیمٌ*

[Al-Hijr: 41]

Isko is tarah bhi padha ja sakta hai:

*قَالَ هَـٰذَا صِرَ ٰ⁠طُ عَلِیٍّ مُسۡتَقِیمٌ*

(Haza Sirato Aliyyin Mustaqeem)

Kiyonki Eraab baad mein lagaye gaye hain.

📚

Allama Majlisi Qur'an mein Tehreef moqif nahi rakhte.

Ab Riwayaat mein mein aisa hai aur Ulama uske qael nahi hain, isko mandarja zel mein samjhen:

📚

Qur'an e Majeed ki do tarah ki Tafseer hain.

(1) Zahiri (2) Batini

Batini Tafseer Ayat ke siyaq o sibaaq o andaz ke mutabiq ki jati hai.

Riwayat of Imam Reza (as): *إنا نحن نزلنا عليك القرآن تنزيلا "؟ قال: بولاية علي عليه السلام تنزيلا، قلت: هذا تنزيل؟ قال: نعم ذا تأويل، قلت: " إن هذه تذكرة"؟ قال: الولاية، قلت: " يدخل من يشاء في رحمته*

Meine Ayat padhi:

"Beshak, ye Ham hi hain Jisne tum par Qur'an ko tadreejan nazil kiya",

Imam (as) ne farmaya:

"Beshak, Ham hi ne Wilayat e Ali ko Tadreejan nazil kiya."

Imam (as) se jab poochha ke kya is tarah Ayat nazil hui.

Imam ne farmaya: "Ye Tawil hai."

(Al Kaafi, Vol-1, P-435)

Yani ye iski Batini Tafseer hai.

📚

Akhir mein ye bhi Riwayat hai:

*عن أبي جعفر عليه السلام أنه قال: ما يستطيع أحد أن يدعي أن عنده جميع القرآن كله ظاهره وباطنه غيرالأوصياء.*

"Koi bhi ye dawa nahi kar sakta ke unke paas tamam Qur'an hai. Iska Zahiri o Batini Tafseer Ausiya (Imam as) ke alawa kisi paas nahi hai."

(Al Kaafi, Vol-1, P-228)

 (The End of Topic......)

                 *7th Safar 1443*

 *15th September 2021, Wednesday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦️ 'SHIA' IN QUR'AN♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1758)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَقَدۡ أَرۡسَلۡنَا مِن قَبۡلِكَ فِی شِیَعِ ٱلۡأَوَّلِینَ.*

"Hamne Aapse pehle sabqa Aqwaam (Shias) mein Rasool bheje."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 10)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Shia doosra bada firqe ke taur par mashhoor hai, aye dekhte hain Qur'an mein ye kis maana mein hai:

📚📖

Iska lafzi Tarjuma aise hoga ke Allah Ta'ala ne tumse pehle bhi guzishta Firqon mein bhi Rasool bheje.

Lafz ' *شیع* ' jama (Plural) hai *شیعہ* ka.

"Lafz *شیع* ka Root hai *شیاع* hai yani 'Taqwiyyat'. *شاع الخبر* us waqt kaha jata hai jab Khabar mutaddid aur qawi ho jaye. *شاع القوم*  us waqt kaha jata hai jab Jamiat phail jaye aur zyada tadaad mein ho. *شیعہ* (Shia) un logon ko kehte hain ke Insaan jinki wajah se qawi ho."

(Mufradat e Raghib)

📚

Majmaul Bayan mein iska Root ' *مشایعت* ' yani *متابعت* bataya gaya hai. Yani Shia ke maana Pairokar, Taabe, follower ke hain.

Rehlat Rasool (saww) ke baad do giroh mein tasaad raha. Ye do giroh Hukumat e Moaviya ke zamane mein Shia'ane Moaviya aur Shia'ane Ali (as) ke naam se maroof hue. Moaviya ke naam se Musalman itna mutanaffir hua ke usne apne giroh ka naam Ahle Sunnat kehelwana pasand kiya. Jabke doosra giroh sirf 'Shia' se wohi Shia'ane Ali (as) murad liya jaane laga.

Aur Shia'ane Ali (as) (شیعان علی) unhe kaha jata hai jo Hazrat Ali (as) ke Pairokar hon, unki Imamat par Eteqaad rakhte hon.

Paighambar e Islam ki maroof Hadis jo Umme Salma (as) se riwayat hai:

*شِیعَةُ عَلِیٍّ ھُمُ الفَائّزُونَ یَومُ القَیَامَة*

"Qayamat e Din Najaat paane wale Ali (as) Pairokar hain."

Ye Hadis se yehi maana ki dalalat karti hai.

Is tarah تشیع ka talluq ek matabe fikr Jamat se hota hai.

Qur'an mein do tarah ke 'Shia' ka zikr kiya gaya hai. Ek achha giroh aur ek bura giroh.

Example:

*ثُمَّ لَنَنزِعَنَّ مِن كُلِّ شِیعَةٍ أَیُّهُمۡ أَشَدُّ عَلَى ٱلرَّحۡمَـٰنِ عِتِیࣰّا.*

_"Ham phir har Giroh se unhe alag nikal kar khada karenge jo Allah Rehman se bahut akde akde phirte the."_ (Maryam: 69)

وَدَخَلَ ٱلۡمَدِینَةَ عَلَىٰ حِینِ غَفۡلَةࣲ مِّنۡ أَهۡلِهَا فَوَجَدَ فِیهَا رَجُلَیۡنِ یَقۡتَتِلَانِ هَـٰذَا مِن *شِیعَتِهِۦ* وَهَـٰذَا مِنۡ عَدُوِّهِۦۖ فَٱسۡتَغَـٰثَهُ ٱلَّذِی مِن *شِیعَتِهِۦ* عَلَى ٱلَّذِی مِنۡ عَدُوِّهِۦ فَوَكَزَهُۥ مُوسَىٰ فَقَضَىٰ عَلَیۡهِۖ قَالَ هَـٰذَا مِنۡ عَمَلِ ٱلشَّیۡطَـٰنِۖ إِنَّهُۥ عَدُوࣱّ مُّضِلࣱّ مُّبِینࣱ. 

"Ek roz woh (Hazrat Musa as) Shaher mein aise waqt mein dakhil hua jabke Ahle Shaher ghaflat mrin the. Wahan usne dekha ke do Admi lad rahe hain. *Ek uski apni Qaum ka tha.* aur doosra uski Dushman Qaum se talluq rakhta tha. Uski Qaum ke ne Dushman Qaum wale ke khilaf use madad ke liye pukara. Musa (as) ne usko ek ghoosa mara aur uska kam tamam kar diya......."  (Surah Al-Qasas 15)

إِنَّ ٱلَّذِینَ فَرَّقُوا۟ دِینَهُمۡ وَكَانُوا۟ *شِیَعࣰا* لَّسۡتَ مِنۡهُمۡ فِی شَیۡءٍۚ إِنَّمَاۤ أَمۡرُهُمۡ إِلَى ٱللَّهِ ثُمَّ یُنَبِّئُهُم بِمَا كَانُوا۟ یَفۡعَلُونَ. (Al-An'am: 159)

Mundarja bala Ayaat Giroh ke maana mein hai.

Achhe maane mein ye hain:

*وَإِنَّ مِن شِیعَتِهِۦ لَإِبۡرَ ٰ⁠هِیمَ.*

"Beshak Ibrahim (as) Shia mein se the." (Surah As-Saaffat 83)

📚

Burai phalana ke maana mein:

إِنَّ ٱلَّذِینَ یُحِبُّونَ أَن *تَشِیعَ* ٱلۡفَـٰحِشَةُ فِی ٱلَّذِینَ ءَامَنُوا۟ لَهُمۡ عَذَابٌ أَلِیمࣱ فِی ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِۚ وَٱللَّهُ یَعۡلَمُ وَأَنتُمۡ لَا تَعۡلَمُونَ. (Surah An-Nur 19)

📚

Yahan hamara maqsad sirf Qur'an mein lafz 'Shia' pesh karna tha.

Shia hone ki alag Fazilat hain woh ham kisi mauqe par pesh karenge.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Qayamat ke din Ali (as) ko 7 naamo'n se pukara jayega. Unse kaha jayega: Aye Siddiq, Aye Rehnuma, Aye Aabid, Aye Haadi, Aye Mahdi, Aye Jawaa'n Mard, Aye Ali (as) tum aur tumhare Shia bagair kisi hisaab ke Jannat mein chale jao."

(Maula Ali (as) Ki Shaan Mein 1000 Ahadees, p31)

🕌🚩

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Agar koi But-Parast (idol-worshipper) bhi marte waqt mazhabe Shia ka eteqaad aur Aimma e Masumeen (as) ki Imamat ka waqai iqraar kar lega to Aatish e Jahannum uske kisi jism ke hisse ko na chhuegi."

(Tehzeeb ul Islam, p318)

🕌🚩

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jo shakhs apni Zabaan se kahe ke main Shia hun, lekin wo Maidan e Amal mein hamari mukhaalifat karta ho, to wo shakhs hamara Shia nahi hai. Hamare Shia woh hain jo Dil o Jaan se hamare muwaafiq hain aur hamare Aasaar o Aamaal ko apne liye Namoona (ideal) qaraar dete hue hamari pairavi karte hain."

(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v65, p164; Wasaail ush Shia, v15, p247, Sharh Chahal Hadees Imam Mahdi (atfs), p50)

🤲🏻

Imam Husain (as) aur Itmaame Hujjjat:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Lekin log Zulm o Sitam ke saath Aapke muqabile par dat gaye. Aise aade waqt par bhi, Aapne pehle to unko Khuda ke Ghazab se daraya aur un par Hujjat tamam ki phir unse Jihad kiya. Tab, unhone Aapse kiya hua Ahd toda nez Aapki Bai'at se nikal kar Aapke Rab aur Aapke Jadd e Amjad ko naraaz kiya aur Aapke saath Jang shuru kar di."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

                 *8th Safar 1443*

  *16th September 2021, Thursday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

            ♦️ HATDHARMI♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1759)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا یَأۡتِیهِم مِّن رَّسُولٍ إِلَّا كَانُوا۟ بِهِۦ یَسۡتَهۡزِءُونَ * كَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ نَسۡلُكُهُۥ فِی قُلُوبِ ٱلۡمُجۡرِمِینَ * لَا یُؤۡمِنُونَ بِهِۦ وَقَدۡ خَلَتۡ سُنَّةُ ٱلۡأَوَّلِینَ * وَلَوۡ فَتَحۡنَا عَلَیۡهِم بَابࣰا مِّنَ ٱلسَّمَاۤءِ فَظَلُّوا۟ فِیهِ یَعۡرُجُونَ * لَقَالُوۤا۟ إِنَّمَا سُكِّرَتۡ أَبۡصَـٰرُنَا بَلۡ نَحۡنُ قَوۡمࣱ مَّسۡحُورُونَ.*

"Unke paas jab bhi koi Rasool aaya to logon ne uska Mazaq udaya. Mujremin ke Dilon mein to ham is Zikr ko isi tarah guzarte hain. Woh us par Imaan nahi laya karte, Qadeem se in logon ki yahi ravish chali aayi hai. Agar ham in par Aasmaan ka Darwaza khol dete aur woh Din dahade us mein chadhne bhi lagte to bhi woh ye kehte ke hamari Nazar Bandi kar di gayi hai, balke ham par Jadoo kar diya gaya hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 11 - 15)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Jaisa ke guzishta Ayaat ke zel mein bhi bayan kar chuke hain, ye Ayaat Kuffar ki Hatdharmi ki taraf nashandahi kar rahi hain. Us waqt ke Kuffar o Munkarin aur aaj ke bhi Munkarin e Wilayat Anbiya wa Aimma ka mazaq udate the aur udate hain. Aise logon ke Dil sakht ho jate hain aur koi Aqalmandi wa achhi baaten in ke Dil mein sarahiyyat nahi karti. Ye aisa bhakt hote hain ke agar ham unke saamne apna Dil bhi cheer kar rakh den to inka Dil nahi pighlega. Rasool ke Mo'jezaat ka Mazaaq udate hain, usko Jadoo ka naam de dete hain. Logon ki ye rawish aaj bhi payi jati hai, jaise apsi Dushmani mein ek doosre ko ilzam lagate hain ke usne kuchh Jadoo kar diya, Nazar band kar di waghaira phir woh Babaon ke Darwaza khatkhatate hain. Kyonke ye bhool jate hain ka unka bhi koi Sarbarah, Mushkil Kusha hai. Ye Ahlebait (as) ki Wilayat ke Dar ko chhodte hain aur dar dar bhatakte hain.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Agar main Momin ki Naak bhi Talwaar se kaat du'n ke mujhse Adaawat kare to nahi karega aur agar Munafiq par saari Duniya undel du'n ke mujhse Mohabbat kar le to nahi karega, isliye ke ye faisla Rasule Akram (saww) ki Zabaan se ho chuka hai ke Aye Ali (as), Momin tumse Dushmani nahi kar sakta aur Munafiq tumse Mohabbat nahi kar sakta."

(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p190)

🤲🏻

Ma'arka-e-Karbala:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Lehaza Aap (as) bhi Maidan e Karzar mein utar aaye, Aapne Fujjar ke Laskaron ko rond dala aur Zulfiqar sont kar Jang ke gehre gubar ke Badalon mein ghus kar ghamasan ka Ran dala ke logon ko Ali (as) ki Jang yaad aa gayi. Dushmano ne Aapki Sabit Qadami, Dileri aur bebaki dekhi to unka Pitta Paani ho gaya aur unhone muqabile ke bajaye Makkari se kaam liya aur Aapke Qatl ke liye Fareb ke Jaal bichha diye. Aur Maloon Umar Saad ne Lashkar ko hukm diya ke woh Aap par Paani band kar de Aap tak Paani pahunchne ke tamam raaston ki naka bandi kar de. Phir Dushman ne tez Jang shuru kar di aur Aap par pai dar pai hamle karne laga. Jiske natije mein us ne Aapko Teeron aur Nezon se chhalni kar diya, aur intihai darindgi ke saath Aapko loot liya......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                 *9th Safar 1443*

    *17th September 2021, Friday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦️ ZODIAC - BURUJ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1760)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَقَدۡ جَعَلۡنَا فِی ٱلسَّمَاۤءِ بُرُوجࣰا وَزَیَّنَّـٰهَا لِلنَّـٰظِرِینَ.*

"Hamne Aasmaan mein Burj (Mansions, Minaar) banaye hain aur unko dekhne walon ke liye (Sitaron se) muzayyan kiya."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 16)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Tafseer e Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi ke mutabiq Burj se Shams o Qamar ke manazil (path) murad hain. Aur Allah ne Aasmaan ko Sitaron se muzayyan kiya hai.

♐⚖️👬🦁🦂🐍🦀🐟🐂🐏🐐🏹🏺

Khuda ne Aasmaan ko Roshan Sitaron se muzayyan kiya aur wo 12 Buruj ( بروج ) ( Zodiac ) mein hain. Muntaqatul Buruj) *منطقة البرج ) par kai Sitaron ka jhurmut hain jinhe qaide se milaya jaye to 12 mukhtalif shaklen ban jati hain aur unhi shaklon ke lehaz se unke naam rakh liye gaye hain. Hindi mein unhi 'Raashi' (राशि) aur Arabic mein Buruj (برج) kaha jata hai. Unke Naam English, Hindi, Arabic respectively mein is tarah hain:

(1) Aries, Mesh, Hamal

(2) Tauras, Vrish, Thaur

(3) Gemini, Mithun, Jauza

(4) Cancer, Kark, Sartan

(5) Leo, Sinh, Asad

(6) Virgo, Kanya, Sanbla

(7) Libra, Tula, Mizaan

(8) Scorpio, Vrishchik, Aqrab

(9) Sagittarius Dhanu, Qaus

(10) Capricornus, Makar, Jadi

(11) Aquarius, Kumbh, Dilo

(12) Pisces, Meen, Hoot

(Majmaul Bayan)

Ilme Nujoom mein Kuchh Nujumi isse Nafse Falaki se relate karte hain. Kuchh Nujumi iske Ilm se Ruhani Amraaz ko hal karte, jabke kuchh Bhavishya Future Predictions karte hain.

Aimma ki Riwayaat ke mutabiq in par bharosa nahi karna chahiye, ye Aqeede ke khilaf hai.

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Woh jo kisi Jaadugar, Ojha, Kaazib ke paas jaata hai aur uske kahe ko sach qaraar deta hai, woh Allah ki sab Kitaabo'n ki nazar mein Kaafir ho gaya."

(Greater Sins 2, Sorcery)

Imam Ali (as):

"Najumi (astrologer) Kaahin jaisa hai, Kaahin (jyotishi) Jaadugar ki tarah hai, Jaadugar Kaafir ki maanind hai aur Kaafir Jahannumi hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah (Intekhaab o Takhlees), v3, p100)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  *18th September 2021, Saturday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦️ 👂🏻 SUN GUN LENA ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1761)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَحَفِظۡنَـٰهَا مِن كُلِّ شَیۡطَـٰنࣲ رَّجِیمٍ * إِلَّا مَنِ ٱسۡتَرَقَ ٱلسَّمۡعَ فَأَتۡبَعَهُۥ شِهَابࣱ مُّبِینࣱ.*

"Aur Hamne har Shaitan Rajeem se mehfooz kar diya hai. Haan magar jo koi chori chhipe sunne ki koshish kare hai to ek roshan dahekta hua Shola uska peechha karta hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 17 - 18)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Chori chhipke jab Shaitan Falak ke Razon ko sunna chahta hai (Kaan lagata hai) to Shahab ke zariye use haanka jata hai.

Is Ayat ke zel Mufassirin ki alag alag Tafseeren hain.

Tafseer fiz Zalal ne isse sarfe nazar kiya ke ye aise Haqaiq hain jiska Idraak mumkin nahi.

Kuchh ka kehna hai ye wohi Meteors ke tukde hain jo Zameen ki had mein aate hain aur jal kar raakh ho jaate hain.

Kuchh Mufassirin ne Ayaat o Riwayaat ke zariye ye farmaya hai ke Aflaak Zameen par Muheet hai. Aur in mein Farishton ke kai giroh hain aur in Aflaak ke kai Darwaze hain jin mein sirf Farishte hi aa ja sakte hain. Un mein se kuchh Farishte haath mein Shahab liye hote hain aur in Shaitano k peechha karte hain jo chore chhipe sunte hain.

Scientists ke mutabiq doosri Duniya mein kucch Zindagiyan (Aleins) hain jo ham se zyada civilized hain aur hamari khabare janne ke liye kuchh Radioactive Rays yahan phekte rehte hain. In rays ko ye Shaitan jinko kuchh log Dev ya Pari kehte hain catch karte hain aur secrets ko paas on karte hain.

Ye alag alag nazaryat the, haqiqat kya hai wallaho Alam

(To be Cont'd....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as) ne Abdus Salam se farmaya:

"Aye Abdus Salam! Logon se hoshiyaar raho aur apne Nafs se bhi hoshiyaar raho."

Arz kiya: 'Maula! Mein logon se to hoshiyaar reh sakta hun bhala apne Nafs se kaise hoshiyaar rahun?'

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Baaz auqaat chori chhipe sunne wala Khabees tumhare paas aata hai aur tumhare Nafs ke Khayalat sun gun leta hai. Phir woh Insaani surat ikhtiyar kar ke logon ko tumhare iraadon se qabl az waqt Khabardar karta hai."

Arz kiya: Maula! Isse bachna to mere bas mein nahi hai!'

Imam (as): "Baat yehi hai."

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Ma'arka-e-Karbala:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Usne na to Aapke silsile mein kisi Ahd o Paiman ki parwa ki aur na hi Aapke Doston ke Qatl, nez Aap aur Aapke Ahle Bait (as) ka samaan ghaarat ke silsile mein kisi Gunah ki fikr ki. Aur Aapne Maidan e Jang mein sabse aage badh kar Masaeb o Mushkelat ko yun jhela ke Aasman ke Farishte bhi Aapki Sabr o Isteqamat par dang reh gaye. Phir Dushman har taraf se Aap (as) par toot pada, usne Aapko Zakhmo se chur chur karke nidhal kar diya aur dam lene tak ki fursat na di, yahan tak ke Aapka koi Nasir o Madadgar baqi na raha aur Aap (as) intehai Sabr o Shakebai se sab kuchh dekhte aur jhelte hue yako tanha Apni Mukhaddarao Asmat o Taharat aur Bachchon ko Dushman ke hamlon se bachane mein masroof rahe......."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

☘️ SHABE WILADAT-E-SADEQAIN (as) ☘️

        16th Rabiul Awwal 1443

    23rd October 2021, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

   ♦️ MILAD-UN-NABI (saww)♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1792)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَحَفِظۡنَـٰهَا مِن كُلِّ شَیۡطَـٰنࣲ رَّجِیمٍ * إِلَّا مَنِ ٱسۡتَرَقَ ٱلسَّمۡعَ فَأَتۡبَعَهُۥ شِهَابࣱ مُّبِینࣱ.

"Aur Hamne har Shaitan Rajeem se mehfooz kar diya hai. Haan magar jo koi chori chhipe sunne ki koshish kare hai to ek roshan dahekta hua Shola uska peechha karta hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 17 - 18)

EVENT TONIGHT ....!!!!!!!

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

(Cont'd after 18th Sep)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Iblees La'een pehle to Saatve Aasmaan tak jaata tha. Hazrat Esa (as) ki Wiladat ke baad use 3 Aasmaano se rok diya gaya. Phir woh 4 Aasmaano tak jaata tha. Jab Rasulallah (saww) ki Wiladat ba Sa'adat hui to use tamam Aasmaano se rok diya gaya. Aur Sitaron ke zariye se Shayateen ko Rajm (stoning) kiya jaane laga."

"Quraish ne ye ghair mamooli tabdeeli dekhi to woh kehne lage: 'Maloom hota hai wo ghadi aa gayi hai jiska Tazkara ham Ahle Kitaab se suna karte the."

"Amr bin Umayya us daur ka mashhoor Kaahin (Priest) tha, usne kaha:' Tum in Sitaron ko dekho, jinko dekh kar Raat ke waqt Simton ka taayyun kiya jata hai. Aur jinke zariye Mausam e Sarma o Garma ki pehchan hoti hai! Agar in Sitaron se Shayateen ko Rajm kiya ja raha hai to phir iska maqsad ye hai ke Kaynaat ka khaatma hone ko hai aur agar inke bajaye doosre Sitaron se Rajm ho raha hai to phir koi azeem waqea runuma hua hai."

"Jis Fajr ko Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki Wiladat hui to tamam Sanam Kadon (Temples) ke But (Idol) aundhe Munh gir pade. Kasra ka Aiwaan laraz utha iske Chauda Kangure gir gaye. Baheera saada khushk ho gaya aur Faaras ke Aatish Kadah (Fire Temple) bujh gaya, jabke isse qabl woh ek hazaar Baras tak musalsal jalta rehta tha."

"Us Raat Aatish Kadah ke Prohit ne Khwab dekha ke bahut se sarkash Oont hain jo Arabi Ghodon ko apne saamne liye hue hain. Unhone Dajla ko kaat diya aur unke Mulk mein dakhil ho gaye. Iraani Kisra (King) ka Mahel darmiyan se toot gaya aur wo Darya e Dajla mein doob gaya hai."

"Aapki Wiladat ba Sa'adat ke waqt Hikaz se tez Roshni namudar hui jo tamam Bilaad e Mishriq tak pahunchi. Duniya ke har Badshah ka Takht ulat gaya aur Wiladat ke Din tamam Badshahon ki Quwwat e Goyayi jawab de gayi aur Kahino (Astrologers) ka Ilm Baatil ho gaya aur Jadugaron ke Jadu be asar ho gaye. Har Kahina (Astrology) apne Moakkil o Jinn se mehroom ho gayi. Quraish ko Arab mein izzat mili aur unhe 'Aale Allah' kaha jaane laga. Unhe 'Aale Allah' ka Laqab isliye diya gaya ke woh Allah ke Haram mein rihaish pazeer the."

"Hazrat Amina (sa) ke bayan hai ke jab mera Farzand mere Shikam se baramad hua to usne apne dono Haath Zameen par rakhe phir Sar utha kar Aasmaan ki jaanib dekha. Uske baad mere Jism se aisa Noor baramad hua jisse har cheez chamak uthi. Us Roshni mein kisi kehne wale ko meine ye kehte hue suna: 'Aye Aamna! Tu ne tamam Insaano ke Sardar ko Janam diya hai uska Naam Muhammad (saww) rakh aur ise Abdul Muttalib ke paas le ja, taake woh apne Pote ka Didaar karen."

"Hazrat Amina (sa) apne Farzand ko le kar Abdul Muttalib ke paas aayin. Unhone nau Maulood ko gaud mein liya aut unhone ye Asha'ar kahe:

الحمد لله الذي اعطاني

هذا الغلام الطيب الاردان

قد ساده فى المهد على الغلمان

"Saari Hamd Allah ke liye Makhsoos hai, Jisne mujhe Tayyabo Tahir Farzand ata kiya jo Mehed (Jhoole) mein reh kar tamam Bachchon ka Sardar hai."

"Phir Abdul Muttalib ne unhe Arkaan e Ka'aba ki Panah mein diya aur uske mutalliq unhone kuchh Asha'ar padhe.

Iblees La'een ne ek zordar cheekh maari. Uski cheekh ki awaaz sun kar uske tamam chele uske paas jama ho gaye aur unhone kaha: 'Aye hamare aaqa! Aap itne pareshan kyon hain?

Iblees La'een ne unse kaha:'

'Tum Halaak ho jao! Aaj Raat se Aasmaan aur Zameen ka Rang badal gaya hai. Hazrat Esa (as) ke uthaye jaane ke baad se le kar aaj tak itna bada waqea kahin runuma nahi hua. Jao chakkar laga kar maloom karo ke kaisa waqea zahoor pazeer hua hai? Shaitani chele har tarag gaye lekin unhe kahin bhi anhoni baat dikhayi na di. Unhone wapas aa kar Iblees se kaha ke 'hame to kuchh bhi dikhayi nahi diya.'

Iblees ne kaha: 'Tumhara kaam nahi hai, ab main khud hi ise talaash karunga.' Phir usne poosri ruye Zameen ka chakkar lagaya. Jab woh Haram aaya to usne dekha ke Haram par Farishton ka pehra laga hai. Usne andar hone ka uraada kiya to Malaika ne use sakhti se rok diya. Usne Chidya ki shakl ikhtiyar ki aur Hira ki taraf se dakhil hua. Jibrael Amin (as) ne usse kaha ke 'tujh par Khuda ki La'anat ho, kya karne aaya hai?'

Usne kaha: 'Jibrael! Mujhe batao ke, aaj Raat kya waqea runuma hua hai?'

Hazrat Jibrael (as) ne kaha: "Muhammad Mustufa (saww) paida hue hain."

Iblees ne kaha: 'Kya is mein mera bhi kuchh hissa hai?'

Jibrael (as) ne kaha:

'Nahi, tera in mein koi hissa nahi hai.'

Iblees ne kaha: 'To kya unki Ummat mein mera koi hissa hai?'

Jibrael (as) ne kaha : 'Nahi.

Jab usne ye suna to woh khush ho gaya.

(Amaali e Sadooq, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

(Dua Yaume Wiladat Rasoole Khuda (saww) - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦️ RIZQ KA EHTEMAM ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1762)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَٱلۡأَرۡضَ مَدَدۡنَـٰهَا وَأَلۡقَیۡنَا فِیهَا رَوَ ٰ⁠سِیَ وَأَنۢبَتۡنَا فِیهَا مِن كُلِّ شَیۡءࣲ مَّوۡزُونࣲ * وَجَعَلۡنَا لَكُمۡ فِیهَا مَعَـٰیِشَ وَمَن لَّسۡتُمۡ لَهُۥ بِرَ ٰ⁠زِقِینَ * وَإِن مِّن شَیۡءٍ إِلَّا عِندَنَا خَزَاۤىِٕنُهُۥ وَمَا نُنَزِّلُهُۥۤ إِلَّا بِقَدَرࣲ مَّعۡلُومࣲ.*

"Aur Hamne Zameen ko phailaya, Hamne is mein mazboot Pahad banaye aur Hamne is mein har tarah ki Nabatat (Vegetation) ki napi tuli miqdar mein ugayi aur Hamne Zameen mein tumhare liye Maeeshat (Economical) ke asbaab faraham kiye hain aur in Makhlooqat ke liye bhi jinke Raaziq tum nahi ho."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 19 - 21)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🍛🍪

Allah ne har Jaandar ke liye uski Tabiyat (Nature) ke mutabiq Rizq faraham kiya hai.

🏔️⛰️⛰️

Imam Baqir (as):

"Allah Ta'ala ne Pahadon mein Sona, Chaandi, Jawaherat, Tanba (Copper), Seesa (Lead), Loha aur Surma rakh diya hai. Algharz Pahadon mein Khuda ne aisi qeemti ashya rakhi hain jo wazan ke mutabiq forokht (sell) hiti hain. (15:21)"

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

🌦️🌧️⛈️

Har cheez ka Khazana Baarish ka Paani hai. Jab Baarish barasti hai to har Jaandar ki khuraq aur Ghaza paida hoti hai.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

☁️

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Tamam Barri o Behri (land & Sea) Makhlooqat ki Arsh mein Shabeeh maujood hai aur ye is Ayat (15:21) ki Taveel hai."

(Rauzatul Waezeen Shaikh Mufeed, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Baqir (as):

"Har Jaandaar (living creature) ke liye Allah ne kuchh na kuchh Rizq e Halaal muqarrar kiya hai jo use khair o aafiyat se (comfortably) mil sakta hai aur uske muqable mein Rizq e Haraam bhi rakha gaya hai. Jab koi shakhs Haraam tariqe se Rizq haasil karta hai to uske muqaddar mein jo Halaal likkha hua hai utna hi Rizq e Halaal usme se kam kar diya jaata hai, jab ke Gunah aur Nafarmani alag se shumaar hoti hai, is liye ke Allah ne insaano'n ko Hukm diya hai "Allah se uska Fazl talab karo."

(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v2, p352)

🤲🏻

Shahadat-e-Imam Husain (as)

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"......Yahan tak ke Dushman ne Aapko Ghode se gira diya Aap (as) Zakhmon se pash pash Jism ke saath Zameen par gir pade. Phir woh Talwaren le kar Aap par pil pada aur usne Ghodon ki sumon ze Aapko pamaal kar diya. Ye wo waqt tha jab Aapki Jabeen e Aqdas par Maut ka Paseena aa gaya aur Rooh nikalne ke sabab Aapka Jisme Nazneen dayen bayen sukadne phailne laga. Ab Aap (as) us mod par the jahan Insaan sab kuchh bhool jata hai. Aise mein Aap (as) ne apne Khayam aur Ghar ki taraf Aakheri bar hasrat bhari nigah dali aur Aapka Asp e Bawafa (Horse - Duldul Zuljana) tezi se hinhinata aur rota hua sunani sunane ke liye Khayam ki taraf rawana ho gaya......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦️ MAUSAM - WEATHER♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1763)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِن مِّن شَیۡءٍ إِلَّا عِندَنَا خَزَاۤىِٕنُهُۥ وَمَا نُنَزِّلُهُۥۤ إِلَّا بِقَدَرࣲ مَّعۡلُومࣲ * وَأَرۡسَلۡنَا ٱلرِّیَـٰحَ لَوَ ٰ⁠قِحَ فَأَنزَلۡنَا مِنَ ٱلسَّمَاۤءِ مَاۤءࣰ فَأَسۡقَیۡنَـٰكُمُوهُ وَمَاۤ أَنتُمۡ لَهُۥ بِخَـٰزِنِینَ.*

"Aur koi cheez aisi nahi hai  jiske Khazane Hamare paas maujood na hon."

"Aur Ham har cheez ke ek muqarrar muqaddar mein nazil karte hain aur Hamne barawar Hawaon (Fertilising Wind) ko bheja, Hamne Aasmaan se Paani naazil kiya, isse Hamne tumhe seraab kiya, tum iske Khazanedar nahi ho."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 21 - 22)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🍃🍃🌬️

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Hawa ko bura bhala na kaho kyonki kuchh Hawain Basharat dene wali hain, kuchh Darane wali hain, aur kuchh Hawain barawar hain. Allah se Hawa ki bhalai talab karo aur uske nuqsaan se panah maago."

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🌬️🌪️🍃

Imam Baqir (as):

"Zill' (Surah Furqaan:45) Tuloo e Fajr aur Tuloo e Shams ke darmiyan hai (between dawn and sunrise). (Ek aur riwayat mein hai ke) sab haalato'n se wo Pakeezatareen hai kyunki Andhera tabiyat mein nafrat ka baais hota hai aur Aa'nkho'n ki binaayi (vision) kam hoti hai lekin Suraj ki shu'a (sunrays) Hawa ko narm aur Pakeeza karti hai aur Aa'nkho'n ki roshni ko zyada karti hai. Is liye Allah Ta'ala ne isse Jannat ki sifat ko bayaan farmaya hai."

(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p105)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇

Riwayat:

Bihaarul Anwaar, v44, p244, Hadees 42 mein bayaan hua hai ke ek martaba Hazrat Sulaiman (as) Bisaat (carpet) par baith kar Hawa mein saer kar rahe the ke Zameen e Karbala ke upar se guzare to Bisaat Hawa mein hichkole khane lagi aur Hazrat Sulaiman (as) ko khatra hua ke woh kahi'n Zameen hi par na gir paden. Thodi der baad aaraam o sukoon paida hua aur Bisaat Zameen e Karbala par utri. Hazrat Sulaiman (as) ne hawa se mukhatib ho kar farmaya:

"Tu ne mujhe kyun yahaa'n utaara hai?"

Hawa ne arz kiya,

"Is jagah Hazrat Imam Husain (as) ko shaheed kiya jayega."

Hazrat Sulaiman (as) ne puchha:

"Ye Imam Husain (as) kaun hain?" 

Hawa ne arz kiya:

"Woh Hazrat Muhammad Mustafa (saww) ke Nawase aur Hazrat Ali (as) ke farzand hain?"

Hazrat Sulaiman (as) ne puchha:

"Unka Qaatil kaun hai?" Hawaa ne arz kiya:

"Uska Naam Yazeed hai aur Zameeno'n aur Aasmaano'n par rehne waale tamaam ki taraf se uspar La'anat hai."

Hazrat Sulaiman (as) ne haath buland kiye aur Yazeed La'een par La'anat ki aur Jinno'n aur Insaano'n ne Aameen kaha. Phir Hawa dobara chali aur unki Bisaat Hawa mein udne lagi.

(Taarikhcha e Azadari e Husaini, p26)

🤲🏻

Karbala mein Mukhadderat e Ismat o Taharat (Bibiyan) ka haal:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"...... Jab Mukhadderat e Ismat o Taharat ne Aapke Duldul ko khaali aur Zeen ko ulta hua dekha ek kohraam mach gaya aur woh Gham ki taab na laate hue Khemon se nikal aayen. Unhone apne Baal Chehron par bikhra liye aur apne Rukhsaron par tamache marte hue apne Buzurgon ko pukar pukar kar Nauha o Girya shuru kar diya, kyonki is sangeen sadme ke baad unko Izzat o Ehteram ki Nigahon se nahi dekha jaa raha tha aur sab ke sab gham se nidhal Aapki Shahadatgah ki taraf ja rahe the......."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  ♦️ MITTI KA BANA INSAAN♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1764)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنَّا لَنَحۡنُ نُحۡیِۦ وَنُمِیتُ وَنَحۡنُ ٱلۡوَ ٰ⁠رِثُونَ * وَلَقَدۡ عَلِمۡنَا ٱلۡمُسۡتَقۡدِمِینَ مِنكُمۡ وَلَقَدۡ عَلِمۡنَا ٱلۡمُسۡتَـٔۡخِرِینَ * وَإِنَّ رَبَّكَ هُوَ یَحۡشُرُهُمۡۚ إِنَّهُۥ حَكِیمٌ عَلِیمࣱ * وَلَقَدۡ خَلَقۡنَا ٱلۡإِنسَـٰنَ مِن صَلۡصَـٰلࣲ مِّنۡ حَمَإࣲ مَّسۡنُونࣲ.*

"Aur Ham hi Zindagi dete hain aur Ham hi Maut dete hain aur Ham hi Waaris hain. Tum mein se jo log pehle guzar chuke hain Ham unhe bhi Jaante hain aur baad mein aane walon ko bhi Ham Jaante hain. Beshak Aapka Rab in sab ko jama karega. Yaqeenan Woh Hikmat wala aur Ilm wala hai. Yaqeenan Hamne Insaan ko sadhi hui Matti ke sookhe gaare se banaya...."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 23 - 26)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

⛰️

Raghib e Mufradat likhte hain ke Lafz ' *صلصال* ' kisi khushk cheez se awaaz baramad hone ko kehte hain. Jaisa ke Qur'an e Hakim mein *مِن صَلۡصَـٰلࣲ كَٱلۡفَخَّارِ.*(Theekri ki tarah khankhanati hui Mitti). Aur  *حماة و حماء* siyah badbudar Mitti ko kaha jata hai.*حَمَإࣲ مَّسۡنُونࣲ*  means aisa gaara jiski rangat badal gayi ho.

🏔️

Insaan e Awwal Hazrat Adam (as) ki Takhleeq (Creation) Mitti se hui jabke Bani Adam ki Takhleeq Madda Manoyyah (Sperm) se hui jaisa ke Farman e Ilahi hai:

"Aur Usne Insaan ki Takhleeq ki ibtida Mitti se ki, phir uski Nasl ko Haqeer Pani ke Wujood ke Johar (Element) se banaya." (Sajdah: 8)

⛰️🏔️

Adam (as) ki Khilqat ka aghaaz Mitti (Turab) se hua, isiliye Allah ne Farmaya:

*......كَمَثَلِ ءَادَمَۖ خَلَقَهُۥ مِن تُرَابࣲ...*

"Khuda ne use "Turab" yani Khushk Mitti se paida kiya."

(Aal-E-Imran: 59)

Phir us mein Paani dala gaya to wo 'Teen - *طین* ' " Geeli Mitti" kehlayi. Isiliye Allah ne Iblees ka qaul naql karte hue Farmaya: *خَلَقَهُ مِن طين* "Tu ne 'Teen' yani Geeli Mitti se banaya hai."

Phir Geeli Mitti padi rahi yahan tak ke uska Rang badal gaya to wo *حَمَإࣲ مَّسۡنُون tabdeel shudah siyah gaara kehlayi. Isiliye Khuda ne Farmaya: مِّنۡ حَمَإࣲ مَّسۡنُون. "Adam (as) ko tabdeel shuda gaare se banane wala hun." phir us gaare ko pada rehne diya gaya, yahan tak ke wo Khushk (dry) ho gaya aur theekri ki si awaazen dene lag gaya to wo صَلۡصَـٰلࣲ kehlaya. Jaisa ke Farmane Ilahi hai. Lehaza Hazrat Adam (as) ki Takhleeq ke mutalliq Qur'an e Majeed mein jo mukhtalif Ayaat dikhayi deti hain un mein koi tazaad (contradictory) nahi hai, balke un mein mukhtalid haalaton ko bayan kiya gaya hai.

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 ⛰️

Imam Ali (as):

"(Insaan apni haqeeqat ko jaane ke) Agar Khuda chahta to Adam (as) ko aise Noor se paida karta jiski Roshni Aa'nkho'n ko chau'ndhiya deti aur uski khushbu Aqlo'n par chha jaati. Magar Khuda ne Adam [as] ko Mitti jaisi maamuli cheez se paida kiya taaki unse Ghuroor o Takabbur aur Khud-pasandi ko door kar de."

(Meezan ul Hikmah (Intekhaab o Takhlees), v3, p195)

🏔️🏔️

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Aye Ali (as)! Main aur aap dono ek Teenat (Mitti) se khalq kiye gaye hain. Aur jo Mitti us Mitti se bach gayi usse hamare Shiyo'n ko khalq kiya gaya hai aur jab Qayamat ka Din hoga to logo'n ko unki Maa ke Naam se pukara jayega siwaye Aapke Shiyo'n ke. Pus unko unke baap ke Naam se pukara jayega, kyunki unki wiladat paak hai."

(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p208)

🧱

Imam Reza (as):

"Tamam qism ki Mitti Haraam hai jaise Murdaar, Khoon aur woh Zibah-shuda Halaal Jaanwar jispar Allah ka Naam na liya gaya ho Haraam hain, siwaaye Hazrat Imam Husain (as) ki Qabr ki Mitti ke. Usko khana Jaayez hai kyunki us mein har Bimaari ke liye Shifa maujood hai."

(Amaali – Shaikh Toosi, v2, p424)

🤲🏻

Shahadat-e-Imam Husain (as)

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"........Afsos! Shimr Maloom Aapke Seene par baitha hua, Aapke Gulu e Mubarak par apni Talwar rakhe hue tha. Woh Kameena Aapki Reshe Aqdas ko pakde hue apni Hindi Talwar se Aapko Zibah kar raha tha! Yahan tak ke, Aapke hosh o hawas sakin ho gaye, Aapki Saans maddham pad gayi aur Aapka Pak o Pakeeza Sar Neze par buland kar diya gaya......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                 ♦️ JINNAT ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1765)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَقَدۡ خَلَقۡنَا ٱلۡإِنسَـٰنَ مِن صَلۡصَـٰلࣲ مِّنۡ حَمَإࣲ مَّسۡنُونࣲ * وَٱلۡجَاۤنَّ خَلَقۡنَـٰهُ مِن قَبۡلُ مِن نَّارِ ٱلسَّمُومِ.*

_"Yaqeenan Hamne Insaan ko sadhi hui Matti ke sookhe gaare se banaya. Isse qabl Ham Jinnaat ko Zehreeli Aag se paida kar chuke hain."_

(Surah Al-Hijr: 26 - 27)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🧞‍♂️😈 Meaning:

Raghib e Mufradat likhte hain ke " *سموم*" us shadeed garam Hawa ko kaha jata hai jo Zeher jaisa asar rakhti ho. Lafz " *جن* - Jinn" means poshida (hidden) cheez ke hain. Is Lafz ke tamam Mushtaqqat mein Posheedgi ka mafhoom paya jata hai. Jaise "Jinn" wo bhi ek poshida Makhlooq hai aur " *ڈھال* - Dhaal" ko Arabic zubaan mein " *ٌجُنَّة* - Junnah" kaha jata hai, kyonki woh bhi apne uthane wale hareef (opposite) se chhupa deti hai. Baagh (Garden) ko *ٌجُنَّة* kaha jata hai kyonki woh Zameen ko chhupa deta hai. Jo Bachcha Rehm e Maadar (Womb) mein ho use " *جنین* - Janeen" kehte hain kyonki wo chhupa hua hota hai aur *جَنَّ عَلَيهِ اللَّيلُ.*  means 'us par Tareeki (darkness) chha gayi yani Raat ki Tareeki chha gayi.

🧞‍♂️😈

"Jinn" ek ba-shu'oor Makhlooq hai jo Tabai taur par (Naturally) hamari Nigahon se ojhal hai. Qur'an e Karim mein is Makhlooq ka zikr kiya gaya aur unki taraf Amaal e Ajeebiya aur tez tareen harkat ko mansoob kiya gaya hai jaisa ke Qissa Hazrat Sulaiman (as) mein bhi iska zikr maujood hai. Qur'an e Karim ki Tilawat se maloom hota hai ke Qaum e Jinn bhi Insaano ki tarah se Shari'at ki Mukallaf (zimmedari) hai. Woh bhi paida hote aur marte rehte hain aur Qayamat ke Din Hisaab ke liye unhe bhi Mehshoor kiya jayega.

🧞‍♂️😈

Raha ye Masa'ala ke " *جان* - Jaan" se mutlaqan Qaum e Jinnat murad hai ya woh bhi Hazrat Adam (as) ki tarah se is No' (type) ka Jadde Aala tha jaisa ke Ibne Abbas se manqool hai. Ya Lafz "Jaann" se Iblees La'een murad hai jaisa ke Hasan se manqool hai ya isse woh Jinn murad hain jinka talluq Nasl e Iblees se hai ya phir isse Jinnat ki ek khaas No' (type) murad hai. Inke mutalliq Mufasserin ne bahut se aqwaal naql kiye hain, jinki aksariyat par koi daleel maujood nahi hai.

(To be Cont'd.....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam e Shafaee (Ahle Sunnat ke Imam)

ne Imam Ali (as) ki shaan mein Ash'aar kahe:

“Ali (as) ki Mohabbat Jahannum se bachne ke liye Dhaal hai, Ali (as) Jannat aur Jahannum ke Taqseem karne wale hain, Hazrat Mustafa (saww) ke barhaq Wasi aur Jinn o Ins ke Imam hain.”

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p125)

🤲🏻

Aseeran-e-Karbala:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Aapke Ahl o Ayaal ko Ghulamo aur Kaneezon ki tarah Qaid kar liya gaya aur unko Ahna e (Iron) Zanjeeron mein jakad kar is tarah be Kajawa Oonton par sawaar kar diya gaya ke Din ki pe panah Garmi unke Chehro ko jhulsaye de rahi thi. Beghairat Dushman unko Jangalon aur Bayabano mein le ja raha tha aur unke nazuk haathon ko Gardano ke peechhe, sakhti se bandh kar Galiyon aur Bazaaron mein unki numayish kar raha tha......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                 ♦️ JINNAT♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1766)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَقَدۡ خَلَقۡنَا ٱلۡإِنسَـٰنَ مِن صَلۡصَـٰلࣲ مِّنۡ حَمَإࣲ مَّسۡنُونࣲ * وَٱلۡجَاۤنَّ خَلَقۡنَـٰهُ مِن قَبۡلُ مِن نَّارِ ٱلسَّمُومِ.*

"Yaqeenan Hamne Insaan ko sadhi hui Matti ke sookhe gaare se banaya. Isse qabl Ham Jinnaat ko Zehreeli Aag se paida kar chuke hain."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 26 - 27)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🧞‍♂️😈

Qur'an e karim ki Ayaat par ghaur karne se ye haqeeqat saamne aati hai ke Allah Insaan aur "Jaan" Naami do Anwa' (types) ko paida kiya hai aur Khuda ne apni Takhleeq ke isbaat mein dono Anwa' ka tazkara kiya hai jaisa ke Farman e Qudrat hai:

*وَخَلَقَ ٱلۡجَاۤنَّ مِن مَّارِجࣲ مِّن نَّارࣲ* (55:15)

"Usne Insaan ko Theekre ki tarah khankhanati Mitti se banaya aur Jinnat ko Aag ke Shole se paida kiya."

🧞‍♂️😈

Ayaat e Qur'ani se maloom hota hai ke Jinnat ki Paidaish Iblees se pehle ho chuki thi aur Iblees us Qaum ka Kafir e Awwal nahi tha jaisa ke Allah Ta'ala ne Farmaya:

*كَانَ مِنَ ٱلۡجِنِّ فَفَسَقَ عَنۡ أَمۡرِ رَبِّهِۦۤۗ*

"Iblees ka talluq Qaum Jinn se tha us ne apne Rab ke Hukm ki Nafarmani ki."

(Al-Kahf: 50)

🧞‍♂️😈

In Ayaat mein Allah Ta'ala ne Insaan ke Moris e Aala aur Qaum e Jinnat ke Jadde Aala Takhleeq ko bayan karte hue Farmaya ke Insaan ke Moris e Aala Hazrat Adam (as) the aur unki Takhleeq Mitti se hui thi. Unki Nasl ka silsila Zaujain ke milaap se qaem hua jabke Qaum e Jinnat ke Moris e Aala ki Paidaish Aag se hui.

🧞‍♂️😈

Qur'an e Majeed ye bhi wazeh karta hai ke is ghair marai (unseen) Qaum mein bhi Nasl ka silsila jaari hai aur kiya unki Nasl bhi doosre Jandaron ki tarah se Zaujain ke milaap se paida hoti hai ya nahi? Is silsile mein Qur'an e Majeed ke zahiri Alfaaz mein koi ishara maujood nahi hai.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as)

se ek shakhs ne kaha, "Mere ghar waalo'n ko Jinnaat tang karte hain". Imam (as) ne farmaya: "Tumhare Makaan ki chhat kitni unchaayi par hai (height of the ceiling)?" Usne arz kiya, "Mere Makaan ki chhat 10 haath buland hai." Imam (as) ne farmaya, "Tum 8 haath naap-kar baaqi 2 haatho'n par Ayatul Kursi likho. Yaad rakho ke jis makaan ki chhat 8 haath se buland hogi wahaa'n Jinnaat ka deraah (padaav) hoga."

(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v1, p501; Tehzeeb ul Islam, p471)

🤲🏻

Imam Husain (as) ki Shahadat ke baad ke asaraat (after-effect)

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....La'anat ho us Fasiq giroh par! Jisne Aapko Qatl karke Islam ko Qatl aur Namaz o Roze ko mo'attal kar diya. Ahkam o Sunan o Ilahi ki Nafarmani ki. Imaan ki Buniyadon ko hila diya. Ayaat e Qur'ani mein tehreef ki aur Baghawat o Dushmani ke daldal mein dhansta hi chala gaya. Aapki Shahadat par Allah ka Rasool (saww) sarapa dard ban gaya. Kitab e Khuda ka koi poochhne wala na raha. Aap (as) par Jafa karne walon ka Haq se Rishta toot gaya. Aapke uth jaane se Takbeer o Tehleel, Haram o Halal nez Tanzeel o Taveel par Parde pad gaye......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                 ♦️ JINNAT ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1767)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَقَدۡ خَلَقۡنَا ٱلۡإِنسَـٰنَ مِن صَلۡصَـٰلࣲ مِّنۡ حَمَإࣲ مَّسۡنُونࣲ * وَٱلۡجَاۤنَّ خَلَقۡنَـٰهُ مِن قَبۡلُ مِن نَّارِ ٱلسَّمُومِ.*

"Yaqeenan Hamne Insaan ko sadhi hui Matti ke sookhe gaare se banaya. Isse qabl Ham Jinnaat ko Zehreeli Aag se paida kar chuke hain."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 26 - 27)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer: (Cont'd)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🧞‍♂️😈

Imam Reza (as) ki zubani "Haroot o Maroot" ka waqea bayan hua. Is guftugu mein Aap (as) ne Malaika ke mutalliq farmaya ke Malaika Masoom hain. Aur Allah ke Lutf o Karam ki wajah se har tarah ke Kufr aur Fe'l e Qabeeh (Evil Actions) se Paak hain.

Mehfil mein baithe afraad ne sawal kiya 'to kya Iblees Farishta nahi tha?'

Imam (as) ne farmaya:

"Nahi Iblees Farishta nahi tha. Uska talluq Qaum e Jinn se hai, uske mutalliq Allah Ta'ala ne wazeh taur par kaha hai (15:27)"

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

🧞‍♂️😈

"Jaan" Iblees ka Waalid tha aur Qaum e Jinnat mein Momin o Kafir, Yahood o Nasaara aur mukhtalif Adyaan (Religions) ke Pairokar hote hain. Shayateen ka talluq Nasle Iblees se hai. Is Nasl mein koi Momin nahi hai albatta sirf ek Fard Saheb e Imaan tha jiska Naam Ham bin Heem bin Laqees bin Iblees tha. Woh Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki khidmat mein bhi hazir hua tha. Woh bada lahim o jaseem jassa (bold body) rakhne wala tha. AanHazrat (saww) ne usse uska naam o nasab poochha to usne bataya ke "mein Ham bin Heem bin Laqees bin Iblees hun. Jab Qabeel ne apne Bhai Habeel ko qatl kiya tha to us waqt meri Umr chand baras ki thi. Us waqt mein logon ko Raaste se bhatkata tha, khaana kharab karta tha."

AanHazrat (saww) ne farmaya: "Jiska Bachpan itna kharab ho to uska budhapa kitna Napaak hoga."

"Jab Ibrahim (as) ko Naar e Namrood mein dala gaya aur Aag unke liye thandi aur Salamti bani to us waqt bhi mein wahan maujood tha. Jab Hazrat Musa (as) ke zamane mein Allah ne Firaun ko gharq kiya aur Bani Israel ko najaat di to us waqt mein Hazrat Musa (as) ke saath maujood tha. Hazrat Hud (as) wa Hazrat Saleh (as) ke saath bhi raha hun aur unki Bad-Dua par meine unhe malamat bhi ki thi."

"Meine Aasmani Kitaben padhi hain, jin mein Aap (saww) ki Basharat di gayi thi aur meine guzishta Anbiya (as) ki zabaan se Aap (saww) ke Fazail sune the aur meine unki zabaani suna tha ke Aap (saww) tamam Anbiya ke Sardar honge. Allah Ta'ala ne jo Kitab Aap (saww) par naazil ki hai us mein se mujhe bhi kuchh taleem farmayen."

Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) se farmaya ke "ise Qur'an ki kuchh Suraton ki taleem do."

Haam ne kaha: "Ya Rasoolullah (saww)! Ham sirf Nabi ki Ita'at karte hain ya Nabi ke Wasi ki Ita'at karte hain, ye kaun hain?"

Aap (saww) ne farmaya:

"Ye mera Bhai, mera Wasi, mera Vazir aur mera Waaris Ali ibne Abi Talib (as) hai."

Ham ne kaha:

"Ji hain, ye wohi hai jiska Naam sabqa Kitabon mein "Eliya" ( *ایلیا* ) hai."

Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ne use chand Suraton ki taleem di. Jab Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ne Jange Siffin ki to Jange Siffin ki shadeed tareen ladayi "Lailatul Hareer" ( *لیلة الهرير* ) mein hui thi. Us Raat woh Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ki khidmat mein hazir hua tha.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain, Kitab Mo'jezat e Aale Muhammad (as), Vol 1)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 🧞‍♂️😈

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Malaaek (Farishte) ye samajhte the ke Iblees unhi mein se hai, jab ke Ilm e Ilahi mein ye tha ke wo unme se nahi. Chunaanche, uski zidd aur gazab ki wajah se uske dil ki baato'n ko baahar nikaal diya. Chunaanche, Iblees na kaha, "Tu ne mujhe aag se aur usay (Adam [as] ko) mitti se paida kiya hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v6, p505)

🧞‍♂️😈

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Baap Teen hain:

(1) Hazrat Adam (as), jinki Aulaad mein Momin bhi hain aur Kafir bhi hain.

(2) Jaan uski Nasl Kafiron par mushtamil hai.

(3) Iblees, uski Nasl bhi Kafiron par mushtamil hai. Un mein Zaujain milaap nahi hota, woh Ande deta hai aur usse bachche paida hote hain, uski Nasl mein saare hi Nar (Male) hote hain Mada (Female) nahi hoti."

(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

Nafsani Khwahishon ki giraft mazboot hui. Gumrahiyon ne zor pakda. Fitno ne Sar uthaya, aur Baatil ki ban aayi!......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦️ KHILQAT-E-ADAM (as)♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1768)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذۡ قَالَ رَبُّكَ لِلۡمَلَـٰۤىِٕكَةِ إِنِّی خَـٰلِقُۢ بَشَرࣰا مِّن صَلۡصَـٰلࣲ مِّنۡ حَمَإࣲ مَّسۡنُونࣲ * فَإِذَا سَوَّیۡتُهُۥ وَنَفَخۡتُ فِیهِ مِن رُّوحِی فَقَعُوا۟ لَهُۥ سَـٰجِدِینَ.*

"Aur jab tere Parwardigar ne Farishton se kaha ke Mein Sadhi hui Matti ke sookhe gaare se ek Insaan bana raha hun. Jab Mein is poora bana lun aur is mein Apni Rooh phoonk dun to tum iske aage Sajde mein gir jana."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 28 - 29)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🕌

Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):

"Allah Ta'ala ne Takhleeq e Adam (as) (Creation) se pehle Bazm-e-Malaika mein Hujjat tamam karne ke liye Paidaish e Adam (as) ka Ailaan kiya. Allah Ta'ala ne Meethe Paani ka chullu liya aur use khushk (dry) kiya. Wo jam gaya aur awaaz dene laga. Allah Ta'ala ne is Maadde se Farmaya ke Mein Anbiya o Mursaleen aur apne Saleh Bande aur Hidayat Yafta Rehbar jo Jannat ke Daayi hon aur unke Pairokaron ko tujh se paida karuga aur Mein koi parwa nahi karunga. Mein Apne Afa'al ke liye kisi ka Jawabdeh nahi hun jabke poori Makhlooq Mere liye Jawabdeh hai."

"Iske baad Allah ne kadwe Paani ka ek chullu liya aur use jamaya to wo khan khan bolne laga. Allah Ta'ala ne usse Farmaya: 'Mein tujh se Jabbar, *فراعنہ* (Pharoah), Sarkash aur Shayateen ke bhai band paida karunga aur tujh sw hi Dozakh ke Daayi aur unke Pairokar ko paida karunga. Mein koi parwa nahi karunga. Mein Apne Afa'al ke liye kisi ka Jawabdeh nahi hun jabke poori Makhlooq Meri Jawabdeh hai. Allah ne is mein "Bada - *بداء* " ki shart rakhi aayed ki thi jabke Ahle Jannat ke liye koi Shart nahi rakhi thi. Phir Allah ne dono qism ke Paani ek doosre se mila diye. Jab wo khan khan karne lage to inhe Apne Arsh ke saamne rkhwa diya."

"Phir Allah ne Chaar Farishton ko Hukm diya ke woh chaaron taraf ki Hawayen chalayen. Chunanche is dher par chaaron taraf se Hawayen chalen aur in chaaron Hawaon ke chalne se chaar  Tabaye (Nature) ne janam liya. Badan mein jo Reeh (Wind) paayi jaati hai iska talluq Shumali Hawa (Northern Wind) se hai. Ikhlaate Arba (Quarter Mixture) mein se doosri cheez Balgham hai, iska talluq Baade Saba (Morning Spring) se hai. Badan mein Sauda paya jata hai, iska talluq Maghribi Hawa (Western Wind) se hai. Aur Jism mein Khoon paya jata, iska talluq Junoobi Hawa (Southern Wind) se hai.

Jab Jism mein Akhlaat (Mixer) aa gaye to Jism mukammal ho gaya. Jism mein maujood Reeh (Wind) ki wajah se Insaan mein Hubbe Hayat (Love of Life), Lambi Ummeeden aur Hirs (Greed) ne Janam liya. Aur Jism mein maujood Balgham ki wajah se Khaane Peene ki Khwahish aur Narmi ne Janam liya. Jism mein maujood Kadwahat yani Sauda ki wajah se Ghussa, Pagalpan, Shaitani Jabr, Sarkashi aur Jaldbaazi ne Janam liya aur Jism mein Khoon ki wajah se Auraton ki Mohabbat, Azaat ki Khwahish aur Afa'al e Haram karne ki Jasarat aur Khwahishat ne Janam liya."

(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

Magar Khuda ne Adam [as] ko Mitti jaisi maamuli cheez se paida kiya taaki unse Ghuroor o Takabbur aur Khud-pasandi ko door kar de."

(Meezan ul Hikmah (Intekhaab o Takhlees), v3, p195)

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)
