⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦️ *KHILQAT-E-ADAM (as)*♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1769)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذۡ قَالَ رَبُّكَ لِلۡمَلَـٰۤىِٕكَةِ إِنِّی خَـٰلِقُۢ بَشَرࣰا مِّن صَلۡصَـٰلࣲ مِّنۡ حَمَإࣲ مَّسۡنُونࣲ * فَإِذَا سَوَّیۡتُهُۥ وَنَفَخۡتُ فِیهِ مِن رُّوحِی فَقَعُوا۟ لَهُۥ سَـٰجِدِینَ.*

"Aur jab tere Parwardigar ne Farishton se kaha ke Mein Sadhi hui Matti ke sookhe gaare se ek Insaan bana raha hun. Jab Mein is poora bana lun aur is mein Apni Rooh phoonk dun to tum iske aage Sajde mein gir jana."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 28 - 29)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🕌

Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):

"Phir Allah ne sakht o Naram aur Shireen o shorazar Zameen se Mitti jama ki, use Paani se itna bhigoya ke wo saaf ho kar nithar gayi aur tari se itna goondha ke us mein lass paida ho gaya. Isse ek aisi surat banayi jis mein mod hai aur Jod A'aza hain aur mukhtalif hisse. Ise yaha tak sukhaya ke wo khud tham gayi aur itna sakht kiya ke wo khankhanane lagi. Ek waqt e moayyan aur muddat e maloom tak use yun hi rehne diya. Phir us mein Rooh phoonki aur wo aise Insaan ki surat mein khadi ho gayi jo Quwwat e Zehni ko harkat denewala, Fikri Harkaat se tasarrufaat  karnewala, A'aza o Jawareh se khidmat lene wala aur Haath Pairon ko chalane wala. Aisi shanakht ka Malik hai jisse Haq o Baatil mein tameez karta hai aur mukhtalif Mazaon, Buon, Rangon aur Jinson mein farq karta hai. Khud Ranga rang ki Mitti aur milti julti hui moafiq cheezon aur mukhalif ziddon (opposite) aur mutazad (contradictory) khalton se uska Khameer hua hai yaani woh Garmi, Sardi, Tari, Khushki ka Paikar hai. Phir Allah ne Farishton se Chaaha ke woh Uski sonpi hui wadi'at (sipurdgi) ada karen aur Uske Paiman e Wasiyyat ko poora karen jo Sajdah e Adam (as) ke Hukm ko tasleem karne aur Uski Buzurgi ke saamne Tawazoh o Forotani (Humbleness) ke liye tha. Isliye Allah ne kaha ke Adam ko Sajdah karo. Iblees ke siwa sabne Sajdah kiya. Use Asbiyyat (Tassub) ne gher liya. Bad-bakhti us par chha gayi aur Aag se paida hone ki wajah se apne aap ko buzurg o bartar samajha aur khankhanati hui Mitti ki Makhlooq ko Zaleel jaana. Allah ne use Mohlat di taake woh poore taur par Ghazab ka Mustaheq ban jaye aur (Bani Adam ki) Azmaish takmeel tak pahunche aur Wada poora ho jaye. Chunaanche Allah ne usse kaha ke tujhe waqt e moayyan ke Din tak ki Mohlat hai."

(Nahjul Balagha, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

Hazrat Imam Mohd Baqir (as):

"Allah ne Ahle Imaan ke liye alaihda Teenat muqarrar ki aur Ahle Kufr ke liye alaihda Teenat muqarrar ki, lekin Usne apni Maslehet ke tehet dono ko aapas mein mila diya. Yehi wajah hai ke Momin se kabhi Badkariyan sarzad hoti hain aur Munkarin e Haq se kabhi Nek kaam sarzad hote hain."

(Noorus Saqlain)

Aur Maula Aapki Madare Grami Janabe Fatema Zehra (sa) par qayamat toot padi! Malaika qatar dar qatar Apke Walid e Grami ke huzoor Taziyat ke liye aaye. Aala Illiyeen mein Saf e Matam bichh gayi. Hooren apni Rukhsaron par Tamache mar mar kar nidhal ho gayi, Aasmaan aur Aasmaani Makhlooq, Jannat aur Jannat ke Dar o Diwaar, Bulandiyon aur Pastiyon, Samandaron aur Machhliyon, Jannat ke Khuddam mil kar Aapki Musibat par Khoon ke Aansu bahaye.!!!!!!!"

               *19th Safar 1443*

    *27th September 2021, Monday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦️ KHILQAT-E-ADAM (as)♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1770)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذۡ قَالَ رَبُّكَ لِلۡمَلَـٰۤىِٕكَةِ إِنِّی خَـٰلِقُۢ بَشَرࣰا مِّن صَلۡصَـٰلࣲ مِّنۡ حَمَإࣲ مَّسۡنُونࣲ * فَإِذَا سَوَّیۡتُهُۥ وَنَفَخۡتُ فِیهِ مِن رُّوحِی فَقَعُوا۟ لَهُۥ سَـٰجِدِینَ.*

_"Aur jab tere Parwardigar ne Farishton se kaha ke Mein Sadhi hui Matti ke sookhe gaare se ek Insaan bana raha hun. Jab Mein is poora bana lun aur is mein Apni Rooh phoonk dun to tum iske aage Sajde mein gir jana."_

(Surah Al-Hijr: 28 - 29)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🌬️🍃 Rooh:

Imam Sadiq (as) se Rooh ke mutalliq poochha jiske mutalliq farmaya hai ke jab Mein Adam (as) mein Apni Rooh phoonk lun.

Imam (as) ne farmaya:

"Woh Khuda ki paida kardah Rooh thi aur Hazrat Esa (as) mein bhi Khuda ki paida kardah Rooh thi."

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🌬️🍃

Imam Baqir (as) se Ayat ke is hisse par sawal hua: "Allah ne Adam (as) ko Apni Surat par banaya."

Imam (as) ne farmaya:

" Allah ne Hazrat Adam (as) ko khoobsurat Shakal o Surat ata farmayi aur ye Surat Khuda ko itni Pasand aayi ke Usne iski izaafat (Nisbat) Apni taraf di. Ye Izaafat bawajah Sharaf hai jaisa ke Ka'abe ki Nisbat Khuda Apni taraf ki aur use Apna Ghar qarar diya aur isi tarah se Allah ne Rooh ki Nisbat bhi Apni taraf ki  (15:29)( *روحی* )"_

(Kitabut Tauheed, Noorus Saqlain)

🌬️🍃

Imam Baqir (as):

_"Rooh *(روح)* Hawa ki tarah mutharrik (flow) hai aur Lafz *روح* mushtaq hai *ریح* se. Ise Rooh kehne ki wajah ye hai ke ye Reeh (Hawa) ka ham Jins hai. Allah ne is Rooh ki izafat Apni taraf isliye ki hai kyonki Allah ne use baqi Arwaah se chun liya tha. Jis tarah se Khuda ne ek Ghar ko baqi gharon se chuna to use Apna Ghar keh diya aur ek Rasool ko Bazme Rusul mein se chuna to us Apna Khaleel keh diya. Ye sab ke sab Makhlooq hain, Masnoo' (Artificial) hain, Ehdaas kardah (created) hain, Marboob ( *مربوب* ) hain aur Tadbeer Shudah (Pre-Planned) hain."

(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🌬️🍃

Imam Baqir (as):

"Ayat *وَنَفَخۡتُ فِیهِ مِن رُّوحِی* ka ek Mafhoom ye bhi hai ke Mein Apni Qudrat mein se is mein phoonk dun."

(Kitabut Tauheed, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

Imam Baqir (as):

"Jab Allah ne Rooh ko Hazrat Adam (as) mein dakhil hone ka Hukm diya tha to wo Nakhush ho kar dakhil hui. Khuda ne Farmaya: 'Tu Nakhush ho kar dakhil hogi aur Nakhush ho kar Jism se bahar aayegi."

(Qurbul Asnaad, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Ziyarat ke akhir mein Dua:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"......Bare Ilaha! Is Ba-Barkat wa Ba-Izzat Jagah ke tufail, Muhammad wa Aale Muhammad (as) par Darood bhej. (Allahumma Swalle ala Muhammadin wa Aale Muhammad wa Ajjil Farajahum) Mujhe unke saath mehshoor farma aur unki Shafa'at ke sabab mujhe Jannat ata kar.

Bare Ilaha! Aye jald Hisaab Karnewale, Aye Sabse Karim Hasti, aur Aye Sabse Bade Hakim! Mein Teri Bargaj mein tamam Jahano ki taraf Tere Rasool aur Akheri Nabi Hazrat Muhammad Mustafa (saww), unke Cousin bhai, Tawana Bazu, Danush aur Agaahi ke Markaz Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali Ibne Abi Taalib (as)...... (waasta deta hun ke un par Darood nazil farma)......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

 **********************************

               *21st Safar 1443*

  *29th September 2021, Wednesday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                 ♦️ *IBLEES*♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1771)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَسَجَدَ ٱلۡمَلَـٰۤىِٕكَةُ كُلُّهُمۡ أَجۡمَعُونَ * إِلَّاۤ إِبۡلِیسَ أَبَىٰۤ أَن یَكُونَ مَعَ ٱلسَّـٰجِدِینَ * قَالَ یَـٰۤإِبۡلِیسُ مَا لَكَ أَلَّا تَكُونَ مَعَ ٱلسَّـٰجِدِینَ * قَالَ لَمۡ أَكُن لِّأَسۡجُدَ لِبَشَرٍ خَلَقۡتَهُۥ مِن صَلۡصَـٰلࣲ مِّنۡ حَمَإࣲ مَّسۡنُونࣲ.*

"Sab ke sab Farishton ne Sajdah kiya siwai Iblees ke. Usne Sajdah karne walon ka saath dene se Inkaar kar diya. Khuda ne kaha: 'Aye Iblees! Kya wajah hai ke tu ne Sajdah karne walon ka saath kyon na diya?' Usne kaha: 'Mein is Bashar ko Sajdah nahi karunga jise Tu ne Sadhi hui Mitti ke sookhe gaare se paida kiya hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 30 - 33)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Malaaek (Farishte) ye samajhte the ke Iblees unhi mein se hai, jabke Ilm e Ilahi mein ye tha ke woh un mein se nahi. Chunanche, uski zidd aur ghazab ki wajah se uske dil ki baato'n ko baahar nikaal diya. Chunanche, Iblees na kaha, "Tu ne mujhe Aag se aur use (Adam [as] ko) Mitti se paida kiya hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v6, p505)

🕌

Imam Ali (as):

"Lambe Sajde karo kyunki ye baat Iblees par is liye badi garaa'n (bhaari) guzarti hai ke use Sajde ka Hukm mila tha to usne na-farmaani ki thi aur Bande ko Sajde ka hukm mila hai to usne Sajda kiya hai aur najaat ka haqdaar bana hai."

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p596)

🕌🧎🏻‍♂️

Imam Ali (as):

" Jab koi shakhs Namaz padhta hai to Iblees usko Hasad ki nigaah se dekhta hai, kyunki uspar Allah ki Rehmat ka nuzool ho raha hota hai."

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p624)

🕌

Imam Ali (as):

"Khuda ne Shaitan ke saath kya kiya? Is se sabaq lo ke itni lambi uski Ibadato'n, mehnato'n par sirf ek pal (one second) ke Takabbur ne paani pher diya. Isliye tum bhi Khuda ke dushman (Iblees) se bacho ke wo kahi'n tum ko bhi apni bimari na lagaa de."

(Meezan ul Hikmah (Intekhaab o Takhlees), v3, p193)

🤲🏻

Ziyarat ke akhir mein Dua:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"(Mein Teri Bargah mein!).......... Tamam Jahano ki Khwateen ki Sardar Hazrat Fatema Zehra (sa). Parhezgaron ke Muhafiz Imam Hasan Zaki (as), Shohada ke Sayyed o Sardar Hazrat Abi Abdullah Al Husain (as). Nez unki Mazloom Itrat. Abidon ki Zeenat Hazrat Ali bin Husain (as), juyaye Haq, logon ke Markaze Tawajjah, Hazrat Mohd bin Ali (as), sabse bade Sadiqul Qaul Hazrat Jafar bin Mohd (as), Deen ke Madadgar, Hazrat Ali bin Musa (as). Pairokaron ke Rahnuma Hazrat Mohd bin Ali (as), sabse bade Parsa Hazrat Ali bin Mohd (as)....... (ka waasta deta hun ke un par Darood nazil farma)....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

 **********************************

               *22nd Safar 1443*

   *30th September 2021, Thursday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                 ♦️ LAA'NAT ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1772)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَالَ فَٱخۡرُجۡ مِنۡهَا فَإِنَّكَ رَجِیمࣱ * وَإِنَّ عَلَیۡكَ ٱللَّعۡنَةَ إِلَىٰ یَوۡمِ ٱلدِّینِ*

"Khuda ne kaha: 'Yahan se nikal ja, yaqeenan tu Raandahe Dargah (Mardood) hai aur Roze Qayamat tak tujh par La'anat hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 34 - 35)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🕌

Jab Shaitan ne Allah ke Khalifa ko Sajdah nahi kiya aur Allah ke Hukm ki Nafarmani ki to La'anat ka mustaheq ho gaya. Isse ye sabit hai ke jo Allah ke Wali ki Wilayat qubool na kare woh bhi La'anat ka mustaheq hai. Jo Musalman Shirk Shirk ki duhayi deten hain woh samajh len ke woh kis ke Pairokar hain.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

🙇‍♂️

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Iblees ne 4 martaba faryaad ki: (1) *Jab uspar La'nat ki gayi,* (2) Jab woh zameen par utaara gaya, (3) Jab Rasulallah ko mab'oos kiya gaya, (4) Jab Surah Fatiha naazil hui."

(Khisaal, p138)

🕌

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Jab koi shakhs zameen par Ghuroor o Takabbur se raasta chalta hai to khud zameen aur zameen ke upar aur niche jitni cheezein hain sab uspar Laa'nat karti hain."

(Tehzibul Islam, p509)

🤲🏻

Ziyarat ke akhir mein Dua:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"(Mein Teri Bargah mein!).......... Nez Silsila e Nabuwwat o Imamat ke tamam Buzurgon ke Waaris aur Aye Allah! Teri tamam Makhlooq par Hujjat (atfs) ka waasta deta hun ke Tu Mohd o Aale Muhammad (as) un par jo Aale Taha wa Yaseen bhi hain aur Sachche aur Nekokar bhi, Darood nazil farma....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

               23rd Safar 1443

       1st October 2021, Friday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦️ SHAITAN KO MOHLAT♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1773)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالَ رَبِّ فَأَنظِرۡنِیۤ إِلَىٰ یَوۡمِ یُبۡعَثُونَ * قَالَ فَإِنَّكَ مِنَ ٱلۡمُنظَرِینَ * إِلَىٰ یَوۡمِ ٱلۡوَقۡتِ ٱلۡمَعۡلُومِ.

"Usne kaha: Mujhe us Din tak ke liye Mohlat de jab log uthaye jayenge.' Khuda ne Farmaya: 'Yaqeenan tu Mohlat Yafta afraad mein se hai, Waqt e Maloom ke Din tak."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 36 - 38)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as) se poochha gaya ke Iblees ko Mohlat kyon di gayi?

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Isse Soor phoonke jaane ki ghadi murad hai. Pehle aur doosre Soor ke darmiyani waqfe mein Iblees par Maut taari ho jayegi."

Wahab! Kya tum samjhte ho ke isse Qayamat ka Din murad hai? Nahi, aisa nahi hai. Allah ne ise Zahoor e Qaem (atfs) tak Mohlat di hai. Jab hamare Qaem (atfs) Zahoor farmayenge aur woh Masjid e Kufa mein baithe honge to Iblees unke saamne aayega aur ghutno ke bal unke saamne baith jayega aur kahega: 'Haye is Din mein meri Badnaseebi!' Hazrat Qaem (atfs) uski Peshani se pakad kar uski gardan qalam (cut) kar denge. Chunanche wohi Din "Yaumil Waqtil Maloom." hai."

(Ilalush Sharaye, Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌🧎🏻‍♂️

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Iblees ne Chauthe Aasmaan par do Rakat Namaz ada ki thi jis mein use 6000 Saal sarf hue the. Allah Ta'ala ne uski Ibaadat ko madde nazar rakh kar use Mohlat di hai."

(Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Banda e Momin Gunah karta hai to usko Mohlat di jaati hai Subah se Raat tak. Pus, agar woh Allah se Tauba o Astagfaar karta hai to wo Gunah nahi likha jaata."

(Al Kaafi, v5, p37)

🤲🏻

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Mere Jadd Imam Sajjad (as) jab Maqam e Multazim (Obedience) par pahunchte the to Aap (as) Bargahe Ahdiyyat (God) mein ye Dua maanga karte the ke:

"Parwardigar! Mere paas Gunahon aur Khataon ke dher hain jabke Tere paas Rehmat o Maghferat ke dher hain. Aye Woh Zaat! Jisne apne napasandidah tareen Fard ki Mohlat ki Dua Qubool kiya tha. Meri Dua ko nhi Qubool Farma, aur meri falan falan Haajat poori Farma."

(Noorus Saqlain)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

**********************************

               24th Safar 1443

    2nd October 2021, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦️ SHAITAN BAIHKANEWALA HAI ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1774)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالَ رَبِّ بِمَاۤ أَغۡوَیۡتَنِی لَأُزَیِّنَنَّ لَهُمۡ فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ وَلَأُغۡوِیَنَّهُمۡ أَجۡمَعِینَ * إِلَّا عِبَادَكَ مِنۡهُمُ ٱلۡمُخۡلَصِینَ

"Usne kaha: 'Mere Rab jaise Tu ne mujhe Gumrah kiya hai, mein Zameen par unke liye Dil Farebi (Deviation) ka samaan faraham kar ke un sab ko Gumrah karunga. Siwai Tere un Bandon ke jinhe Khaalis kar liya gaya hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 39 - 40)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🕌

Hazrat Ali (as):

"Aye Khuda ke Bandon! Allah ke Dushman se Daro ke kahin woh tumhe apna Rog na laga de aur apni pukar se tumhe na behkaye aur apne sawar aur pyade le kar tum par chadh na daude, isliye ke meri Jaan ki Qasam! Usne Sharangezi ke Teer ko Chille Kaman mein jod rakha hai aur qareeb ki jagah se tumhe apne Nishaane ki zad par rakh kar Kaman ko zor se kheench liya hai jaisa ke Allah ne uski zabani farmya hai ke, "Aye mere Parwardigar! Chunke Tu ne mujhe behkaya hai ab mein bhi unke saamne Zameen mein Gunahon ko saka kar pesh karunga aur un sab ko Gumrah karunga. Halaanke usne ye atkal pachchu kaha tha aur ghalat guman ki bena par (andheri mein) Teer chalaya tha, lekin Farzandan Raoonat (Naughty), Baradaran e Asbiyyat (tassub), Ghuroor o Jahiliyyat shehsawaron ne uski baat ko sachcha kar dikhaya."

(Nahjul Balagha)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️

Imam Sajjad (as):

" Khuda Wande Kareem ne Machhli ke shikaar karne waalo'n ko maskh (deform) kar diya to kya hoga un logo'n ka jinhone na-haq Aulaad e Rasool (saww) ko qatl kiya aur unki hurmat ki hatak ki? Khuda Wande Kareem ne Duniya mein chaahe un logo'n ko Saza e Maskh nahi di lekin Azaab e Akherat jo unke liye tayyar hai wo us maskh hone se bahut zyada hai."

Pus, ek shakhs ne Imam (as) ki khidmat mein arz ki, "Yabn Rasulallah (as)! Kuchh Naasibi hum par eteraaz karte hain ke agar Qatl e Husain (as) na-jaayez hota aur Bani Israel ke Machhli ke shikaar se uska jurm sangeen hota to phir qaatilaan e Husain (as) par Khuda ka ghazab kyun naazil nahi hua jaisa ke Bani Israel ke Machhli ke shikaariyo'n par naazil hua?"

Imam (as) ne farmaya:

"Un Naasibiyo'n se kaho ke Iblees ka Gunah jn logo'n se sangeen hai jo uske Behkaane se Gumrah hue, lekin woh garq ho gaye jinka Gunah halka tha aur woh garq nahi hua jiska Gunah sangeen tha. Pus, Khuda ne apni Maslehat se sangeen jurm waale ko Mohlat de di aur halke jurm waale ko Moazzab (Azaab mein mubtela) kar diya. Isi tarah Bani Israel ke shikaari jo halke jurm waale the woh moazzab (Azaab mein mubtela) ho gaye aur Imam Husain (as) ke qaatil ko Iblees ki tarah ek waqt tak Mohlat di gayi halaa'nki unka jurm sangeen tha."  Phir aap se sawaal hua, "Ye fe'l to guzishta zamane Bani Israil ka tha phir zamana e Islam ke Bani Israel ko is fe'l se kyun mukhatib kiya jaa raha hai?" To Imam (as) ne farmaya jiska ma-hasl (conclulsion / nishkarsh) ye hai, "Ek shakhs ki qaum agar kisi ko qatl kar de ya kahi'n daaka daal de to us shakhs ko kaha jaa sakta hai ke tum ne fulaa'n ko qatl kiya ya fulaa'n par daaka daala, halaa'nki ye us qatl ya daake mein shareek nahi tha. Aur iske alaawa kyunki Bani Israel apne Ajdaad (forefathers) ke af'aal (actions) par raazi the, lihaaza unko unke fe'l ka shareek qaraar diya gaya. Aur unko taubeekh aur sarzanish (daa'ntt fattkaar) ki gayi taaki apne Faasid aqeede (corrupted belief) se baaz aa kar Islami Taalimaat par Amal karne ki koshish kare."

(Tafseer e Anwaar e Najaf, v2, p120)

🙏🏻

Imam Ali (as)

se puchha gaya ke agar koi shakhs Tauba kar ke phir Gunah kare aur baar baar Tauba karta rahe? Imam (as) ne farmaya,

"Allah uske Gunah Baksh dega." Phir puchha gaya ke, "Is tarah kab tak hota rahega?" Imam (as) ne farmaya, "Jab tak Shaitan se behkaane ki quwwat salb na ho (chheen na li) jaaye."

(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p33)

🤲🏻

Ziyarat ke akhir mein Dua:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Aur mujhe Roze Qayamat un logon mein shamil farma le jinko us Din Amn o Itminan hasil hoga, aur woh us pareshani wale Din bhi khush o Khurram honge aur Jinhe Jannat Rizwan ki khush khabari sunayi jayegi......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

               25th Safar 1443

      3rd October 2021, Sunday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

         ♦️ MUKHLIS BANDA♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1775)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالَ رَبِّ بِمَاۤ أَغۡوَیۡتَنِی لَأُزَیِّنَنَّ لَهُمۡ فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ وَلَأُغۡوِیَنَّهُمۡ أَجۡمَعِینَ إِلَّا عِبَادَكَ مِنۡهُمُ ٱلۡمُخۡلَصِین*

"Usne kaha: 'Mere Rab jaise Tu ne mujhe Gumrah kiya hai, mein Zameen par unke liye Dil Farebi (Deviation) ka samaan faraham kar ke un sab ko Gumrah karunga. Siwai Tere un Bandon ke jinhe Khaalis kar liya gaya hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 39 - 40)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🕌 🧎🏻‍♂️

Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Jibrael Amin (as) se kaha ke "Ikhlaas - اخلاص "  ka kya mafhoom hai?

Jibrael (as) ne farmaya:

"Mukhlis woh hai jo logon se sawal na kare, yahan tak ke woh paa le aur jab woh paa le to woh Raazi ho jaye aur agar uske paas kuchh bach jaye to woh Khuda ke naam par khairat kar de. Jisne Makhlooq se sawal na kiya to usne Allah Ta'ala ki uboodiyyat ka iqraar kiya aur jo paa kar raazi ho jaye woh shakhs Khuda se Raazi hai aur Allah usse Raazi hai aur jab woh Allah ke Naam par kuchh deta hai to use Khuda par Bharosa hota hai."

(Kitab Ma'anil Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌🧎🏻‍♂️

Hazrat Esa (as):

"Mukhlis (Sincere) woh hota hai jo Allah Ta'ala hi ke liye Amal karta hai aur is baat ko pasand nahi karta ke us Amal ki koi shakhs taarif kare."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Momin ke aage har cheez sar jhuka deti hai aur usse darti hai. Jab Momin Khuda ke liye Mukhlis hota hai to Allah bhi har cheez ko oos se khauf-zada kar deta hai, hatta ke zameen ke hashraat (insects), darindo'n aur aasmaan ke parindo'n ko bhi."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3, p124)

🕌

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Khuda nahi chahta ke uska Mukhlis banda mashkook (suspicious) Raaste se Rizq paaye."

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p21)

🤲🏻

Ziyarat ke akhir mein Dua:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Bare Ilaha! Aye Arhamur Rahemeen Apni Rehmat ke Sadqe mein mera naam Musalmano mein likh le, mujhe Saleh aur Nekokar logon mein shamil farma le, mere pasmandgan aur baad wali Naslon mein Zikre Sachhayi aur bhalayi ke saath jaari rakh, Baghiyon ke muqabile mein meri Nusrat farma, Hasad karne walon ki Chaal o Shar se meri hifazat farma, Zalimon ke haathon ko meri jaanib badhne se rok de......."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

               *26th Safar 1443*

      *4th October 2021, Monday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦️ PAIRVANE ALI (as) PAR SHAITAN MUSALLAT NAHI HO SAKTA ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1776)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَالَ هَـٰذَا صِرَ ٰ⁠طٌ عَلَیَّ مُسۡتَقِیمٌ * إِنَّ عِبَادِی لَیۡسَ لَكَ عَلَیۡهِمۡ سُلۡطَـٰنٌ إِلَّا مَنِ ٱتَّبَعَكَ مِنَ ٱلۡغَاوِینَ.*

"Khuda ne kaha: 'Ye Raasta hai jo Seedha Mujh tak pahunchta hai. Mere Haqeeqi Bandon par teri koi hukmarani na hogi. Tera bas un behke hue logon par hi chalega jo teri pairavi karenge."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 41 - 42)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🛣️🛤️

Ayat *هَـٰذَا صِرَ ٰ⁠طٌ عَلَیَّ مُسۡتَقِیمٌ* se Hazrat Ali (as) ka Raasta murad hai.

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

📚📖

Jab Qur'an nazil hua to Ashaab hifz, memorise kar liya karte the. Likhne padhne ka dastoor kam tha. Us waqt na Nuqte the, na Eraab. Nuqton aur Eraab ko Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ne apne student Abul Aswad Doyili ko sikhaye. Jaise ke pehle bayan kar chuke hain Qur'an ki 7 copies bani jinki Qara'at alag alag thi.

Isi lehaaz jo Qur'an aaj padha jata hai woh ek khaas Qiraat ka hai.

Lekin Eraab ki tabdeeli se Ayat is tarah se bhi padhi ja sakti hai aur ye Qira'at e Ahlebait (as) mein bhi hai: *هَـٰذَا صِرَ ٰ⁠طُ عَلَیٍّ مُسۡتَقِیمٌ* (Haza Sirato Aliyyin Mustaqeem - "Yehi Ali (as) ka Raasta Seedha hai." Ise Tehreef nahi kaha ja sakta, kyunki Alfaaz wohi hai. Lekin Imam (as) ka Hukm ke mutabiq jo raaej Qur'an hai usi ko padha jaye.

👺

 Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hamare Mannewalon par Iblees ka koi tasallut nahi hai."

Raavi ne sawal kiya ke in mein to Gunehgar bhi hain?

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Jo kuchh tum ne samajh liya hai usse meri wo murad nahi hai. Mein ye kehna chahta hun ke Iblees unki nazar mein Imaan ko qabil e Nafrat aur Kufr ko laeq e Muhabbat nahi bana sakta."

(Kitab Ma'anil Akhbar, Noorus)

👺

Imam Sadiq (as) ne Abu Baseer se farmaya:

"Aye Abu Mohd! Khuda ne tumhe apni Kitab mein yaad kiya hai aur Usne Iblees se farmaya hai: "Mere Haqeeqi Bando par teri koi hukmarani na hogi." Un Haqeeqi Bando se Aimma Huda (as) aur unke Shia murad hain."

(Rauza e Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)

👺

Imam Baqir (as):

"Is Ayat ka maqsad ye hai ke Khuda ne kaha tha ke tere ikhtiyar mein nahi ke tu Jannat o Dozakh mein kisi ko dakhil kar sake."

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Ham Ahle Rehmat aur Ne'mat o Barkat ka Ghar hain aur ham Zameen ka Sutoon (Pillar) hain aur hamare Shia Islam ki Buniyad rasi hain. Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne hamare aur hamare Shiyon ke Haq mein Dua ki thi. Allah ne hame aur hamare Shiyon ko Iblees ke Tasallut se mehfooz rakha hai (15:42)"

(Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Ziyarat ke akhir mein Dua:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Mujhe Aalal Illiyeen mein Ba-Barkat Peshwaon aur Aimma e Ahlul Bait (as) ke Jawaar (neighbour) mein un Anbiya, Siddiqeen, Shohada aur Saleheen ke saath jama kar, jin par Tu ne Apni Ne'maten nazil farmayi hain......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

 **********************************

               *27th Safar 1443*

      *5th October 2021, Tuesday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

 ♦️ JAHANNUM KE TABAQAAT ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1777)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنَّ جَهَنَّمَ لَمَوۡعِدُهُمۡ أَجۡمَعِینَ * لَهَا سَبۡعَةُ أَبۡوَ ٰ⁠بࣲ لِّكُلِّ بَابࣲ مِّنۡهُمۡ جُزۡءࣱ مَّقۡسُومٌ.*

"Yaqeenan in sab ke liya Dozakh hi Wadagah hai. Uske Saat Darwaze honge, har Darwaze ke liye ek khaas hissa muqarrar kar diya gaya hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 43 - 44)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🚪 🔥

Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim mein marqoom hai ke har Millat ke liye Dozakh mein alaihda alaihda Darwaza hoga. Jannat ke 8 Darwaze honge.

🚪🔥

Majmaul Bayan mein mein manqool hai ke *لَهَا سَبۡعَةُ أَبۡوَ ٰ⁠بࣲ* (Dozakh ke 7 Darwaze honge) ki Ayat ke mutalliq Mufassirin ke do Qaul manqool hain:

Un mein se ek qaul wo hai jiski Riwayat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) se ki gayi hai.

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Dozakh ke 7 Tabaqaat honge aur wo sab ek doosre ke upar honge. Jabke Jannat ki chaudayi mein phaili hui hogi. Tabaqaat e Dozakh ki Tarteeb yun hogi:

Sab se neeche Jahannum hogi, upar Laza hogi, uske upar Hutama hogi, uske upar Saqar hogi, uske upar Jaheem hogi, uske upar Sa'eer hogi aur uske upar Haviya hogi."

Kulaini ki Riwayat mein sab se neeche Haviya aur sab se upar Jahannum hogi.

(Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️ 🚪🔥

Imam Reza (as) se arz kiya gaya: 'Ek shakhs ne marte waqt Wasiyyat ki ke meri Maut ke baad meri Maal mein ek "Juz - *جزو*" Khuda ke Naam par di jaye. Woh shakhs mar gaya. Ab uske Maal mein se kitna hissa dena chahiye?

Imam (as):

"Kyonki Lafz " *جزو*" ka itlaaq Saatvin (7th) hisse par hota hai, jaisa ke Farman e Ilahi hai: (15:44), is Ayat mein Lafz "Juz" ka itlaaq Saatvin hisse par hua."

(Tehzeebul Ahkam, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Ziyarat ke akhir mein Dua:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"Parwardigar! Tujhe Qasam hai: Tere Masoom Nabi (saww) ki, Tere Hatmi Ahkam ki, Tere muqarrarah manhiyyat ki. Aur us Pak o Pakeeza Qabr ki jiske pehlu mein Mahsoom, Maqtool aur Mazloom Imam Dafn hain, ke Tu mujhe Duniya ke Ghamon se Nijaat ata farma......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔹🔹🔹🔹﷽🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

*SHIA CHANNEL COMMEMORATE SHAHADAT OF HAZRAT RASOOLE KHUDA (saww) & IMAM HASAN (as)*

               *28th Safar 1443*

    *6th October 2021, Wednesday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

 ♦️ *JAHANNAM KE TABAQAAT*♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1778)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنَّ جَهَنَّمَ لَمَوۡعِدُهُمۡ أَجۡمَعِینَ * لَهَا سَبۡعَةُ أَبۡوَ ٰ⁠بࣲ لِّكُلِّ بَابࣲ مِّنۡهُمۡ جُزۡءࣱ مَّقۡسُومٌ.*

"Yaqeenan in sab ke liya Dozakh hi Wadagah hai. Uske Saat Darwaze honge, har Darwaze ke liye ek khaas hissa muqarrar kar diya gaya hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 43 - 44)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖 🚪🔥

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd....)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🚪 🔥

Imam Baqir (as):

"Allah ne Dozakh ke 7 Darajaat banaye hain. Sab se Badtareen darje ka Naam "Jaheem - *جحیم*" hai. Jab Ahle Jaheem us mein khade honge to unke dimagh yun ublenge jaisa ke Handi mein Paani ubalta hai."

*وَ اِنَّ الْفُجَّارَ لَفِیْ جَحِیْمٍۚۖ * یَّصْلَوْنَهَا یَوْمَ الدِّیْنِ*

(Surah Infitar: 14-15)

"Dozakh ke doosre Darje ka Naam" Laza - *لظیٰ*" hai.

*كَلَّاۤۖ إِنَّهَا لَظَىٰ * نَزَّاعَةࣰ لِّلشَّوَىٰ * تَدۡعُوا۟ مَنۡ أَدۡبَرَ وَتَوَلَّىٰ * وَجَمَعَ فَأَوۡعَىٰۤ.*

 "Hargiz Nahi, wo to Bhadhakti hui Aag ki Lapat hogi jo Gosht Post ko chaat jayegi. Pukar pukar kar apni taraf bulayegi. Har us shakhs ko jisne Haq sw Munh moda aur Peeth pheri aur Maal jama kiya aur saint saint kar rakha."

(Al Meraj: 15-18)

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(Riwayat will be Cont'd)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️ 🚪🔥

Ek Yahoodi ne Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) 1 se 100 tak ginte se sawal kiye, un mein se ek sawal ye tha:

"Wo Saat (7) kya hain jinka Aathwa (8th) nahi hai?"

Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ne farmaya:

"Wo 7 jinka Aathwa nahi hai wo Dozakh ke 7 Darwaze hain."

(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

*Ziyarat ke akhir mein Dua:*

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"......Mere Muqaddar ki Burayi aur Sharr ko mujh se door kar de aur mujhe Zehrili Aag se bacha le. Bare Ilaha! Tu Apni Ne'mat ke tufail mujhe Izzat o Aabru marhamat farma, mujhe Apni Taqseem ki hui Rozi par raazi rakh, mujhe Apne Karam aur Jood o Sakha se dhanp le, nez mujhe Apni Nagawari aur Naraazgi se mehfooz farma de......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

               *29th Safar 1443*

     *7th October 2021, Thursday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦️ JAHANNAM KE TABAQAAT ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1779)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنَّ جَهَنَّمَ لَمَوۡعِدُهُمۡ أَجۡمَعِینَ * لَهَا سَبۡعَةُ أَبۡوَ ٰ⁠بࣲ لِّكُلِّ بَابࣲ مِّنۡهُمۡ جُزۡءࣱ مَّقۡسُومٌ.*

"Yaqeenan in sab ke liya Dozakh hi Wadagah hai. Uske Saat Darwaze honge, har Darwaze ke liye ek khaas hissa muqarrar kar diya gaya hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 43 - 44)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖 🚪🔥

👉 _*Tafseer:*_  (Cont'd....)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🚪 🔥

Imam Baqir (as):

"Dozakh ke Teesre Darje ka Naam hai" Saqar - *سقر*" aur iske mutalliq Allah Ta'ala ne Farmaya:

*سَأُصۡلِیهِ سَقَرَ * وَمَاۤ أَدۡرَىٰكَ مَا سَقَرُ * لَا تُبۡقِی وَلَا تَذَرُ * لَوَّاحَةࣱ لِّلۡبَشَرِ * عَلَیۡهَا تِسۡعَةَ عَشَرَ.*

"Anqareeb mein use" Saqar" mein dal dunga aur tum kya jaano ke "Saqar" kya hai? Na baqi rakhegi, na chhidegi. Khaal jhulsa denewali. Unnees Karkun us par muqarrar hain." (Al Muddassir: 26-30)"

Aur jab Ahle Saqar se Ahle Jannat poochhenge:

*مَا سَلَكَكُمۡ فِی سَقَرَ * قَالُوا۟ لَمۡ نَكُ مِنَ ٱلۡمُصَلِّینَ * وَلَمۡ نَكُ نُطۡعِمُ ٱلۡمِسۡكِینَ * وَكُنَّا نَخُوضُ مَعَ ٱلۡخَاۤىِٕضِینَ * وَكُنَّا نُكَذِّبُ بِیَوۡمِ ٱلدِّینِ * حَتَّىٰۤ أَتَىٰنَا ٱلۡیَقِینُ * فَمَا تَنفَعُهُمۡ شَفَـٰعَةُ ٱلشَّـٰفِعِینَ.*

"Tumhe kis cheez ne "Saqar" mein dala? Woh kahenge ke "Ham Namaz padhne walo mein se na the aur ham Miskeen ko khana nahi khilaate the aur Haq ke Khilaf baaten bananewalon ke saath mil kar ham bhi baaten banate the aur Roz e Jaza ko ham jhutlate the, yahan tak ke ham par Maut aa gayi. Un logon ko Shafa'at karne walon ki Shafa'at Fayda na degi."

(Al Muddassir: 42-48)

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(Riwayat will be Cont'd)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️ 🚪🔥

Imam Ali (as):

"Jo bhi Jahannam ki Aag se darta hai, wo Haraam cheezo'n se ijtenaab (parhez) karta hai."

(Ghurar al-Hikam, v1, p225)

🤲🏻

Ziyarat ke akhir mein Dua:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"..... Parwardigar! Laghzishon (Slips) se meri hifazat farma. Mere Qaul o Amal ko durust kar de. Meri muddat e Umr ko badha de. Mujhe Dard o Amraaz (Diseases) se aafiyat ata farma de. Aur mujhe Aimma (as) ke sadqe aur Apne Fazl o Karam ke tufail behtareen Ummeedon tak pahucha de....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

♦️ JAHANNAM KE TABAQAAT ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1780)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنَّ جَهَنَّمَ لَمَوۡعِدُهُمۡ أَجۡمَعِینَ * لَهَا سَبۡعَةُ أَبۡوَ ٰ⁠بࣲ لِّكُلِّ بَابࣲ مِّنۡهُمۡ جُزۡءࣱ مَّقۡسُومٌ.*

"Yaqeenan in sab ke liya Dozakh hi Wadagah hai. Uske Saat Darwaze honge, har Darwaze ke liye ek khaas hissa muqarrar kar diya gaya hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 43 - 44)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖 🚪🔥

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd....)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🚪 🔥

Imam Baqir (as):

"....Dozakh ke Chauthe Tabqe ka Naam hai "Hutama - *حطمة*" aur ye wohi hai jiske mutalliq Allah Ta'ala ne Farmaya:

🔥

*كَلَّاۖ لَیُنۢبَذَنَّ فِی ٱلۡحُطَمَةِ * وَمَاۤ أَدۡرَىٰكَ مَا ٱلۡحُطَمَةُ * نَارُ ٱللَّهِ ٱلۡمُوقَدَةُ * ٱلَّتِی تَطَّلِعُ عَلَى ٱلۡأَفۡـِٔدَةِ * إِنَّهَا عَلَیۡهِم مُّؤۡصَدَةࣱ * فِی عَمَدࣲ مُّمَدَّدَةِۭ.*

"Hargiz nahi, woh shakhs to Hutama (Chakna choor karnewali) mein phenk diya jayega aur tum kya jaano ke wo Hutama kya hai? Wo Allah ki khoob bhadkayi hui Aag hai jo Dilon tak pahunchegi aur un par dhank kar band kar di jayegi. Wo oonche oonche Sutoono mein ghire hue honge."

(Al Humazah: 4-9)

🔥

Isi Hutama ke mutalliq Irshaade Ilahi hai:

*إِنَّهَا تَرۡمِی بِشَرَرࣲ كَٱلۡقَصۡرِ * كَأَنَّهُۥ جِمَـٰلَتࣱ صُفۡرࣱ.*

"Wo Aag Mahel jaisi badi badi chingariya phenkegi jo uchhalti hui yun dikhayi degi ke goya woh zard (yellow) rang ke Oont hain."

(Al-Mursalat: 32-33)

🔥

Jo bhi is mein dakhil hoga woh use pees kar Surme ke maanind kar degi magar Rooh nahi maregi jabke Jism pis kar Surma ban jayega to az sare no unhe Jism diya jayega."

........

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(Riwayat will be Cont'd)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️ 🔥

Imam Ali (as):

"Tumhe maalum hona chahiye ke ye naazuk Jild (Chamdi / skin) Jahannam ka Azaab bardaasht Nahi kar sakti, lihaza tum apne aap par Rahem karo."

(Bihaar ul Anwaar v8, p307, Meezan ul Hikmah, v2)

🔥

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Jahannam mein kuchch Chakkiyaa'n hain jinme Ulama e Soo (bad-kaar Ulama) ko khoob peesa jayega."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v6, p793)

🤲🏻

Ziyarat ke akhir mein Dua:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".......Khuda wanda! Muhammad (saww) wa Aale Muhammad (as) par Darood nazil farma, meri Tauba qubool farma le, mere Aansuon par Rahem farma, meri takleef aur ranj o gham mein mera Munis o Ghamkhwar ban ja, meri khatayen Ma'af farma de aur meri Aulad ko Saeed o Saleh bana de....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

♦️ *JAHANNAM KE TABAQAAT*♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1781)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنَّ جَهَنَّمَ لَمَوۡعِدُهُمۡ أَجۡمَعِینَ * لَهَا سَبۡعَةُ أَبۡوَ ٰ⁠بࣲ لِّكُلِّ بَابࣲ مِّنۡهُمۡ جُزۡءࣱ مَّقۡسُومٌ.*

"Yaqeenan in sab ke liya Dozakh hi Wadagah hai. Uske Saat Darwaze honge, har Darwaze ke liye ek khaas hissa muqarrar kar diya gaya hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 43 - 44)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖 🚪🔥

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd....)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🚪 🔥

Imam Baqir (as):

"Dozakh ke Panchven Tabqe ka Naam "Haaviya - *ھاویة*" hai aur iske mutalliq Allah Ta'ala ne Farmaya:

*وَأَمَّا مَنۡ خَفَّتۡ مَوَ ٰ⁠زِینُهُۥ * فَأُمُّهُۥ هَاوِیَةࣱ * وَمَاۤ أَدۡرَىٰكَ مَا هِیَهۡ * نَارٌ حَامِیَةُۢ.*

"Aur jiski Neki ka Palda halka hoga to uski jaaye qarar "Haviya" (Gehri Khaayi) hogi aur tumhe kya khabar ke wo kya cheez hai? Wo Bhadakti hui Aag hai."

(Al Qare'ah: 8-11)

🚪🔥

Aur Maalik Naami Darogha isi Tabqe ka Nigebaan hoga. Log" Maalik" se 🥛 Paani talab karenge to woh unhe Peep mila hua khaulta hua Paani dega. Jab woh Paani peene ke liye Munh badhayenge to uski tapish se unke Chehre ka Gosht gal kar gir padega aur is Mashroob ke mutalliq Allah Ta'ala ne Farmaya:

🥛

*وَقُلِ ٱلۡحَقُّ مِن رَّبِّكُمۡۖ فَمَن شَاۤءَ فَلۡیُؤۡمِن وَمَن شَاۤءَ فَلۡیَكۡفُرۡۚ إِنَّاۤ أَعۡتَدۡنَا لِلظَّـٰلِمِینَ نَارًا أَحَاطَ بِهِمۡ سُرَادِقُهَاۚ وَإِن یَسۡتَغِیثُوا۟ یُغَاثُوا۟ بِمَاۤءࣲ كَٱلۡمُهۡلِ یَشۡوِی ٱلۡوُجُوهَۚ بِئۡسَ ٱلشَّرَابُ وَسَاۤءَتۡ مُرۡتَفَقًا.*

🥛

"Wahan agar woh Paani maangenge to un ki tawaza aise Paani se ki jayegi jo Tel ki talchhat jaisa hoga, unka Munh bhoon dalega woh badtareen Mashroob hoga aur wo jagah badtareen araamgah hogi."

(Al Kahf: 29)

🔥

Jo is mein girega woh 70 Saal tak girta hi jayega aur jab unki Khaal jal jayegi to us ki jagah unhe nayi Khaal pehna di jayegi.

........

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(Riwayat will be Cont'd)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️ 🔥

Imam Ali (as):

"Tumhe maalum hona chahiye ke ye naazuk Jild (Chamdi / skin) Jahannam ka Azaab bardaasht Nahi kar sakti, lihaza tum apne aap par Rahem karo." 

(Bihaar ul Anwaar v8, p307, Meezan ul Hikmah, v2)

🤲🏻

Ziyarat ke akhir mein Dua:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"..... Rabbe Jaleel! Is Azeem Baargah aur ba-Karamat maqam par mere tamam Gunah bakhsh de, mere saare Gham door kar de, mere Rizq mein wus'at ata farma ke fursat na mile, aur mujh par itna Fazl o Karam kar ke mein tamam Makhlooqaat se beniyaaz ho jaon........"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

    11th October 2021, Monday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦️ JAHANNAM KE TABAQAAT ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1782)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَإِنَّ جَهَنَّمَ لَمَوۡعِدُهُمۡ أَجۡمَعِینَ * لَهَا سَبۡعَةُ أَبۡوَ ٰ⁠بࣲ لِّكُلِّ بَابࣲ مِّنۡهُمۡ جُزۡءࣱ مَّقۡسُومٌ.

"Yaqeenan in sab ke liya Dozakh hi Wadagah hai. Uske Saat Darwaze honge, har Darwaze ke liye ek khaas hissa muqarrar kar diya gaya hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 43 - 44)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖 🚪🔥

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd....)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🚪 🔥

Imam Baqir (as):

"Dozakh ke Chhate (6th) Tabqe ka Naam "Sa'eer - سعیر" hai. Us mein Aag ke 300 Parde honge aur har Parde mein Dozakh ke 300 Mahel honge aur har Mahel mein Aag ke 300 Ghar honge aur har Ghar mein Aag ke Azaab ke alawa 300 Azaab honge. Us mein Aag ke bane hue Saanp aur Bichchhu honge aur Aag ka Libaas hoga aur Aag se bane hue Tauq aur Zanjeer honge.

Allah ka Farman hai:

🔥

إِنَّاۤ أَعۡتَدۡنَا لِلۡكَـٰفِرِینَ سَلَـٰسِلَا۟ وَأَغۡلَـٰلࣰا وَسَعِیرًا.

"Kufr karne walon ke liye  Hamne Zanjeeren aur Tauq aur Bhadakti hui Aag muhayya kar rakhi hai."

(Al Daher: 4)

🔥

Dozakh ke Saatvin (7th) Tabqe ka Naam "Jahannam - جھنم" hai aur is mein "Falaq - فلق" hai aur "Falaq" Jahannam ka ek Kuwan hai. Jab wo khola jayega to uske sholon mein tezi aa jayegi aur wo badtareen Azaab ka maqam hai.

"Su'ood - سعود" Dozakh ke darmiyan Tanbe (Copper) ka Pahad hai aur "Atham - اثام" Pahad ke gird Tanbe ki behne wali garm tareen Waadi hai aur wo Dozakh ka sakht tareen Azaab hai."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️ 🔥

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"3 baatein Jahannamiyo'n ki sifaat (characteristics) hain: Takabbur, Khud-pasandi (self admiration) aur bad-Akhlaaqi."

(Meezanul Hikmah, v2, p273)

🤲🏻

Ziyarat ke akhir mein Dua:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"Mere Allah! Tu ne mujh par jo farawan Ne'maten nazil farmayi hain Tu hi mujhe unke bare mein Shukro sipaas ki Taufeeq ata farma aur iske natije mein mujh par Ehsaan o Karam mein izaafa farma."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

   12th October 2021, Tuesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦️ JAHANNAM KE TABAQAAT ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1783)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَإِنَّ جَهَنَّمَ لَمَوۡعِدُهُمۡ أَجۡمَعِینَ * لَهَا سَبۡعَةُ أَبۡوَ ٰ⁠بࣲ لِّكُلِّ بَابࣲ مِّنۡهُمۡ جُزۡءࣱ مَّقۡسُومٌ.

"Yaqeenan in sab ke liya Dozakh hi Wadagah hai. Uske Saat Darwaze honge, har Darwaze ke liye ek khaas hissa muqarrar kar diya gaya hai."_

(Surah Al-Hijr: 43 - 44)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖 🚪🔥

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd....)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🚪 🔥

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Dozakh ke 7 Darwaze honge. Ek Darwaze se Firaun, Hamaan aur Qaroon guzrenge. Ek Darwaze se woh Kuffar o Mushrekin guzrenge jo Chashme zadan ke liye bhi Allah par Imaan na laaye honge. Ek Darwaze se Bani Umayyah guzrenge. Woh Darwaza unke liye makhsoos hoga aur woh 'Bab e Laza - باب لظیٰ, Bab e Saqar - باب سقر, Bab e Haviya - باب ھاویة, hai. 70 Kharif tak woh is mein girte jayenge aur jab woh Pataal tak pahunchenge to unhe phir neeche dhakel diya jayega. Is tarah se woh hamesha Azaab mein rahenge."

"Ek Darwaze se hamse Bughz rakhne wale, hamse Jang karne wale aur hamari Nusrat se kinaara kashi karne wale dakhil honge aur ye sakht Garam Darwaza hoga."

(Noorus Saqlain)

🚪🔥

Raavi ne sawal kiya, Maula! Jis Darwaze ke mutalliq Aap (as) ne bayan kiya ke wo Bani Umayyah ke liye makhsoos hai. Kya Bani Umayyah ke Zamana e Jahiliyyat ke afraad dakhil honge jinhone Islam ko paya tha?

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Tere Maa mare! Kuffar o Mushrekin ke liye to alaihda Darwaza hai. Is mein tamam Kuffar o Mushrekin dakhil honge. Ye Darwaza Bani Umayyah ke liye makhsoos hai. Is mein sare fehrist woh dakhil hoga jisne Rasoole Khuda (saww) se kayi Jange ki thi aur uski Aulaad hogi aur Aale Marwaan dakhil hogi. Jab woh us Darwaze se dakhil honge to Dozakh ka Azaab unhe chakna choor kar dega. Wahan unki cheekhen sunnewala koi na hoga. Wahan pahunch kar na to woh zinda rahenge aur na marenge."

(Noorus Saqlain)

(The End of Topic)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️ 🤲🏻

Imam Ali (as):

"(Ilaahi!) Maine Teri Ibaadat, na Tere Jahannam ke khauf se ki hai aur na Teri Jannat ki laalach mein, balke maine Tujhe Ibaadat ke laayak paaya is liye Teri ibadaat ki."

(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Ibadat)

🤲🏻

Ziyarat ke akhir mein Dua:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"......(Bare Ilaha!) Logon ke darmiyan mere Qaul mein taseer ata kar, mere Amal ko Apni Bargah mein bulandi ata farma, mujhe aisa bana de ke meri Nekiyon ki pairavi ki jaane lage, aur mere Dushman ko tabah o barbad kar de..... "

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

             ♦️ MUTTAQEEN ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1784)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

إِنَّ ٱلۡمُتَّقِینَ فِی جَنَّـٰتࣲ وَعُیُونٍ * ٱدۡخُلُوهَا بِسَلَـٰمٍ ءَامِنِینَ.

"Beshak, Parhezgar Baghaat aur Chashmo (well) ke darmiyan honge. Unhe Hukm hoga ke tum in Baghaat mein Salamti aur Amn ke saath dakhil ho jao."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 45 - 46)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖 🚪

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd....)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🚪🚪🌱🌿🪴

Khurba Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):

"Logo! Taqwa ki Sawariyan Ram Sawariyan hain jin par Ahle Taqwa sawar hain aur unki baagen unke haathon mein hain, woh unhe le kar Jannat mein dakhil hogi aur Jannat ke Darwaze un par khol diye jayenge aur woh Jannat ki Khushbu payenge aur unse kaha jayega ke tum Salamti aur Amn ke saath Baghaat mein dakhil ho jao."

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🚪🚪🌱🌿

AanHazrat (saww) ne Hazrat Ali (as) aur unki Aulaad ka Tazkara karte hue Farmaya:

"Unke chahne wale Amn ke saath Jannat mein dakhil honge aur Farishte un par Salam kar ke kahenge ke tum Paak ho, ab hamesha ke liye Jannat mein chale jao"

(Ehtejaaj e Tabarsi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️ 👋🏻

Hazrat Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):

"Logo! Na Ghussa karo aur na kisi ko Ghussa dilao. Aapas mein *Salaam* ko rawaj do aur achhi guftugu karo aur jab Raat ke waqt log soye hue hon to tum Namaz padho, iske ewaz tum Salamti ke saath Jannat mein dakhil ho sakoge."

Phir Aap (as) ne ye Ayat ki tilawat ki  ٱلسَّلَـٰمُ ٱلۡمُؤۡمِنُ ٱلۡمُهَیۡمِنُ (Al-Hashr: 23)

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

Is riwayat mein Imam Ali (as) ne 'Salaam' karne ki takeed ki hai, 'Salamun Alaikum' se greet karna chahiye. Maulai Hazrat jo doosre fiqre istemal karte hain, wo apni taraf se hai jiski koi riwayat nahi hai, jabke ghalat bhi nahi. Lekin hame wohi alfaaz ka istemal karna chahiye jiski Imam (as) ne takeed ki hai, aur isi mein Sawab bhi hai.

🤲🏻

Ziyarat ke akhir mein Dua:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"..... Aye Jahano ke Palanhaar! Tu Apne Behtareen Bandon yani Muhammad (saww) aur Aale Muhammad (as) par Shabo Roz Apni Rehmaten aur Darood nazil farma, aur mujhe buron ke shar se mehfooz kar de, Gunahon se paak farma de. Mere bojh utar de. Mujhe Sukoon o qaraar ki jagah yani Jannat mein jagah de......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

♦️AHLE JANNAT KI KHUSOOSIYAT ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1786)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَنَزَعۡنَا مَا فِی صُدُورِهِم مِّنۡ غِلٍّ إِخۡوَ ٰ⁠نًا عَلَىٰ سُرُرࣲ مُّتَقَـٰبِلِینَ * لَا یَمَسُّهُمۡ فِیهَا نَصَبࣱ وَمَا هُم مِّنۡهَا بِمُخۡرَجِینَ * نَبِّئۡ عِبَادِیۤ أَنِّیۤ أَنَا ٱلۡغَفُورُ ٱلرَّحِیمُ * وَأَنَّ عَذَابِی هُوَ ٱلۡعَذَابُ ٱلۡأَلِیمُ.

"Aur Hamne unke Seeno se har tarah ki Kadoorat (Ranjish, Keena) nikal li hai. Woh Bhaiyyon ki tarah aamne saame Takht par baithe honge. Unhe wahan kisi mashaqqat se wasta nahi padega aur woh un Baghaat se nahi nikale jayenge. Mere Bandon ko Khabar do ke Mein Bada Bakhshne Wala, Meherban hun. Aur Yaqeenan Mera Azaab bhi Nihayat Dardnaak Azaab hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 47 - 50)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖 🚪

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🚪🚪🌱🌿🪴

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Qayamat ke Din jab hamare Shiyon ko Jannat mein bheja jayega to unke Dilon mein agar ek doosre ke khilaf Kadoorat hogi to woh nikal li jayegi aur woh Bhaiyyon ki tarah se ek doosre ke aamne saamne Takht par baithe honge."

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

👋🏻

Imam Sadiq (as) to Abu Baseer:

"Aye Abu Mohd! Khuda ne tumhe apni Kitab mein yaad kiya hai aur tumhare mutalliq farmaya hai إِخۡوَ ٰ⁠نًا عَلَىٰ سُرُرࣲ مُّتَقَـٰبِلِینَ Is Ayat (15:47) ka ruye sukhan tumhare alawa aur kisi ki taraf nahi hai."

(Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️ 🚪🌿🌱🪴

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Tum mein se har Mard o Zan par Farishte Salam karte hain aur tum hi woh log ho jinke mutalliq Khuda ne is Ayat (15:47) mein Farmaya."

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🚪🪴🌿

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Momin ka Keena (bair) jhagde ki jagah tak mehdood hota hai yaani jab tak wo apne biraadar e Momin se alag ho kar us jagah se hat'ta hai to Dil se uska Keena bhi jaata rehta hai magar Kaafir ki taraf se Keena umr bhar rehta hai."

(Tehzeeb ul Islam, p346)

🤲🏻

Ziyarat ke akhir mein Dua:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".......Nez mujhe aur Mo'meneen o Mo'menaat mein se mere tamam Bhaiyyon aur Behnon, Aizza o Aqroba ko bakhsh de. Aye sab Rahem karnewalon se zyada Rahem karne wale Apni Rehmat ki Tasdeeq, meri ilteja ko qabool farma le."

(The End of Ziyarat)

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

        *8th Rabiul Awwal 1443*

      *15th October 2021, Friday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦️ HAZRAT IBRAHIM (as) ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1787)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَنَبِّئۡهُمۡ عَن ضَیۡفِ إِبۡرَ ٰ⁠هِیمَ * إِذۡ دَخَلُوا۟ عَلَیۡهِ فَقَالُوا۟ سَلَـٰمࣰا قَالَ إِنَّا مِنكُمۡ وَجِلُونَ * قَالُوا۟ لَا تَوۡجَلۡ إِنَّا نُبَشِّرُكَ بِغُلَـٰمٍ عَلِیمࣲ * قَالَ أَبَشَّرۡتُمُونِی عَلَىٰۤ أَن مَّسَّنِیَ ٱلۡكِبَرُ فَبِمَ تُبَشِّرُونَ * قَالُوا۟ بَشَّرۡنَـٰكَ بِٱلۡحَقِّ فَلَا تَكُن مِّنَ ٱلۡقَـٰنِطِینَ.*

"Aur Aap (saww) unhe Ibrahim (as) ke Mehmaano ke mutalliq Khabar den. Jab woh aaye to kaha: 'Salam ho tum par.' Usne kaha: 'Ham tum se khaufzada hain.' Unhone kha ke: 'Mat daren ham Aapko Sahib e Ilm ki Basharat dete hain.' Usne kaha: 'Ab jabke mujh par Budhapa chha gaya hai tum mujhe kis baat ki Basharat dete ho?' Unhone kaha ke: 'Ham tumhe Sahih Basharat de rahe hain.'

(Surah Al-Hijr: 51 - 55)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖 🚪

👉 Tafseer:  

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ki Zauja Saara ne Aap (as) se arz kiya ke ab ham boodhe ho chuke hain, magar Aulaad se mehroom hain. Aap (as) Khuda ke Khaleel hain aur Khuda Aapki Dua qubool karta hai. Aap (as) Khuda se Dua maange ke Woh hame ek Farzand ata kare, taake hamari Aankhen ko thandak naseeb ho."

"Ibrahim (as) ne Khuda ki Bargah mein Sahib e Ilm Farzand ke liye Dua ki. Allah Ta'ala ne unki taraf Wahy Farmayi ke Mein tujhe Sahib e Ilm Farzand ata karunga aur phir teri Ita'at ka Imtihan lunga. Iske baad 3 Baras mazeed guzar gaye, phir 3 Saal ke baad Allah ne Ibrahim (as) ko Ismael (as) ki dubara Basharat di."

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️

Riwayat:

Pehle jisne Qaatil e Husain ibne Ali (as) par La'anat ki Hazrat Ibrahim Khaleelullah (as) the aur unhone hukm kiya apne Farzandon ko aur unse Ahd o Paimaan (promise) liya ki hamesha is Mal'oon par La'anat karein. Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke baad Hazrat Musa (as) ne uspar La'anat ki aur apni ummat ko hukm kiya ke La'anat karein. Unke baad Hazrat Dawood (as) ne La'nat ki aur Bani Israel ko hukm kiya ke us shaqi par La'anat karein. Unke baad Hazrat Esa (as) ne us par La'anat ki…."

(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v1, p133)

🤲🏻

*السَّلامُ عَلٰى إِبْرَاهِيْمَ الَّذي حَبَاهُ اللهُ بِخُلَّتِهِ، السَّلامُ عَلٰى إِسْمَاعِيْلَ الَّذي فَدَاهُ اللهُ بِذِبْحٍ عَظِيْمٍ مِنَ جَنَّتِهِ*

"Salam ho Ibrahim (as) par jinko Allah ne Apni Khullat se Sarfraz kiya, Salam ho Ismael par jinko Allah ne Zibhe Azeem ko Qarardad ke saath Apni Jannat se Fidya bheja."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

        11th Rabiul Awwal 1443

     18th October 2021, Monday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦️ HAZRAT IBRAHIM (as) ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1788)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَنَبِّئۡهُمۡ عَن ضَیۡفِ إِبۡرَ ٰ⁠هِیمَ * إِذۡ دَخَلُوا۟ عَلَیۡهِ فَقَالُوا۟ سَلَـٰمࣰا قَالَ إِنَّا مِنكُمۡ وَجِلُونَ * قَالُوا۟ لَا تَوۡجَلۡ إِنَّا نُبَشِّرُكَ بِغُلَـٰمٍ عَلِیمࣲ * قَالَ أَبَشَّرۡتُمُونِی عَلَىٰۤ أَن مَّسَّنِیَ ٱلۡكِبَرُ فَبِمَ تُبَشِّرُونَ * قَالُوا۟ بَشَّرۡنَـٰكَ بِٱلۡحَقِّ فَلَا تَكُن مِّنَ ٱلۡقَـٰنِطِینَ.

"Aur Aap (saww) unhe Ibrahim (as) ke Mehmaano ke mutalliq Khabar den. Jab woh aaye to kaha: 'Salam ho tum par.' Usne kaha: 'Ham tum se khaufzada hain.' Unhone kha ke: 'Mat daren ham Aapko Sahib e Ilm ki Basharat dete hain.' Usne kaha: 'Ab jabke mujh par Budhapa chha gaya hai tum mujhe kis baat ki Basharat dete ho?' Unhone kaha ke: 'Ham tumhe Sahih Basharat de rahe hain.'

(Surah Al-Hijr: 51 - 55)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Hazrat Imam Baqir (as):

"Hazrat Lut (as) aur Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ko Qaum e Lut par Azaab ki tawaqqo nahi thi aur dono Anbiya ko Khuda ki Bargah mein bada maqam hasil tha. Chunanche ek arse tak Allah Ta'ala ne in dono Anbiya ki wajah se Azaab ko mo'akhkhar (delay) rakha.

Phir jab Qaum e Lut ki Sarkashi urooj ko pahunchi aur Allah ne un par Azaab nazil karne ka iraada kiya to Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ka gham kam karne ke liye unhe Sahib e Ilm Farzand ki Basharat di.

Chunanche Allah ne Apne Farishte Ibrahim (as) ke paas Basharat le kar bheje. Farishte Raat ke waqt Ibrahim (as) ke paas aaye. Ibrahim (as) unhe dekh kar ghabra gaye aur Aapko ye khatra mehsoos hua ke ye kahin chor uchakke na hon."

"Jab Farishton ne Aapki Parishani ko dekha to unhone Aap (as) ko Salaam kiya. Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne farmaya ke ham tumse khaufzada hain. Farishte kehne lage ke Aap (as) mat ghabrayen, ham Aap (as) ko  Sahib e Ilm Farzand ki Basharat dete hain."

Imam Baqir (as):

"Ghulam e Alim غلام علیم" se Hazrat Ismael (as) murad hain."

"Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne Farishton se kaha: 'Ab to mujh par budhapa taari ho gaya hai. Is Umr mein tum mujhe kis tarah ki Khush Khabri de rahe ho?'

Farishton ne kaha: 'Hamne Aap (as) ko Sachchi Basharat di hai. Aap (as) mayoos hone walon mein se na banen.'

(Noorus Saqlain)

(Riwayat to be Cont'd.....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️

Imam Sadiq (as)

Allah ne H. Ibrahim (as) ko Nabi banane se pehle apna Abd (Banda) banaya aur unhe Rasool banane se pehle apna Nabi banaya aur Khaleel banane se pehle unhe Rasool banaya aur unhe Imam banane se pehle apna Khaleel banaya.

(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v2, p508)

🤲🏻

یَا اِلٰهِىْ وَاِلٰهَ اٰبَاۤئِىْۤ اِبْرَاهِیْمَ وَاِسْمَاعِیْلَ وَاِسْحٰقَ وَیَعْقُوْبَ وَرَبَّ جَبْرَئِیْلَ وَمِیْكَاۤئِیْلَ وَاِسْرَافِیْلَ وَرَبَّ مُحَمَّدٍ خَاتَمِ النَّبِیِّیْنَ

(Dua e Arafa Imam Husain (as) - Mafaatih

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦️ MAYOOSI - HOPELESSNESS ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1789)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالُوا۟ بَشَّرۡنَـٰكَ بِٱلۡحَقِّ فَلَا تَكُن مِّنَ ٱلۡقَـٰنِطِینَ * قَالَ وَمَن یَقۡنَطُ مِن رَّحۡمَةِ رَبِّهِۦۤ إِلَّا ٱلضَّاۤلُّونَ.

"Unhone kaha ke ham tumhe Sahih Basharat de rahe hain, tum Mayoos na hon. Usne kaha ke Khuda ki Rehmat se to Gumrah afraad ke alawa bhala kaun mayoos ho sakta hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 55 - 56)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafsir:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🕌

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Allah Ta'ala Insaan se kehta hai: 'Aye Farzande Adam! Mere hi Ehsaan ki wajah se tu Meri Ita'at ke qaabil hua hai aur apni Badgumani ki wajah se tu Meri Rehmat se mayoos hua hai."

(Kitabut Tauheed, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Ali (as):

"Sahi maani mein Aqlmand wo hota hai jo logo'n ko Khuda ki Rehmat se na to mayoos kare aur na unhe Allah ki Sazaao'n se bilkul be-khauf aur mutmaeen kar de."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, Intekhaab o Takhlees, v3, p189)

🙏🏻

Imam Ali (as):

"Mujhe us shakhs par tajjub hai jo Khuda ki di hui Astagfaar ki gunjaaish ke bawajood mayoos ho jaata hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, Intekhaab o Takhlees, v3, p188)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️

Allah Ta'ala:

"Balaa o Musibat se maayus mat ho; Jaise Sona aag mein pighla kar parkha jaata hai waise Momin balaa'on mein parkha jaata hai."

(Al-Hadith Al-Qudsi - ABISN, Nairobi, Kenya)

🕌

Imam Ali (as):

"Mukammal Aalim e Deen wohi hai jo logo'n ko Rehmat e Khuda se mayoos na banaye aur Uski Meherbaniyo'n se na-ummeed na kare aur Uske Azaab se bilkul mutmaeen na kar de."

(The perfect jurist of Islam is whoever does not let people lose hope from the mercy of Allah, does not make him despondent of Allah’s kindness and does not make him feel safe from Allah’s punishment.)

(Nahjul Balagah, p659)

🤲🏻

Imam Jafar Sadiq (as) ne Namaz ke baad ye Dua maangi:

"Parwardigar! Mujhe Apni Rehmat se mayoos na hone dena."

Phir Aap (as) ne ye Ayat ki tilawat farmayi: (15:56)

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦️ AZAAB LANE WAALE FARISHTE ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1790)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالَ فَمَا خَطۡبُكُمۡ أَیُّهَا ٱلۡمُرۡسَلُونَ * قَالُوۤا۟ إِنَّاۤ أُرۡسِلۡنَاۤ إِلَىٰ قَوۡمࣲ مُّجۡرِمِینَ * إِلَّاۤ ءَالَ لُوطٍ إِنَّا لَمُنَجُّوهُمۡ أَجۡمَعِینَ * إِلَّا ٱمۡرَأَتَهُۥ قَدَّرۡنَاۤ إِنَّهَا لَمِنَ ٱلۡغَـٰبِرِینَ

"Phir usne (Ibrahim (as) ne poochha: 'Aye Farastadgane Ilahi (Messengers)! 'Tum kis muhim par rawana kiye gaye ho?' Unhone kaha ke: 'hame Mujrim Qaum ki taraf bheja gaya hai. Sirf Lut (as) ke gharwale mustasna (exception) hain, Ham un sab ko bacha lenge albatta uski Biwi ko nahi bachayenge, uske mutalliq hamne tay kar liya hai ke woh peechhe reh jaane walon mein shamil rahegi."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 57 - 60)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:  

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🕌

Hazrat Imam Baqir (as):

"Phir jab Qaum e Lut ki Sarkashi urooj ko pahunchi"

"Iske baad Aap (as) ne farmaya: 'Tumhe kis maqsad ke khatir bheja gaya hai?'

Malaika ne kaha: 'Hame Mujrim Qaum ki taraf bheja gaya hai.'

"Jab Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne ye khabar suni to Aap (as) ne farmaya: 'Wahan to Lut (as) bhi rehta hai, kya woh to halaak nahi ho jayega?'

Farishton ne kaha: 'Ham wahan par tamam rehne walon ko achchi tarah jaante hain. Ham Lut (as) aur uske Khaandan ko bacha lenge, magar uski Biwi Khuda ke Azaab se na bach sakegi, woh peechhe reh jaane walon mein shamil rahegi."

"Phir theek Aathwe (8th) Din Tulu' e Fajr ke waqt Allah ne Ibrahim (as) ke paas Farishte bheje jinhone Aap (as) ko Ishaaq (as) ki Basharat di aur Qaum e Lut ki halakat par tasalli di."

(Noorus Saqlain)

(Ye Waqea Surah Hud ki Tafseer mein tafaeel se bayan ho chuka hai.)

(Noorus Saqlain)

(Ye Waqea Surah Hud ki Tafseer mein tafaeel se bayan ho chuka hai last year isi Mahine mein.)

(Riwayat to be Cont'd.....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️

Imam Ali (as)

ke paas ek mujrim ko laaya gaya, jiske saath tamashayio'n ka hujoom tha. To aap (as) ne farmaya, "In Chehro'n par phithkaar ho, jo sirf burayi aur ruswayi ke mauqe par nazar aate hain."

(Imam Ali ibn Abu Talib (as) said the following when a criminal was brought to him escorted by mobs: There is no welcome for you here, O faces that are not seen except when a bad deed is committed.)

(Nahjul Balagah, p701)

🤲🏻

..... وَ هَب لِىْ جُرْمِيْ فِيْهِ يَا اِلـٰهَ الْعَالَمِيْنَ، وَاعْفُ عَنِّي يَا عَافِيًا عَنِ الْمُجْرِمِيْنَ۔

"Aur hamare Gunahon ko Bakhsh de, Aye Aalamin ke Malik, hame Ma'af farma de, Aye tamam Mujrimon ko Ma'af karnewala."

(Maahe Ramazan ke Dino ki Dua - Mafateeh)

      🌹 HAFTA-E-BARA'AT 🌹

🍁 MARG-E-YAZEED MUBARAK 🍁

**********************************

        14th Rabiul Awwal 1443

    21st October 2021, Thursday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

          ♦️ AZAAB-E-ILAHI ♦️

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1791)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَمَّا جَاۤءَ ءَالَ لُوطٍ ٱلۡمُرۡسَلُونَ * قَالَ إِنَّكُمۡ قَوۡمࣱ مُّنكَرُونَ * قَالُوا۟ بَلۡ جِئۡنَـٰكَ بِمَا كَانُوا۟ فِیهِ یَمۡتَرُونَ * وَأَتَیۡنَـٰكَ بِٱلۡحَقِّ وَإِنَّا لَصَـٰدِقُونَ.

"Pas ye Farastade (Messengers) Aale Lut (as) ke paas pahunche. Unhone kaha 'tum ajnabi log dikhayi dete ho.' Farishton ne kaha ke 'ham wo Azaab le kar aayen hain jis mein woh shak kiya karte the. Ham sach much Azaab laye hain aur ham bilkul sachche hain."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 61 - 64)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🕌

Hazrat Imam Baqir (as):

"Phir woh Farishte Hazrat Lut (as) ke paas aaye. Hazrat Lut (as) ne unhe dekh kar unse kaha: 'Tum ajnabi log mehsoos hote ho.'

Farishton ne kaha: 'Ham Aap(as) ke paas wo Azaab le kar aaye hain jiske mutalliq Aapki Qaum shak kar rahi hai. Aaj se poore saat Din guzarne ke baad Aap (as) Raat ke waqt yahan se nikal paden aur jab yahan se niklen to tum mein se koi mud kar peechhe na dekhe. Aapke Khaandan ko Najaat di jayegi. Albatta Aapki Biwi par Khuda ka Azaab nazil hoga."

(Noorus Saqlain)

(Ye Waqea Surah Hud ki Tafseer mein tafaeel se bayan ho chuka hai last year isi Mahine mein.)

(Riwayat to be Cont'd.....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇‍♂️

Imam Ali (as):

"Jiska Akhlaq bura hota hai wo khud ko Azaab mein daalta hai."

(Ghurar al-Hikam, v1, p423)

😱

Imam Ali (as):

"Khuda ke Azaab se darna Muttaqeen aur Parhezgaro'n ki aadat hai."

(Ghurar al-Hikam, v1, p429)

😨

Imam Ali (as):

"Aisi Aag (Jahannum) se bacho jiski cheekh o pukaar sakht hogi, jikse sholay (flames) shadeed (extreme) honge aur jiska Azaab hamesha naya hoga."

(Ghurar al-Hikam, Meezan ul Hikmah, v2)

🤲🏻

Imam Ali (as):

"Aye mere Ma'bood aur mere Sardar aur mere Maula aur mere Parwardigar! Maan le ke main Tere Azaab par Sabr bhi kar lun, magar Teri Rehmat se judaai par kyun kar Sabr karunga? Aur maan le ke main Teri Aag ki haraarat seh lunga, magar Teri Nazar e Karamat ke badal jaane ko kyun kar bardaasht karunga? Ya aatish e Jahannum mein kyun kar qaraar paaunga, jabke Teri Ma'afi ki ummeed lagi hui hai?"

(Dua e Kumail)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

**********************************

        *18th Rabiul Awwal 1443*

    *25th October 2021, Monday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦ QAUM-E-LUT (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1793)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَلَمَّا جَاۤءَ ءَالَ لُوطٍ ٱلۡمُرۡسَلُونَ * قَالَ إِنَّكُمۡ قَوۡمࣱ مُّنكَرُونَ * قَالُوا۟ بَلۡ جِئۡنَـٰكَ بِمَا كَانُوا۟ فِیهِ یَمۡتَرُونَ * وَأَتَیۡنَـٰكَ بِٱلۡحَقِّ وَإِنَّا لَصَـٰدِقُونَ.*

"Pas ye Farastade (Messengers) Aale Lut (as) ke paas pahunche. Unhone kaha 'tum ajnabi log dikhayi dete ho.' Farishton ne kaha ke 'ham wo Azaab le kar aayen hain jis mein woh shak kiya karte the. Ham sach much Azaab laye hain aur ham bilkul sachche hain."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 61 - 64)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

----------------------------------------------

🕌

Last year is Ayat ki Tafseer pesh ki thi, phir repeat kar rahe hain:

*وَجَاۤءَهُۥ قَوۡمُهُۥ یُهۡرَعُونَ إِلَیۡهِ وَمِن قَبۡلُ كَانُوا۟ یَعۡمَلُونَ ٱلسَّیِّـَٔاتِۚ قَالَ یَـٰقَوۡمِ هَـٰۤؤُلَاۤءِ بَنَاتِی هُنَّ أَطۡهَرُ لَكُمۡۖ فَٱتَّقُوا۟ ٱللَّهَ وَلَا تُخۡزُونِ فِی ضَیۡفِیۤۖ أَلَیۡسَ مِنكُمۡ رَجُلࣱ رَّشِیدࣱ. * قَالُوا۟ لَقَدۡ عَلِمۡتَ مَا لَنَا فِی بَنَاتِكَ مِنۡ حَقࣲّ وَإِنَّكَ لَتَعۡلَمُ مَا نُرِیدُ * قَالَ لَوۡ أَنَّ لِی بِكُمۡ قُوَّةً أَوۡ ءَاوِیۤ إِلَىٰ رُكۡنࣲ شَدِیدࣲ.*

"Jaise hi Woh (Farishte) aaye to Lut (as) ki Qaum ke log daudte hue unke paas aaye aur isse pehle woh Badkariyan kiya karte the. Lut (as) ne kaha: "Aye meri Qaum! Ye meri Betiyan (Tumhari Biwiyan) maujood hain. Ye tumhare liye zyada Pakeeza hain. Tum Allah se Daro aur Mehmano ke mutalliq ruswa na karo. Kya tumhara andar koi basha'oor shakhs maujood nahi hai?"

"Woh kehne lage ke tu jaanta hai ke tumhari Betiyon se hamara koi talluq nahi hai aur ham jo kuchh chahte hain usse mutalliq tumhe bakhoobi ilm hai. Lut (as) ne kaha: Aye Kaash! Meri paas tumhare muqabile ke liye Quwwat maujood hoti ya mein kisi mazboot Sahare ki panah le sakta."

(Surah Hud: 77 - 80)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Qaum e Lut (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Imam Baqir (as): (Cont'd)

"Hazrat Lut (as) ne logon ko is Bad-Fe'li se mana kiya lekin Hazrat (as) ki Nasihat ka un par koi asar na hua. Jab unki Behayai had se badhi to Allah ne un par Azaab bhejne ka faisla kiya. Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Jibrael (as), Mikael aur Israfeel ko khoobsurat ladko ki shakl mein wahan rawana kiya. Teeno Farishte Hazrat Lut (as) ke paas aaye. Us waqt Aap (as) kheton mein kam kaj kar rahe the. Aap (as) ne unse kaha: 'Tum log kahan ja rahe ho, meine apni zindagi mein tum se zyada haseen afraad nahi dekhe?' Unhone kaha ke hamare Aaqa ne hame is shaher ke Sardar ke paas bheja hai.

Hazrat Lut (as) ne kaha: "Kya tumhare Aaqa ko ye Ilm nahi hai ke is Shaher ke log naujawan ladkon se kya sulook karte hain? Suno! Ye bade kamine log hain. Ye Mardon ko pakad kar Jinsi (Sex) taskeen hasil karte hain, yahan tak ke dubur (Anus) se Khoon nikal aata hai."

Farishton ne kaha: "Hamare Aaqa ne hamko Hidayat di hai ke ham Shaher ke Markaz (Centre) mein jayen."

Hazrat ne Farmaya:

"Phir tum meri baat maano, tum abhi yahan mere paas thehre raho, yahan tak ke tareeki chha jaye." Aap (as) ki ye baat sun kar woh Aap (as) ke paas baith gaye. Itne mein Aap (as) ki beti Aap (as) ke paas aayi. Aap (as) ne beti se farmaya: "Mehmanon ke liye khaana aur Paani lao aur sardi se mehfooz rehne ke liye kuchh chaadaren bhi yahan le aao. Hazrat (as) ki beti ghar gayi ke tez Baarish aa gayi aur waadiyan behne lagin. Hazrat Lut (as) ne ladko ko saath liya aur farmaya: "Ab meri bachchi khaana nahi la sakegi, lehaza tum mere saath mere ghar tak chalo, wahan mein tumhari Ziyafat karunga."

Hazrat Lut (as) Diwaar ke saaye mein chalne lage, jabke teeno Mehmaan raaste beech mein chalne lage. Hazrat (as) ne farmaya: "Bachcho! Darmiyan mein na chalo. Diwaar ke saath saath tareeki hai tum mere saath tareeki mein chalo. Mehmamo ne kaha: "Hamen hamare Aaqa ne Nasihat ki thi ke ham raaste ke beech mein chalen."

Hazrat Lut (as) ne Tareeki e Shab ko ghanimat jana. Aap (as) unhe saath le kar apne ghar le aaye. Aap (as) ke Darwaze ke paas ek Kuwan tha jahan se log Paani bhara karte the. Ittifaq se us waqt ek Aurat apne bachche ko uthaye hue Paani bharne ke liye wahan aayi. Iblees ne uske Bachche ko Kuwen mein dhakka diya. Aurat cheekhne lagi. Log uski madad ke liye wahan aaye. Jab woh wahan aaye to unhone Hazrat Lut (as) ke ghar 3 khubsurat ladkon ko baithe hue dekha. Jab unhone khubsurat ladke dekhe to unki ral tapakne lagi aur unhone Aap (as) se kaha: "Aap (as) hame to mana karte the, lekin Aap (as) khud hamare kaamo mein shamil hain."

Aap (as) ne farmaya: "Ye log mere Mehman hain aur Mehmano ke mutalliq mujhe ruswa na karo."

Un logon ne kaha: "Achha ham Aap (as) se musalehat kar lete hain. Aap (as) ke 3 ladke thehre hue hain, un mein se ek ladke ko apne paas rakho aur do ladke hamare sipurd kardo."

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hazrat Lut (as) ne *ان لى بكم قوة او آوى الى ركن شديد* keh kar do cheezon ki khwahish ki thi: Unhone Badkaar Qaum ke muqabile mein Quwwat aur Mazboot Sahare ki khwahish ki thi. Qaem Aale Muhammad (atfs) jab Zahoor karenge to unhe dono cheezen hasil hongi. Khuda unhe bemisaal Quwwat ata karega aur Sahare ke liye aise saathi ata karega jinke Dil Faulad se bhi zyada Mazboot honge. Woh Lohe ke Pahad ko bhi kaatne ki quwwat rakhte honge aur us waqt tak Shasheerzani karte rahenge jab tak Khuda Raazi na ho jayega."

(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

*یَا رُكْنَ مَنْ لَا رُكْنَ لَهٗ یَا غِیَاثَا مَنْ لَاغِیَاثَ لَهٗ........*

(Dua-e-Joshane Kabir)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

        *19th Rabiul Awwal 1443*

   *26th October 2021, Tuesday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦ QAUM-E-LUT (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1794)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَأَسۡرِ بِأَهۡلِكَ بِقِطۡعࣲ مِّنَ ٱلَّیۡلِ وَٱتَّبِعۡ أَدۡبَـٰرَهُمۡ وَلَا یَلۡتَفِتۡ مِنكُمۡ أَحَدࣱ وَٱمۡضُوا۟ حَیۡثُ تُؤۡمَرُونَ * وَقَضَیۡنَاۤ إِلَیۡهِ ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ ٱلۡأَمۡرَ أَنَّ دَابِرَ هَـٰۤؤُلَاۤءِ مَقۡطُوعࣱ مُّصۡبِحِینَ * وَجَاۤءَ أَهۡلُ ٱلۡمَدِینَةِ یَسۡتَبۡشِرُونَ * قَالَ إِنَّ هَـٰۤؤُلَاۤءِ ضَیۡفِی فَلَا تَفۡضَحُونِ * وَٱتَّقُوا۟ ٱللَّهَ وَلَا تُخۡزُونِ*

"Aap Raat rahe, apne Gharwalon ko le kar yahan se nikal jayen aur khud unke peechhe peechhe chalo aur tum mein se koi palat kar na dekhe aur jidhar jaane ka tumhe Hukm diya ja raha hai us simt mein seedhe chale jao aur hamne us tak ye faisla pahuncha diya ke Subah hote hote unki jad kaat di jayegi."

"Shaher ke log khushiyan manate hue aa gaye. Lut (as) ne kaha: 'Ye mere Mehmaan hain, mujhe Badnaam na karo aur tum Khuda se daro aur mujhe ruswa na karo.'"

(Surah Al-Hijr: 65 - 69)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

----------------------------------------------

🕌

Last year is Ayat ki Tafseer pesh ki thi, phir repeat kar rahe hain:

*وَجَاۤءَهُۥ قَوۡمُهُۥ یُهۡرَعُونَ إِلَیۡهِ وَمِن قَبۡلُ كَانُوا۟ یَعۡمَلُونَ ٱلسَّیِّـَٔاتِۚ قَالَ یَـٰقَوۡمِ هَـٰۤؤُلَاۤءِ بَنَاتِی هُنَّ أَطۡهَرُ لَكُمۡۖ فَٱتَّقُوا۟ ٱللَّهَ وَلَا تُخۡزُونِ فِی ضَیۡفِیۤۖ أَلَیۡسَ مِنكُمۡ رَجُلࣱ رَّشِیدࣱ. * قَالُوا۟ لَقَدۡ عَلِمۡتَ مَا لَنَا فِی بَنَاتِكَ مِنۡ حَقࣲّ وَإِنَّكَ لَتَعۡلَمُ مَا نُرِیدُ * قَالَ لَوۡ أَنَّ لِی بِكُمۡ قُوَّةً أَوۡ ءَاوِیۤ إِلَىٰ رُكۡنࣲ شَدِیدࣲ.*

"Jaise hi Woh (Farishte) aaye to Lut (as) ki Qaum ke log daudte hue unke paas aaye aur isse pehle woh Badkariyan kiya karte the. Lut (as) ne kaha: "Aye meri Qaum! Ye meri Betiyan (Tumhari Biwiyan) maujood hain. Ye tumhare liye zyada Pakeeza hain. Tum Allah se Daro aur Mehmano ke mutalliq ruswa na karo. Kya tumhara andar koi basha'oor shakhs maujood nahi hai?"_

"Woh kehne lage ke tu jaanta hai ke tumhari Betiyon se hamara koi talluq nahi hai aur ham jo kuchh chahte hain usse mutalliq tumhe bakhoobi ilm hai. Lut (as) ne kaha: Aye Kaash! Meri paas tumhare muqabile ke liye Quwwat maujood hoti ya mein kisi mazboot Sahare ki panah le sakta."

(Surah Hud: 77 - 80)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Qaum e Lut (as) jaari hai:

🕌

*قَالُوا۟ یَـٰلُوطُ إِنَّا رُسُلُ رَبِّكَ لَن یَصِلُوۤا۟ إِلَیۡكَۖ فَأَسۡرِ بِأَهۡلِكَ بِقِطۡعࣲ مِّنَ ٱلَّیۡلِ وَلَا یَلۡتَفِتۡ مِنكُمۡ أَحَدٌ إِلَّا ٱمۡرَأَتَكَۖ إِنَّهُۥ مُصِیبُهَا مَاۤ أَصَابَهُمۡۚ إِنَّ مَوۡعِدَهُمُ ٱلصُّبۡحُۚ أَلَیۡسَ ٱلصُّبۡحُ بِقَرِیبࣲ.*

"Unhone (Farishton) kaha: Aye Lut! Ham tere Rab ke Numainde hain. Ye log tumhara kuchh na bigad sakenge. Raat ke andar hi apne Khandan ko le kar nikal jao aur tum mein se koi peechhe palat kar na dekhe, siwai teri Biwi ke. Us par bhi wohi Azaab aanewala hai jo un par aanewala hai. Unke Azaab ke liye Subah ka waqt muqarrar ho chuka hai. Kya Subah qareeb nahi hai?"

(Surah Hud: 81)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Qaum e Lut (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Imam Hasan (as):

"Algharz Farishte Hazrat Lut (as) ke paas aaye. Us waqt Aap (as) Basti ke qareeb Kheti mein masroof the. Malaika ne Aap (as) ko Salam kiya. Us waqt woh Amaama bandhe hue the. Aap (as) ne unko apne ghar qayam karne ke liye kaha. Aap (as) ne Farishton se farmaya ke tum log Khuda ki Bad-tareen paas ja rahe ho. Aisa unhone ne 3 bar kaha, yani 3 bar gawahi di.

Jo woh ghar par aaye to Hazrat Lut (as) ki Biwi ne jab in haseen o jameel ladko ko dekha to woh Chhat par gayi aur seeti bajayi. Lekin kisi ne na suna. Jab ye harba kamyab nahi hua to Aag jala kar dhuwan kiya. Log Dhuwen ko dekh kar Aap (as) ke Makan ki taraf daude. Jab log pahunchne to Biwi ne kaha aaj hamare ghar haseen o jameel ladke aaye hue hain aise haseen aaj tak nahi dekhe.

Ye sun kar logon ne mutaliba kiya ke un jawano ko hamare hawale kar do.

Hazrat Lut (as) ne farmaya:

"Aye meri Qaum! Khuda se Daro! Mehmano ke mutalliq mujhe ruswa na karo. Kya tum mein koi ba sha'oor fard maujood nahi hai? Agar tumhe Jinsi Taskeen (Sex) hi bujhani hai to apni Biwiyon se Taskeen hasil karo. Tumhari Biwiyan meri ek tarah se Betiyan hain aur woh tumhare liye Pakeeza tar hain."

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hazrat Lut (as) ne  ن لى بكم قوة او آوى الى ركن شديد*  اkeh kar do cheezon ki khwahish ki thi: Unhone Badkaar Qaum ke muqabile mein Quwwat aur Mazboot Sahare ki khwahish ki thi. Qaem Aale Muhammad (atfs) jab Zahoor karenge to unhe dono cheezen hasil hongi. Khuda unhe bemisaal Quwwat ata karega aur Sahare ke liye aise saathi ata karega jinke Dil Faulad se bhi zyada Mazboot honge. Woh Lohe ke Pahad ko bhi kaatne ki quwwat rakhte honge aur us waqt tak Shasheerzani karte rahenge jab tak Khuda Raazi na ho jayega."

(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

*یَا رُكْنَ مَنْ لَا رُكْنَ لَهٗ یَا غِیَاثَا مَنْ لَاغِیَاثَ لَهٗ........*

(Dua-e-Joshane Kabir)

       ♦ QAUM-E-LUT (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1795)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَالُوۤا۟ أَوَلَمۡ نَنۡهَكَ عَنِ ٱلۡعَـٰلَمِینَ * قَالَ هَـٰۤؤُلَاۤءِ بَنَاتِیۤ إِن كُنتُمۡ فَـٰعِلِینَ * لَعَمۡرُكَ إِنَّهُمۡ لَفِی سَكۡرَتِهِمۡ یَعۡمَهُونَ * فَأَخَذَتۡهُمُ ٱلصَّیۡحَةُ مُشۡرِقِینَ * فَجَعَلۡنَا عَـٰلِیَهَا سَافِلَهَا وَأَمۡطَرۡنَا عَلَیۡهِمۡ حِجَارَةࣰ مِّن سِجِّیلٍ * إِنَّ فِی ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ لَـَٔایَـٰتࣲ لِّلۡمُتَوَسِّمِینَ * وَإِنَّهَا لَبِسَبِیلࣲ مُّقِیمٍ.*

"Unhone kaha ke: 'Hamne tumhe sabke aane se mana nahi kiya tha?' Lut (as) ne kaha ke: 'Tumhe kuchh karna hai to ye mere Betiya maujood hain. Teri Jaan ki Qasam! Woh log Shehwat ke nashe mein madhosh the."

"Po phatte hi unhe ek dhamake ne aa liya. Hamne unhe teho bala kar diya aur Hamne un Paki hui Mitti ke Pattharon ki Baarish kar di."

"Is Waqae mein Sahibaane Farasat Afraad (Intellectuals) ke liye bahut si Nishaniyan hain aur ye waqea jahan pesh aaya wo aam guzargah par waqe hai. 'Aika' wale Zalim the. Hamne unse Inteqaam liya. In dono Qaumon ke ujde hue ilaaqe khule Raaste par waqe hain."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 70 - 76)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

----------------------------------------------

🕌

Last year is Ayat ki Tafseer pesh ki thi, phir repeat kar rahe hain:

*قَالُوا۟ یَـٰلُوطُ إِنَّا رُسُلُ رَبِّكَ لَن یَصِلُوۤا۟ إِلَیۡكَۖ فَأَسۡرِ بِأَهۡلِكَ بِقِطۡعࣲ مِّنَ ٱلَّیۡلِ وَلَا یَلۡتَفِتۡ مِنكُمۡ أَحَدٌ إِلَّا ٱمۡرَأَتَكَۖ إِنَّهُۥ مُصِیبُهَا مَاۤ أَصَابَهُمۡۚ إِنَّ مَوۡعِدَهُمُ ٱلصُّبۡحُۚ أَلَیۡسَ ٱلصُّبۡحُ بِقَرِیبࣲ.*

"Unhone (Farishton) kaha: Aye Lut! Ham tere Rab ke Numainde hain. Ye log tumhara kuchh na bigad sakenge. Raat ke andar hi apne Khandan ko le kar nikal jao aur tum mein se koi peechhe palat kar na dekhe, siwai teri Biwi ke. Us par bhi wohi Azaab aanewala hai jo un par aanewala hai. Unke Azaab ke liye Subah ka waqt muqarrar ho chuka hai. Kya Subah qareeb nahi hai?"

(Surah Hud: 81)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Qaum e Lut (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Imam Baqir (as):

"Hazrat Lut (as) ki Qaum Shaam aur Misr (Syria & Egypt) ki Tijarti Shahrao (Business Street) par rihaish pazeer the."

"Hazrat Lut (as) ne 30 Saal tak unhe Deen ki Dawat di thi. Aap un logon ko Allah ki Raah ki taraf dete rahe aur unhe Azaab e Ilahi se Khabardar karte rahe. Woh log intihai gande the. Paishab Paikhane ke baad safai nahi karte the aur woh Ghusle Janabat bhi nahi karte the.

Hazrat Lut (as) Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke Khalazad bhai the aur Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ki Zauja Hazrat Sarah (sa) unki Bahen thi. Hazrat Ibrahim (as) aur Hazrat Lut (as) dono Allah ke Paighambar the. Lut (as) Sakhi aur Fayyaz Insaan the. Aap (as) Mehmano ki Tawazah karte the aur apni Ummat ko bhi Mehman Nawazi ki targheeb dete the.

Hazrat Lut (as) ki Qaum ne unse kaha: "Agar Mehman Nawazi se baaz na aaye to ham Aap (as) ke Mehmano ko ruswa karenge, jiski wajah se Aap (as) ko bhi ruswai uthani padegi.

Us dhamki ke baad Aap (as) chori chhupe Mehman Nawazi karte the ke kahin Aap (as) ki Qaum Aap (as) ke Mehmano ko ruswa na kare. Jis ilaqe mein Hazrat Lut (as) Tableegh e Deen karte the wahan Aap (as) ka Qabila nahi tha. Hazrat Ibrahim (as) aur Hazrat Lut (as) dono ko hi in Badbakhton ke mutalliq Azaab ka andesha tha. Dono Bagahe Ahdiyyat mein Azeem Maqam rakhte the. Allah Ta'ala Ibrahim (as) aur Lut (as) ki bahami Muhabbat ki wajah se unse Azaab ko muakhkhar (delay) karta raha....."

(Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Khuda ko jis shakhs ki zaroorat hoti hai Woh use Aadat e Bad mein kabhi bhi mubtila nahi hone deta. Aise logon ke dubur (Anus) mein ulte Rahem hote hain aur unko bhi Aurto ki tarah se Shehwat mehsoos hoti hai. Un mein Iblis ka Beta jiska naam "Zawal" hai sharik hota hai. Woh jis Mard mein sharik ho jaye to woh Mard Maf'ool ban jata hai aur jis Aurat mein sharik ho jaye woh Badkaar ban jati hai. Aur jo shakhs 40 Saal ki umr mein Aghlambazi (Homosexuality) kare to woh usse kabhi juda nahi hota. Aise afraad "Sodom - *سدوم*" ki baqiyaat hain. Mein ye nahi kehta ke woh Nasli etbar se Ahle Sodom se talluq rakhte hain albatta unki Teenat Ahle Sodom ki si hai."

"Allah ne 4 Bastiyon ko ulta tha jinke naam: Sodom, Sareem - *صريم*, Ladma - *لدما* " aur Ameera - *عميرا* " the. Jibrael Amin (as) ne un Bastiyon ko Saatvin Zameen se kaat kar unhe apne Paron par itna buland kiya tha ke Aasmaan walon ne unke Kutton ki bhonkne ki awazen suni thi."

(Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Bare Ilaha hame aise Badkaaron se mehfooz rakh.

(To be Cont'd......)

       ♦ QAUM-E-LUT (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1796)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَالُوۤا۟ أَوَلَمۡ نَنۡهَكَ عَنِ ٱلۡعَـٰلَمِینَ * قَالَ هَـٰۤؤُلَاۤءِ بَنَاتِیۤ إِن كُنتُمۡ فَـٰعِلِینَ * لَعَمۡرُكَ إِنَّهُمۡ لَفِی سَكۡرَتِهِمۡ یَعۡمَهُونَ * فَأَخَذَتۡهُمُ ٱلصَّیۡحَةُ مُشۡرِقِینَ * فَجَعَلۡنَا عَـٰلِیَهَا سَافِلَهَا وَأَمۡطَرۡنَا عَلَیۡهِمۡ حِجَارَةࣰ مِّن سِجِّیلٍ * إِنَّ فِی ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ لَـَٔایَـٰتࣲ لِّلۡمُتَوَسِّمِینَ * وَإِنَّهَا لَبِسَبِیلࣲ مُّقِیمٍ.*

"Unhone kaha ke: 'Hamne tumhe sabke aane se mana nahi kiya tha?' Lut (as) ne kaha ke: 'Tumhe kuchh karna hai to ye mere Betiya maujood hain. Teri Jaan ki Qasam! Woh log Shehwat ke nashe mein madhosh the."

"Po phatte hi unhe ek dhamake ne aa liya. Hamne unhe teho bala kar diya aur Hamne un Paki hui Mitti ke Pattharon ki Baarish kar di."

"Is Waqae mein Sahibaane Farasat Afraad (Intellectuals) ke liye bahut si Nishaniyan hain aur ye waqea jahan pesh aaya wo aam guzargah par waqe hai. 'Aika' wale Zalim the. Hamne unse Inteqaam liya. In dono Qaumon ke ujde hue ilaaqe khule Raaste par waqe hain."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 70 - 76)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

----------------------------------------------

🕌

Last year is Ayat ki Tafseer pesh ki thi, phir repeat kar rahe hain:

*فَلَمَّا جَاۤءَ أَمۡرُنَا جَعَلۡنَا عَـٰلِیَهَا سَافِلَهَا وَأَمۡطَرۡنَا عَلَیۡهَا حِجَارَةࣰ مِّن سِجِّیلࣲ مَّنضُودࣲ *  مُّسَوَّمَةً عِندَ رَبِّكَۖ وَمَا هِیَ مِنَ ٱلظَّـٰلِمِینَ بِبَعِیدࣲ.*

"Jab hamare Faisle ka waqt aaya to Hamne uske upar ke hisse ko neeche ulat diya aur us par Paki hui Mitti ke Patthar tabad tod barsai. Un mein se har Patthar tere Rab ki taraf se Nishanzadah tha aur ye Azaab Zalimon se door nahi hai."

(Surah Hud: 82 - 83)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Qaum e Lut (as) ka akheri hissa pesh hai:

🕌

Imam Baqir (as): (Cont'd)

"..... Chunanche jab aadhi Raat ka waqt hua to Hazrat Lut (as) apni Betiyon ko le kar wahan se rawana hue. Uski Biwi ne saath jaane se inkar kar diya aur woh apni Qaum ki taraf daud padi aur woh unko ye batane gayi ke Lut (as) apni Betiyon ko lekar yahan se ja rahe hain.

Subah ke waqt Arsh se mujhe ye sada sunayi di ke Aye Jibrael! Allah ki taraf se Qaum e Lut (as) par Azaab ka Faisla ho chuka hai. Lehaza tum Qaum e Lut (as) ki Basti mein jao. Us Basti ko Saatvin Zameen se kaat kar Aasmaan ki taraf le aao. Aur wahan pahunch kar thehre raho, yahan tak ke iske ulatne ke ke mutalliq tujhe Khuda ka Hukm mausool ho. Haan, us jagah par ye Ibrat ke liye Lut (as) ke Ghar ko baqi rakho. Phir waisa hi kiya. Phir Allah ne un par Pattharon ki Baarish ki aur Aap (as) ki Ummat mein se jo ye Bad-Fe'li (Un-Natural Sex) karega usse bhi ye Azaab door nahi hoga. Unka Shaher Baheera e Tabriya hai jo Syria ke Suburb mein hai. Unko Behre Shaam aur Misr ke darmiyan ulat diya tha aur jahan wo Zameen giri to usne Samandar mein Teelon ki shakl ikhtiyar kar li."

(Noorus Saqlain)

(The End ......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as)

"Jo bhi shakhs Qaum e Lut (as) ke amal (Homosexuality) ko Halal samajhta hai to Maut ke waqt us par Khuda ek Patthar bhejta hai jisse uski Maut waqe hoti hai, lekin Duniya walon ko woh Patthar dikhayi nahi deta."

👉🏻

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Jab Qaum e Lut (as) ne Bad-kaari (Homosexuality) ko rawaj diya to Zameen itna royi ke uske Aansu Arsh e Ilahi tak pahuche. Allah Ta'ala ne Aasmaan ko Hukm diya ke un par Patthar barsa aur Zameen ko Hukm diya ke un ko nigal le."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

👉🏻

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Jo shakhs apne aap se chhedkhani ki be raza o raghbat (inclined) ijazat de to Khuda us par Aurton ki si Shehwat (Lust) dal deta hai."

(Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

"Khudaya! Kitne hi Bande hain ke jinki Subah o Shaam Samandaron ki Tareekiyon, Hawaon ki tez jhadokon aur haulnak Maujon ke darmiyan guzar rahi hai ke har aan ye ummeed rehti hai ke kab gharq aur halaak ho jayenge aur bachne ki koi tadbeer nahi hai ya phir Bijli ke girne, Makan ke girne, Aag lagne, Luqme ke gulugir ho jane, Zameen dhans jane, Surat ke bigad jaane aur Sangsaar (Stoning) ho jaane ke khatarat mein mubtila hain aur mein in sab ki taraf se aafiyat mein hun..... Al Hamdo lillah... Allahumma Swalle ala Muhammadin wa Aale Muhammad...."

(Dua-e-Joshan e Sagheer - Mafateeh)
