⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ MAUQA O MASLAHET ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1797)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ فِی ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ لَـَٔایَـٰتࣲ لِّلۡمُتَوَسِّمِینَ * وَإِنَّهَا لَبِسَبِیلࣲ مُّقِیمٍ. * إِنَّ فِی ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ لَـَٔایَةࣰ لِّلۡمُؤۡمِنِینَ * وَإِن كَانَ أَصۡحَـٰبُ ٱلۡأَیۡكَةِ لَظَـٰلِمِینَ * فَٱنتَقَمۡنَا مِنۡهُمۡ وَإِنَّهُمَا لَبِإِمَامࣲ مُّبِینࣲ*

"Is Waqae mein Sahibaane Farasat Afraad (Intellectuals) ke liye bahut si Nishaniyan hain aur ye waqea jahan pesh aaya wo aam guzargah par waqe hai. 'Aika' wale Zalim the. Hamne unse Inteqaam liya. In dono Qaumon ke ujde hue ilaaqe khule Raaste par waqe hain."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 70 - 79)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

----------------------------------------------

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

*فَٱنتَقَمۡنَا مِنۡهُمۡ وَإِنَّهُمَا لَبِإِمَامࣲ مُّبِینࣲ*

Iska zahiri lafzi tarjuma yun bhi ho sakta hai:

"Pas Hamne unse Badla liya jabke in dono Qaumon ke ek khula Imam tha."

Yani is Qaumon ke saamne khule hue Imam (Rahnuma) hote hue bhi, in Qaumon ne un par Zulm kiya aur un par Allah ka Qaher nazil hua. Yehi rawayya Ummat e Rasool (saww) ka tha.

🕌

Last year is Ayat ki Tafseer pesh ki thi, phir repeat kar rahe hain:

"Jaise hi Woh (Farishte) aaye to Lut (as) ki Qaum ke log daudte hue unke paas aaye aur isse pehle woh Badkariyan kiya karte the. Lut (as) ne kaha: "Aye meri Qaum! Ye meri Betiyan (Tumhari Biwiyan) maujood hain. Ye tumhare liye zyada Pakeeza hain. Tum Allah se Daro aur Mehmano ke mutalliq ruswa na karo. Kya tumhara andar koi basha'oor shakhs maujood nahi hai?"

"Woh kehne lage ke tu jaanta hai ke tumhari Betiyon se hamara koi talluq nahi hai aur ham jo kuchh chahte hain usse mutalliq tumhe bakhoobi ilm hai. Lut (as) ne kaha: Aye Kaash! Meri paas tumhare muqabile ke liye Quwwat maujood hoti ya mein kisi mazboot Sahare ki panah le sakta."

(Surah Hud: 77 - 80)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Ab is Ayat ka doosre pehlu se mafhoom samjhen.

🕌

Jo situation Hazrat Lut (as) ke Ghar par thi, waisi hi Hazrat Ali (as) wa Janabe Zehra (sa) ke Ghar par hui thi. Baad e Shahadat e Rasool (saww) Wehshi Darinde Aap (as) ke Ghar par toot pade, Janabe Zehra (sa) par jalta hua Dirwaza giraya gaya, pehlu shakista hua, Janabe Mohsin (as) ki Paidaish se pehle hi Shahadat hui. Aap (as) ke gale mein Rassi bandhi aur khechte hue Ghar se nikala.

Woh Bahadur Wasi e Rasool (saww) Jinhone itne Ma'arke Fatah kiye, Bahadur Dushmano ko pachhada. Jinke saamne Kuffar ki aane ki himmat nahi hoti thi unhone ye sab kaise bardasht kiya. 25 Saal Khamosh Zindagi kyon guzari. Iska jawab khud Imam (as) ne diya. Ek wajah to ye thi ke Rasool (saww) ki Ali (as) ko Wasiyyat thi ke mere baad agar saathi na hon to apne Dushmano se muqabila na karna.

👉🏻

Jange Jamal ke baad Hazrat Ali (as) kuchh saathiyon ne kaha ke agar Aap (as) ke Siyasi Hareefon (Opponents) ki Hukumat sahi na hoti to Aap (as) unse bhi Jang karte jis tarah Jange Jamal mein Jang ki.

Hazrat Ali (as) ne Masjid mein Khutba diya aur farmaya:

"Suno! Meine Jang na karke 6 Anbiya ki pairavi ki hai. Meine Jang na karke Hazrat Lut (as) ki pairavi ki hai, (Ye Ayat padhi 11:80) Jab Quwwat na hone ki wajah se Hazrat Lut (as) ne Mukhalefin se Jang nahi ki thi to meine agar Quwwat na hone ki wajah se Jang nahi ki to is mein kya etraz hai? Agar tum kaho ke Lut (as) ke paas Quwwat thi to Kafir ban jaoge. Agar kaho ke unhone Quwwat na hone ki wajah se Jang nahi ki thi to phir yaad rakho, Wasi ne bhi Quwwat na hone ki wajah se Jang nahi ki thi."

(Ilalus Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hazrat Lut (as) ne

ن لى بكم قوة او آوى الى ركن شديد* 

keh kar do cheezon ki khwahish ki thi: Unhone Badkaar Qaum ke muqabile mein Quwwat aur Mazboot Sahare ki khwahish ki thi. Qaem Aale Muhammad (atfs) jab Zahoor karenge to unhe dono cheezen hasil hongi. Khuda unhe bemisaal Quwwat ata karega aur Sahare ke liye aise saathi ata karega jinke Dil Faulad se bhi zyada Mazboot honge. Woh Lohe ke Pahad ko bhi kaatne ki quwwat rakhte honge aur us waqt tak Shasheerzani karte rahenge jab tak Khuda Raazi na ho jayega."

(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

*یَا رُكْنَ مَنْ لَا رُكْنَ لَهٗ یَا غِیَاثَا مَنْ لَاغِیَاثَ لَهٗ........*

(Dua-e-Joshane Kabir)

♦ MOTAWASSEMIN - INTELLECTUALS ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1798)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

إِنَّ فِی ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ لَـَٔایَـٰتࣲ لِّلۡمُتَوَسِّمِینَ

"Is Waqae mein Sahibaane Firaasat Afraad (Intellectuals) ke liye bahut si Nishaniyan hain."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 75)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

Lafz متوسم ka Root hai وسم yaani asarandaz hona. متوسم yaani jo koi sirf kam asar ya nishani se pehchaan le. Isliye iske maani Urdu mein Firaasat, hoshyari, English mein those who discern, those who read signs. Jo Nishaniyon ko padh le.

😰

مُّحَمَّدٌ رَّسُولُ ٱللَّهِ ۚ وَٱلَّذِينَ مَعَهُۥٓ أَشِدَّآءُ عَلَى ٱلْكُفَّارِ رُحَمَآءُ بَيْنَهُمْ ۖ تَرَىٰهُمْ رُكَّعًا سُجَّدًا يَبْتَغُونَ فَضْلًا مِّنَ ٱللَّهِ وَرِضْوَٰنًا ۖ سِيمَاهُمْ فِى وُجُوهِهِم مِّنْ أَثَرِ ٱلسُّجُودِ ۚ

"Muhammad Rasoolullah hain. Aur jo log unke saath hain, woh Kuffar par sakht aur aapas mein Raheem hain, tum jab dekhoge unhe Ruku o Sujood aur Allah ke Fazl aur Uski Khushnoodi ki talab mein mashghool paoge. *Sujood ke Asaraat unke Chehron par maujood hain jin se woh alag pehchane jaate hain."* (48:29)

🧠

Imam Baqir (as):

"Har shakhs ki Aankhon ke darmiyan likha hua hai ke ye Momin hai ya Kafir, lekin wo Tehreer tum se poshida hai,  lekin Aimma e Huda (as) se ye Tehreer poshida nahi hai. Woh har shakhs ko dekh kar pehchan lete hain ke ye Momin hai ya Kafir hai."

Phir Aap (as) ne ye Ayat padhi (15:75) aur farmaya:

"Ham "متوسم - Motawassim (Ahle Firaasat) hain."

(Ikhtesaas e Mufeed, Noorus Saqlain)

📚🧠

Imam Baqir (as) ne Janabe Salman e Muhammadi (ra) ko Motawassemin mein shumar qarar diya hai.

(Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 🕌

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Momin ki Firsaasat se bacho, kyonki Momin Allah ke Noor se dekhta hai. (15:75)"

(Noorus Saqlain)

🧠

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Aqlmand Shakhs ki Nishaani ye hai ke jab bhi woh koi kalaam karta hai to Tadabbur aur Tafakkur ke saath karta hai. Agar kalaam mufeed (faydemand) ho to use kehta hai aur use nafaa pahu'nchta hai aur soodmand (faayde-mand) na ho to khamosh rehta hai, jis se wo amaan mein rehta hai."

(Mafaatih al Hayaat, p26)

⚰️

Imam Baqir (as):

"Momin ki Nishaani ye hai ke jab uski Maut ka waqt aata hai to uske chehre ka rang jitna safed tha usse zyada safed aur roshan ho jaata hai, pehsaani par paseena aane lagta hai, uski Aa'nkho’n se Aa'nsuo’n ki tarah rutubat behne lagti hai; to yehi uski Rooh nikalne ki Nishaani hai…"

(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v1, p100)

🤲🏻

اَلسَّلَامُ عَلٰى خَآصَّةِ اللّٰهِ مِنْ خَلْقِهِ اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَى الْمُتَوَسِّمِيْنَ....

(Ziyarat-e-Ameerul Mo'meneen (as) in Kufa - Mafateeh)

_______________________________________

Kuchh Aur Riwayat:

تفسير آية ﴿إِنَّ فِي ذَلِكَ لَآيَاتٍ لِلْمُتَوَسِّمِينَ﴾ . من هم المتوسمين ؟

عَنْ سَلْمَانَ الْفَارِسِيِّ (رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ) قَالَ :

سَمِعْتُ أَمِيرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ (عَلَيْهِ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ) يَقُولُ‏ فِي قَوْلِ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَ‏ :

﴿إِنَّ فِي ذلِكَ لَآياتٍ لِلْمُتَوَسِّمِينَ﴾ .

فَكَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ (صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وَآلِهِ وَسَلَّمَ) يَعْرِفُ الْخَلْقَ بِسِيمَاهُمْ ،

وَأَنَا بَعْدَهُ الْمُتَوَسِّمُ وَالْأَئِمَّةُ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّتِيَ الْمُتَوَسِّمُونَ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ .

المصدر : (بصائر الدرجات : ص104.)

-------

عَنْ الْإِمَامِ الرِّضَا (عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ) قَالَ :

لَنَا أَعْيُنٌ لَا تُشْبِهُ أَعْيُنَ النَّاسِ ، وَفِيهَا نُورٌ لَيْسَ لِلشَّيْطَانِ فِيهِ شِرْكٌ‏ .

المصدر : (بصائر الدرجات : ص124.)

-------

عَنْ الْإِمَامِ الصَّادِقِ (عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ) قَالَ :

إِنَّ فِي الْإِمَامِ آيَاتٍ لِلْمُتَوَسِّمِينَ وَهُوَ السَّبِيلُ الْمُقِيمُ ،

يَنْظُرُ بِنُورِ اللَّهِ وَيَنْطِقُ عَنِ اللَّهِ لَا يَعْزُبُ عَنْهُ شَيْ‏ءٌ مِمَّا أَرَادَ .

المصدر : (تفسير العياشي : ج2، ص247.)

-------

عَنْ الْإِمَامِ الصَّادِقِ (عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ) قَالَ :

نَحْنُ الْمُتَوَسِّمِينَ وَالسَّبِيلُ فِينَا مُقِيمٌ ،

وَالسَّبِيلُ طَرِيقُ الْجَنَّةِ ﴿وَإِنَّها لَبِسَبِيلٍ مُقِيمٍ‏﴾ .

المصدر : (البحار : ج24، ص123.)

------

عَنْ الْإِمَامِ الصَّادِقِ (عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ) قَالَ :

مَا مِنْ أَحَدٍ إِلَّا وَمَكْتُوبٌ بَيْنَ عَيْنَيْهِ مُؤْمِنٌ أَوْ كَافِرٌ ،

مَحْجُوبَةٌ عَنِ الْخَلَائِقِ إِلَّا الْأَئِمَّةَ وَالْأَوْصِيَاءَ فَلَيْسَ بِمَحْجُوبٍ عَنْهُمْ .

ثُمَّ تَلَا : ﴿إِنَّ فِي ذلِكَ لَآياتٍ لِلْمُتَوَسِّمِينَ﴾‏ . ثُمَّ قَالَ (عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ) :

نَحْنُ الْمُتَوَسِّمُونَ ، وَلَيْسَ وَاللَّهِ أَحَدٌ يَدْخُلُ عَلَيْنَا إِلَّا عَرَفْنَاهُ بِتِلْكَ السِّمَةِ .

المصدر : (البحار : ج24، ص127. عن كنز الفوائد.)

-------

عَنْ الْإِمَامِ الصَّادِقِ (عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ) قَالَ :

إِنَّ الْإِمَامَ إِذَا نَظَرَ إِلَى رَجُلٍ عَرَفَهُ وَعَرَفَ مَا هُو عَلَيْهِ وَعَرَفَ لَوْنَهُ‏ ، وَإِنْ سَمِعَ كَلَامَهُ مِنْ خَلْفِ حَائِطٍ عَرَفَهُ وَعَرَفَ مَا هُوَ ، لِأَنَّ اللَّهَ‏ يَقُولُ‏ : ﴿وَمِنْ آياتِهِ خَلْقُ السَّماواتِ وَالْأَرْضِ وَاخْتِلافُ أَلْسِنَتِكُمْ وَأَلْوانِكُمْ إِنَّ فِي ذلِكَ لَآياتٍ لِلْعالِمِينَ‏﴾ . فَهُمُ الْعُلَمَاءُ وَلَيْسَ يَسْمَعُ شَيْئاً مِنَ الْأَلْسُنِ إِلَّا عَرَفَهُ نَاجٍ أَوْ هَالِكٌ ، فَلِذَلِكَ يُجِيبُهُمْ بِالَّذِي يُجِيبُهُمْ بِهِ‏ .

المصدر : (البحار : ج24، ص124. عن الاختصاص.)

♦ TAKZEEB-E-ANBIYA KA ANJAAM ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1799)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَإِن كَانَ أَصۡحَـٰبُ ٱلۡأَیۡكَةِ لَظَـٰلِمِینَ.

وَلَقَدۡ كَذَّبَ أَصۡحَـٰبُ ٱلۡحِجۡرِ ٱلۡمُرۡسَلِینَ * وَءَاتَیۡنَـٰهُمۡ ءَایَـٰتِنَا فَكَانُوا۟ عَنۡهَا مُعۡرِضِینَ * وَكَانُوا۟ یَنۡحِتُونَ مِنَ ٱلۡجِبَالِ بُیُوتًا ءَامِنِینَ * فَأَخَذَتۡهُمُ ٱلصَّیۡحَةُ مُصۡبِحِینَ * فَمَاۤ أَغۡنَىٰ عَنۡهُم مَّا كَانُوا۟ یَكۡسِبُونَ

"Aika' wale Zaalim the. Hamne unse Inteqam liya."

"Hijr' ke log bhi Rasoolon ki Takzeeb (Denying) kar chuke the. Hamne Apni Nishaniyan unke paas bheji, magar woh unhe nazarandaz karte rahe. Woh Pahad Tarash kar mehfooz qism ke Makanaat banate the. Akhirkar Subah hote hi unhe ek zabardast dhamake ne aa liye. Unki kamaayi unke kisi kaam na aayi."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 78, 80-84)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

In Ayaat mein Allah Ta'ala ne mukhtalif Qaumon ka zikr kiya hai jin par Azaab e Ilahi ka etaab nazil hua tha. Jaisa ke Asaab e Aika, Ashaab e Hijr aur Qaum e Lut.

Qaum e Lut ke bare mein tazkara ho chuka hai.

Ashaab e Aika Hazrat Shu'aib (as) ke zamane mein thi. Jabke Ashaab e Hijr Hazrat Saleh (as) ki Qaum thi.

Aika ke maani hain baham jude hue Darakht ya Jangal. Ashaabul Aika Hijaz o Shaam ke darmiyan sarsabz o shadab zameen par abaad thi. Unki Zindagi bahut khushhaal thi. Lekin un ko Daulat ke Takabbur wa Ghaflat ne gher liya. Fitna o Fasaad mein mubtila ho gaye. Apne Paighambar ki Takzeeb ki.

Isi tarah Ashhab e Hijr.

Jinhone Mursaleen ki Takzeeb ki. Ye log Madina aur Shaam ke darmiyan rehte the. Patthar Tarash log the. Ye Qaum Civilized thi. Inhone apne Ghar Mazboot Pattharon se bana rakhe the. History mein aur Museum mein hamne dekha hoga old Civilization, jahan Pattharon ki gufayen (Caves) nazar aate hain. Pattharon ki Murtiyan nazar aati hain. Is Ayat mein inhi Qaumon ki taraf ishaara hai. Ye log Allah ke bheje hue Numaindon ka inkaar karte the aur Patthar ke Devi Devtaon ki pooja karte the.

Ye sab Nishaniyon ke taur par aaj bhi maujood hain taake aaj bhi log dekhen aur is se Ibrat hasil karen.

Chaahe kitni ye Qaumen Khush haal thi ya Civilized thi lekin inhone Sarkashi ki, Paighambaron ki Takzeeb ki, Qaum e Lut jaisi ghalat Sexi Afaal mein maloos hui to Azaab e Ilahi ne ek hi jhatke inhe gher liye aur ye Qaumen tabaah o barbaad ho gayi.

Riwayat mein hai ke 9th Hijri mein jab Rasoole Khuda (saww) Jange Tubuk par Rome ki taraf ja rahe the to Lashkare Islam ek maqam par ruka to Aap (saww) ne wahan rukne se mana kiya aur farmaya:

"Ye wohi Qaum e Samood ka ilaaqa hai jis par Azaab e Ilahi naazil hua tha."

(Alaamul Qur'an Khazaili P-292)

Allah Ta'ala ne ye misaalen hame isliye pesh ki taake ham bhi aise afa'al se door rahen jo unhone kiya.

Ye waqeat aur Tafseel se repeat hote rahege, jaise Surah Hud mein bayan hua aur Surah Shu'ara mein bhi tazkara hoga.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 🙌🏻

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Aye Farzand e Adam! Jo tere liye kaafi hai, utna tere paas hai. Magar tu uski talab kar raha hai jo tujhe Sarkashi (rebellion/ disobedience/nafarmaani) par ubhaare. Farzand e Adam! Na tu kam par Qana'at (content) karta hai aur na tu zyada se ser (satisfied) hota hai."

(Ahadees e Rasul (saww), p97)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ لَا تَجْعَلْنِيْ مِنَ الْاَشْرَارِ وَ لَا مِنْ اَصْحَابِ النَّارِ، وَ لَا تَحْرِمْنِيْ صُحْبَةَ الْاَخْيَارِ......

(Dua-e-Arafa)

   2nd November 2021, Tuesday

       ♦ SAFH-E-JAMEEL ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1800)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَمَا خَلَقۡنَا ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضَ وَمَا بَیۡنَهُمَاۤ إِلَّا بِٱلۡحَقِّۗ وَإِنَّ ٱلسَّاعَةَ لَـَٔاتِیَةࣱۖ فَٱصۡفَحِ ٱلصَّفۡحَ ٱلۡجَمِیلَ * إِنَّ رَبَّكَ هُوَ ٱلۡخَلَّـٰقُ ٱلۡعَلِیمُ.

"Hamne Aasmaano aur Zameen aur jo kuchh in dono mein hai, sab ko Haq ke saath banaya hai aur Qayamat yaqeenan aa kar rahegi. Aap khoobsoorati ke saath darguzar karen. Yaqeenan Aapka Rab sab ko Paida Karnewala hai aur sab kuchh Jannewala hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 85 - 86)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Anbiya ki Qaumon ke waqeat ke baad Allah Ta'ala Tauheed ke mauzo par zikr karta hai, jiska paigham har Nabi ne diya aur yehi unka maqsad bhi tha. Allah Ta'ala  logon ko is baat par tawajjoh dila raha hai ke ye Aasmaano aur Zameen mein aur inke darmiyan jo kuchh tum dekh rahe ho ye sab Allah ne banaya hai. Aur ye sab koi permanent cheez nahi, Qayamat to aane wali hi hai, sab khatm ho jayega. Ye sab woh baaten hain jiska har Insaan mushaheda karta hai, to phir iske Bananwale ka Inkaar kyonkar kar sakta hai.

Allah ne Apne Nabi (saww) ki diljoi bhi ki hai, jo bhi unki Ummat unke saath kya bartao kar rahi hai us par Sabr karen aur is tarah Bakhsh den jis mein malamat na ho. Isliye Fateh Makkah ke baad Aap (saww) ne sab ko Ma'af kiya. Kyonki Deen mein Jabr nahi hai. Insaan apne ikhtiyar ghaur o fikr se Deen ko samjhe aur Imaan laaye.

☘️

Imam Zainul Abedin (as) & Imam Reza (as):

"(Safhe Jameel) Khoobsurat Darguzar se aisi Ma'afi muraad hai jis mein Malamat shamil na ho."

(Amaali e Sadooq, Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Aasmaan mein Momin ko aise jaana pehchana jaata hai jaisa ke koi shakhs apne Ahl o Ayaal ko jaanta pehchaanta hai aur ek Momin Allah ko Malak e Muqarrab se zyada azeez hota hai."

(Uyoon Akhbaar ar Reza, v2, p88)

🕌

Imam Kazim (as):

"Jab Rasul e Akram (saww) shikam e Maadar se Zameen par tashreef laaye to Baayaa'n (left) haath zameen par rakha aur Daayaa'n (right) Aasmaan ki taraf buland kar ke Labo'n ko Tauheed e Ilaahi mein harkat di…."

(Seerat e Masumeen, Ahsaan ul Maqaal, v1, p26)

🤲🏻

.....وَ اٰتِنَا فِيْ مُوَالَاتِهِ مِنْ لَدُنْكَ فَضْلًا وَ اِحْسَانًا وَ مَغْفِرَةً وَ رِضْوَانًا اِنَّكَ ذُو الْمَنِّ الْقَدِيْمِ وَ الصَّفْحِ الْجَمِيْلِ۔....

(Salwat Imam Mohd Taqi (as) - Mafateeh)

       ♦ SAB-E-MASAANI ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1801)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَقَدۡ ءَاتَیۡنَـٰكَ سَبۡعࣰا مِّنَ ٱلۡمَثَانِی وَٱلۡقُرۡءَانَ ٱلۡعَظِیمَ.

"Aur Hamne Aapko bar bar dohrayi jaane wali 7 Ayaat aur Qur'an e Azeem diya hai."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 85 - 86)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Imam Jafar Sadiq (as) ne farmaya ke "*سبع مثانی* - Sabun Masaani" se Surah Fateha muraad hai. Surah Fateha mein Bismillah bhi shamil hai aur ye afzal tareen Ayat hai. " *مثانی* - Masaani" kehne ki wajah ye hai ke do Rakaat mein ise lazmi taur par padha jata hai.

(Tehzeebul Ahkam, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Mohd Baqir (as):

"Ham woh "Masani" hain jo Khuda ne Apne Nabi ko ata farmayi hai."

(Noorus Saqlain)

📖

Imam Sadiq (as) se *سبع مثانی* ke bare mein sawal kiya to farmaya:

"Iske zahir se Surah Al Hamd murad hai aur iske Baatin se woh Saat Hadi murad jinka Saatwan Qaim (atfs) hai."

(Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Baqir (as), Imam Ali (as), Imam Musa Kazim (as) se riwayat hai ke 'Sab e Masaani' se murad 7 Imam aur Qaem (atfs) hain.

👉🏻

Muhaddis Kashani ke baqaul is hadis mein 7 Hadi ke Naam ka is tarah imkaan hai: 'Mohd, Ali, Fatema, Hasan, Husain, Jafar, Musa (as) etc.'

Kuchh Mufassirin ka Nazariya ye hai ke: '7 se muraad Chahardah Masoomeen (as) hain, kyonki Lafz Sab e Masaani means '7 double' mein 7x2=14.

(Bihaarul Anwaar, Vol 7, P-114, Isbaatul Huda, Vol 7, P-102)

🕌

Hazrat Ali (as) Imam Baqir (as), Imam Sadiq (as):

"Ham woh "Masaani" hain jo Khuda ne apne Paighambar ko ata kiye hain aur ham 'Wajhullah' hain, tumhare darmiyan Zameen par chal rahe hain, jisne hame pehchana so pehchana aur jo ham se na-waqif raha to us ke aage Dozakh hai."

(Kitabut Tauheed, Usoole Kaafi, Majmaul Bayan)

📖

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Taurat ke ewaz Khuda ne mujhe taweel Suraten ata ki aur Injeel ki jagah mujhe 100 Ayaat rakhne wali Suraten ata farmayi aur Zuboor ki jagah Khuda ne mujhe "Masaani" ata farmayi."

📖

" Jise Khuda ne Qur'an ata kiya ho aur iske bawajood woh ye samjhe ke kisi aur ko isse afzal Ne'mat ata hui hai to usne Azeem ko mamooli samjha aur mamooli ko Azeem samjha."

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

📚📖

Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):

"Bismillah Surah Fateha ki Ayat hai aur 7 Ayaat ki takmeel (complete) Bismillah se hoti hai. Meine Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke zabaan e athar se ye Kalemaat sune ke Allah Ta'ala ne Ayat Sab e Masaani nazil farmayi. Allah ne is Ayat mein Surah Fateha ko poore Qur'an ke barabar qaraar diya aur mujh par Ehsaan jataate hue kaha ke Meine tujhe Surah Fateha aur Qur'an ata kiya."

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab tumhe koi Haajat dar pesh ho to do Rakat Namaz padho jis mein "Masaani" ke saath aur Surah padho aur Namaz khatm karne ke baad Khuda se Haajat talab karo."

Jab Masaani ke baare mein sawal kiya to bataya Bismillah ke baad Al Hamd...

(Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

......اَللّٰهُمَّ رَبَّ السَّمَاوَاتِ السَّبْعِ، وَرَبَّ الْاَرَضِيْنَ السَّبْعِ وَمَا فِيْهِنَّ وَما بَيْنَهُنَّ، وَرَبَّ الْعَرْشِ الْعَظِيْمِ، وَرَبَّ السَبْعِ الْمَثَانِيْ، وَالْقُرْاٰنِ الْعَظِيْمِ، وَرَبَّ اِسْرَافِيْلَ وَمِيْكَاۤئِيْلَ وَجَبْرَاۤئِيْلَ، وَرَبَّ مُحَمَّدٍ صَلَّى اللهُ عَلَيْهِ وَاٰلِهِ سَيِّدِ الْمُرْسَلِيْنَ وَخَاتَمِ النَّبِيِّيْنَ،......

(Sahifa Kamila Dua 44 - Mafateeh)

           ♦ DUNIYADARI ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1802)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

لَا تَمُدَّنَّ عَیۡنَیۡكَ إِلَىٰ مَا مَتَّعۡنَا بِهِۦۤ أَزۡوَ ٰ⁠جࣰا مِّنۡهُمۡ وَلَا تَحۡزَنۡ عَلَیۡهِمۡ وَٱخۡفِضۡ جَنَاحَكَ لِلۡمُؤۡمِنِینَ.

"Tum is Mata e Duniya (Provisions) ki taraf Aankh utha kar na dekho, jo Hamne un mein mukhtalif qism ke logon ko de rakhi hai aur unke haal par apna Dil na kudhao (grief) aur Aap apne Shaano ko Sahiban e Imaan ke liye jhukaye rakhen."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 88)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Sadeqain (as):

"Ek martaba Hazrat Rasoole Khuda (saww) par tangdasti chha gayi. Aap (saww) ne ek Yahoodi se kuchh Raqam bataur Qarz talab ki. Usne kaha ke Muharramat (saww) ke paas na to Bhed Bakriyan hain aur na unke paas Oont hain iske bawajood mein unhe udhar dun to kaise du?"

Rasoole Akram (saww) ne farmaya: "Khuda ne mujhe Aasmaan o Zameen ka Ameen banaya hai agar tu mujhe Qarz dega to mein tujhe zaroor lauta dunga. Phir Aap (saww) ne uske paas kuchh Dhaalen (Shields) rahen rakhin aur usse Qarz hasil kiya. Us waqt Allah Ta'ala ki taraf se Aap (saww) par ye Ayat nazil hui (15:88)"

(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🌍

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Allah Ta'ala ne Rasoole Khuda (saww) par ye Ayat (15:88) nazil hui to AanHazrat (saww) ne farmaya:

"Jise Khuda ki Tasalli dene par bhi sukoon hasil na ho to uska Dil Duniyavi Ne'maat ki hasraton ki wajah se tukde tukde ho jayega aur jo shakhs doosron ki Daulat ki taraf nazren jamayega to uske Gham aur Pareshani mein izaafa hoga aue uske Ghusse ko shifa nahi milegi aur jo Khuda ki Ne'mat ko sirf Khurak aue Poshak tak mehdood samajhta ho woh intihai qaleel Ilm wala hai aur uske liye Azaab qareeb aa chuka hai aur jo Duniya ki wajah se ghamgeen hua to woh Allah par naraz hua aur jisne apne upar aane wali musibat ka logon ke paas shikwa kiya to usne apne Rab ki shikayat ki aur jo kisi Daulatmand ke darwaze par kuchh Daulat hasil karne ki gharz se gaya to uske Deen ka do tihai (⅔) hissa chala gaya."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 🌍

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Fuqaha Rasoolo'n ke Ameen (Amanatdar) hain, jab tak ke woh Duniyadari mein na padein."

Logo'n ne puchha, "Duniyadari se Aapki kya murad hai?" Farmaya: "Badshaho'n ki pairavi karna. Aur jab Fuqaha aisa karne lagein to unse apne Deen ke baare mein daro."

(Kaafi, v1, p46, h5, Ijtehaad Ke Jalwe, p91)

🤲🏻

...... وَ لَا تَمُدُّنَّ اَعْيُنَكُمْ مِنْهَا اِلٰى مَا مُتِّعَ الْمُتْرَفُوْنَ بِهِ وَ اسْتَهِيْنُوْا بِهَا وَ لا تُوَظِّنُوْهَا وَ اَضِرُّوْا بِاَنْفُسِكُمْ فِيْهَا وَ اِيَّاكُمْ وَ التَّنَعُّمَ وَ التَّلَهِّيَ وَ الْفَاكِهَاتِ، فَاِنَّ فِيْ ذٰلِكَ غَفْلَةً وَ اغْتِرَارًا اٰلَاۤ اِنَّ الدُّنْيَا قَدْ تَنَكَّرَتْ وَ اَدْبَرَتْ وَ احْلَوْلَتْ وَ اٰذَنَتْ بِوَدَاعٍ اَلَا وَ اِنَّ الْاٰخِرَةَ قَدْ رَحَلَتْ فَاَقْبَلَتْ وَ اَشْرَفَتْ وَ اٰذَنَتْ بِاطِّلَاعٍ اَلَا وَ اِنَّ الْمِضْمَارَ الْيَوْمَ وَ السِّبَاقَ غَدًا اَلَا وَ اِنَّ السُّبْقَةَ الْجَنَّةُ وَ الْغَايَةَ النَّارُ اَلَاۤ اَفَلَا تَاۤئِبٌ مِنْ خَطِيْۤئَتِهِ قَبْلَ يَوْمِ مَنِيَّتِهِ اَلَا عَامِلٌ لِنَفْسِهِ قَبْلَ يَوْمِ بُؤْسِهِ.

(Khutba Eid-ul-Fitr, Man La Yahzarul Faqih, Mafateeh)

    ♦ KHUL KAR TABLEEGH ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1803)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَقُلۡ إِنِّیۤ أَنَا ٱلنَّذِیرُ ٱلۡمُبِینُ * كَمَاۤ أَنزَلۡنَا عَلَى ٱلۡمُقۡتَسِمِینَ * ٱلَّذِینَ جَعَلُوا۟ ٱلۡقُرۡءَانَ عِضِینَ * فَوَرَبِّكَ لَنَسۡـَٔلَنَّهُمۡ أَجۡمَعِینَ * عَمَّا كَانُوا۟ یَعۡمَلُونَ.

"Aur Aap keh den ke mein to saaf saaf tanbih karnewala hun. Ye usi tarah ki tanbih hai jaisi Hamne in Tafarraq Parwaazon (Who make Divisions) ki taraf bhejin. Jinhone Kitab e Khuda hisse bant liye the. Aapke Rab ki Qasam! Ham zaroor un sab se sawal karenge jo kuchh woh kiya karte the."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 89 - 93)

https://youtu.be/hP1d2RvuigE

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🗣️

Makkah mein Ailaan e Nabuwwat ke baad AanHazrat (saww) khufiya taur par Tableegh karte rahe aur 3 Saal tak Aap (saww) ne makhsoos afraad ko hi Paigham e Ilahi pahunchaya. Iske baad Allah Ta'ala ne Aap (saww) par ye Ayat nazil farmayi aur is Ayat ke nuzool ke baad AanHazrat (saww) ne khul kar Tableegh e Islam shuru kar di.

🗣️

Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):

"Rasoole Akram (saww) ne 5 Baras tak khufiya Tableegh ki. Aap (saww) khul kar Nabuwwat ka izhaar nahi karte the. Is tamam arse mein Ali (as) wa Khadija (sa) hamesha Aapke sath hote the. Phir Allah Ta'ala ne Aapko khul kar Tableegh ka Hukm diya to Aap (saww) ne alal Ailaan Tableegh shuru kar di."

"Nuzool e Wahy ke baad AanHazrat (saww) 13 Baras tak Makkah mein qayam pazeer rahe aur 3 Saal tak Aapne khufiya Tableegh ki, yaha tak ke Khuda ne Aapko Ailaaniya Tableegh ka Hukm diya to Aap (as) ne khul kar Tableegh shuru ki."

(Kitab Kamaluddin, Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Tum hamare liye apne Aamaal se tableegh karo, na ke Zabaan se. Aisa kaam karo ke log hamari taraf aayein, na ke hum se door aur mutanaffir (nafrat) ho jaayein."

(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v85, p136, Ahlebait (as) Hallale Mushkilaat (Dr. Muhammad Tijani Samaawi), p117)

🤲🏻

 اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا رَسُوْلَ اللّٰهِ اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ اَيُّهَا الْبَشِيْرُ النَّذِيْرُ اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ اَيُّهَا السِّرَاجُ الْمُنِيْرُ اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ اَيُّهَا السَّفِيْرُ بَيْنَ اللّٰهِ وَ بَيْنَ خَلْقِهِ.....

(Ziyarat-e-Rasoole Khuda (saww) 17 Rabiul Awwal, Zaadul Ma'ad Allama Majlis - Mafateeh)

  20th November 2021, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ KHUL KAR TABLEEGH ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1804)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَٱصۡدَعۡ بِمَا تُؤۡمَرُ وَأَعۡرِضۡ عَنِ ٱلۡمُشۡرِكِینَ.

"Aapko jiska Hukm diya ja raha hai use wazeh taur par suna den aur Shirk karne walon ki parwa na karen."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 94)

https://youtu.be/5LlQbPqOkSs

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🗣️

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Ek Din mere Waalid (as) baithe hue the ke unke paas ek shakhs aaya aur usne kaha ke mein Aap (as) se ek mushkil maslah poochhna chahta hun. Aap (as) mujhe ye batayen ke Aap (as) ki taraf khul kal Ilm ka izhaar kyon nahi ho raha, jabke Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne to khul kar apne Ilm ka izhaar kiya tha?

Ye sun kar mere Waalid (as) muskuraye aur farmaya:

"Khuda chahta hai ke Uske Ilm ki ittela sirf us Shakhs ko di jaye jiske Dil ka Imaan ke liye Imtihan liya ja chka ho. Nabi e Akram (saww) ne bhi Be'sat ke ibtidayi saalon mein apni Dawat ko aam nahi kiya tha. Phir jab Aap par Ayat (15:94) nazil hui to Aap (saww) ne apni Dawat ko aam kiya. Haan wo waqt aane wala hai jab is Ummat ka Mahdi (atfs) zahoor karega. Uske saath Farishte honge, jinke haath mein Aale Dawood ki Talwaren hongi  aur unki tadaad itni zyada hogi ke Zameen o Aasmaan unse bhar jayenge. Us waqt Malaika Murda Kafiron ki Arwaah ko Azaab denge aur unke Zinda bhai bandon ki Arwaah ko bhi unke saath shamil karenge."

"Jab mere Waalid e Mohtaram ne ye baat ki to us shakhs ne Niyaam se Talwaar nikali aur kaha: 'Un Talwaaron mein ye Talwaar bhi shamil hogi. Us Zaat ki Qasam Jisne Muhammad (saww) ko tamam Insaano mein se muntakhab kiya. Aisa hi hoga. Phir us shakhs ne apna Amama apne Sar par rakha aur kaha: 'Mein Ilyaas (as) Nabi hun. Meine na-waqfiyat ki wajah se Aap (as) se sawal nahi kiya. Mein sochta tha ke Aap (as) ke saathiyon ki Imaani quwwat mein izaafa ho jaye."

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Baqir (as):

"Jo shakhs jaabir Sultaan (King) ke paas jaaye, use Allah ke Taqwe ki Hidayat aur Maueza (preaching / Tableegh) kare aur Allah ka khauf dilaaye, use Saqlain yaani Jinn o Insaan ke Ajr aur unke Aamaal ke barabar sawaab milega."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v6, p401)

🤲🏻

 يَا رَسُوْلَ اللّٰهِ مَعَ كُلِّ شَاهِدٍ وَ اَتَحَمَّلُهَا عَنْ كُلِّ جَاحِدٍ اَنَّكَ قَدْ بَلَّغْتَ رِسَالَاتِ رَبِّكَ، وَ نَصَحْتَ لِاُمَّتِكَ وَ جَاهَدْتَ فِيْ سَبِيْلِ رَبِّكَ وَ صَدَعْتَ بِاَمْرِهِ وَ احْتَمَلْتَ الْاَذٰى فِيْ جَنْبِهِ وَ دَعَوْتَ اِلٰى سَبِيْلِهِ بِالْحِكْمَةِ وَ الْمَوْعِظَةِ الْحَسَنَةِ الْجَمِيْلَةِ وَ اَدَّيْتَ الْحَقَّ الَّذِيْ كَانَ عَلَيْكَ وَ اَنَّكَ قَدْ رَؤُفْتَ بِالْمُؤْمِنِيْنَ وَ غَلُظْتَ عَلَى الْكَافِرِيْنَ.....

(Ziyarat-e-Rasoole Khuda (saww) 17 Rabiul Awwal, Zaadul Ma'ad Allama Majlis - Mafateeh)

          15th Rabius Sani 1443

    21st November 2021, Sunday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ ISLAM KA MAZAAQ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1805)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَٱصۡدَعۡ بِمَا تُؤۡمَرُ وَأَعۡرِضۡ عَنِ ٱلۡمُشۡرِكِینَ * إِنَّا كَفَیۡنَـٰكَ ٱلۡمُسۡتَهۡزِءِینَ * ٱلَّذِینَ یَجۡعَلُونَ مَعَ ٱللَّهِ إِلَـٰهًا ءَاخَرَۚ فَسَوۡفَ یَعۡلَمُونَ.

"Aapko jiska Hukm diya ja raha hai use wazeh taur par suna den aur Shirk karne walon ki parwa na karen. Aapki taraf se Ham Mazaq udane walon ke liye kafi hain, jo Allah ke saath aur Ma'bood ko bhi Khuda qarar de rahe hain. Iska Anjaam woh anqareeb jaan lenge."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 94 - 96)

https://youtu.be/5LlQbPqOkSs

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

🗣️

Ye Ayat Ailaan e Nabuwwat ki 3 Baras baad nazil hui. AanHazrat (saww) ke Somwar (Monday) Din mab'oos hue the aur Hazrat Ali (as) ne Mangal ke Din izhaar e Islam kiya. Unke baad Hazrat Khadija binte Khwalid ne izhaar e Islam kiya. Hazrat Abu Talib (as) Nabi e Akram (sa) ke Ghar mein aaye. Unke Farzand Jafar bhi unke hamra the. Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ne dekha ke Nabi e Akram (saww) aur Ali (as) Namaz padh rahe hain. Abu Talib (as) ne Jafar se kaha ke tum bhi apne Ibne Am (Cousin) ke saath shamil ho jao. Jafar Nabi e Akram (saww) ki bayen jaanib khade ho gaye.

Iske baad 3 Saal tak Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke peechhe Ali (as), Jafar, Zaid bin Haris aur Khadija (sa) Namaz padhte rahe. 3 Baras ke baad ye Ayat (15 :94-95) nazil farmayi.

🕋

Makkah mein 5 afraad aise the jo AanHazrat (saww) ka Mazaaq udate the aur unke Naam ye hain: 1. Waleed Bin Mughaira, 2. Aas bin Wail, 3. Aswad bin Matlab, 4. Aswad bin Abd Yaghoos, 5. Haris bin Talatah.

👉🏻

(Aur aaj ke daur mein Salman Rushdie, Tasleema Nasreen, *Wasim Mardood* )

AanHazrat (saww) ne Waleed bin Mughaira ke liye Bad-dua ki thi aur Aap (saww) ne kaha tha:

"Khudaya! Ise andha kar aue uske Bete ki Maut ka sadma pahuncha." Chunanche woh Andha ho gaya aur uska Beta Jange Badr mein qatl hua tha. Usi tarah se Aap (as) ne Aswad bin Yaghoos aur Haris bin Talatah Khuzai ke mutalliq bhi bad-Dua ki thi.

👉🏻

Jab Islam ke Mazaaq udhane aur Tauheen e Risaalat ki ye Saza Khuda de raha hai to kya Wasim Mardood is Etaab e Ilahi se bach sakta hai, jabke khud apni Chita jalane ki qubool kar raha hai.

👉🏻

Ab ham denkhenge ke Jinhone Tauheen e Risaalat ki aur Islam ka Mazaaq udaya unka kya hashr hua.

(To be Cont'd.....)

 اَللّٰهُمَّ الْعَنِ الَّذِيْنَ بَدَّلُوْا نِعْمَتَكَ وَ اتَّهَمُوْا نَبِيَّكَ وَ جَحَدُوْا بِاٰيَاتِكَ وَ سَخِرُوْا بِاِمَامِكَ وَ حَمَلُوْا النَّاسَ عَلٰۤى اَكْتَافِ اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ اَللّٰهُمَّ اِنِّيۤ اَتَقَرَّبُ اِلَيْكَ بِاللَّعْنَةِ عَلَيْهِمْ وَ الْبَرَاۤءَةِ مِنْهُمْ فِيْ الدُّنْيَا وَ الْاٰخِرَةِ يَا رَحْمَانُ۔.....

(Ziyarat-e-Imam Reza (as) - Mafateeh)

    22nd November 2021, Monday

      ♦ ISLAM KA MAZAAQ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1806)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَٱصۡدَعۡ بِمَا تُؤۡمَرُ وَأَعۡرِضۡ عَنِ ٱلۡمُشۡرِكِینَ * إِنَّا كَفَیۡنَـٰكَ ٱلۡمُسۡتَهۡزِءِینَ * ٱلَّذِینَ یَجۡعَلُونَ مَعَ ٱللَّهِ إِلَـٰهًا ءَاخَرَۚ فَسَوۡفَ یَعۡلَمُونَ.

"Aapko jiska Hukm diya ja raha hai use wazeh taur par suna den aur Shirk karne walon ki parwa na karen. Aapki taraf se Ham Mazaq udane walon ke liye kafi hain, jo Allah ke saath aur Ma'bood ko bhi Khuda qarar de rahe hain. Iska Anjaam woh anqareeb jaan lenge."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 94 - 96)

https://youtu.be/5LlQbPqOkSs

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Us daur mein bhi aur aaj ke daur mein bhi Qur'an o Risaalat ka Mazaaq udaya jata raha hai. Aaj bhi Salman Rushdie, Tasleema Nasreen, Wasim Mardood in logon mein shamil hain.

AanHazrat (saww) ne Waleed bin Mughaira ke liye Bad-dua ki thi aur Aap (saww) ne kaha tha:

"Khudaya! Ise andha kar aue uske Bete ki Maut ka sadma pahuncha." Chunanche woh Andha ho gaya aur uska Beta Jange Badr mein qatl hua tha. Usi tarah se Aap (as) ne Aswad bin Yaghoos aue Haris bin Talatah Khuzai ke mutalliq bhi bad-Dua ki thi.

Jis zamane mein Waleed Andha nahi hua tha ek bar woh Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke saamne se guzra. Us waqt Hazrat Jibrael Amin (as) bhi AanHazrat (saww) ke saath baithe hue the. Jibrael Amin (as) ne Aap (saww) se kaha: "Ye Waleed bin Mughaira hai aur ye Aapka Mazaaq udane walon mein shamil hai."

Aap (saww) ne farmaya: " Ji haan."

Bani Khaza'ah ka ek shakhs Lohaar tha aur woh Waleed ke liye Teer taraash raha tha. Waleed jab uske paas gaya to uski edi Teer ki ani par ja lagi aur uski se Khoon baha.

Hazrat Jibrael (as) ne uski edi ki taraf ishara kiya. Waleed ghar aaya aur aa kar apne Bistar par let gaya. Uski edi se betahasha Khoon jaari hua aur Khoon behta hua uski Beti ke Bistar par pahuncha. Uski Beti ne Kaneez ko awaaz de kar kaha: "Dekho kya Mashk ka Munh khul gaya hai?"

Waleed ne Beti se kaha: "Nahi, ye Mashk ka Paani nahi, ye tere Baap ka Khoon hai. Apne Bhaiyyon, Bhatijon ko bulao mein marne wala hun."

Waleed ki Beti ne qareebi Rishtedaron ko bulaya. Waleed ne Abdullah bin Rabiah se kaha ke mera Beta Amara bin Waleed Habasha ki sar zameen par sargardan ho kar phir raha hai. Mere marne ke baad Muhammad (saww) se Najashi ke naam par sifarashi Khat likhwana ke woh use wapas Makkah bhej de.

(Story to be Cont'd.....)

👉🏻

*Wasim Mardood* ka bhi aisa hi hashr hoga.

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Insaan jis qadr Mizaah (Mazaaq) karta hai, usi qadr apni Aql ka ek hissa alag kar deta hai."

(Nahjul Balagah, p787)

🤲🏻

 .........فَكُوْنُوْا لِيْ شُفَعَاۤءَ، فَقَدْ وَفَدْتُ اِلَيْكُمْ اِذْ رَغِبَ عَنْكُمْ اَهْلُ الدُّنْيَا وَ اتَّخَذُوْا اٰيَاتِ اللّٰهِ هُزُوًا وَ اسْتَكْبَرُوْا عَنْهَا۔.....

(Ziyarat-e-Imam Reza (as) - Mafateeh)

          17th Rabius Sani 1443

   23rd November 2021, Tuesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ ISLAM KA MAZAAQ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1807)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَٱصۡدَعۡ بِمَا تُؤۡمَرُ وَأَعۡرِضۡ عَنِ ٱلۡمُشۡرِكِینَ * إِنَّا كَفَیۡنَـٰكَ ٱلۡمُسۡتَهۡزِءِینَ * ٱلَّذِینَ یَجۡعَلُونَ مَعَ ٱللَّهِ إِلَـٰهًا ءَاخَرَۚ فَسَوۡفَ یَعۡلَمُونَ.

"Aapko jiska Hukm diya ja raha hai use wazeh taur par suna den aur Shirk karne walon ki parwa na karen. Aapki taraf se Ham Mazaq udane walon ke liye kafi hain, jo Allah ke saath aur Ma'bood ko bhi Khuda qarar de rahe hain. Iska Anjaam woh anqareeb jaan lenge."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 94 - 96)

https://youtu.be/5LlQbPqOkSs

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Us daur mein bhi aur aaj ke daur mein bhi Qur'an o Risaalat ka Mazaaq udaya jata raha hai. Aaj bhi Salman Rushdie, Tasleema Nasreen, Wasim Mardood in logon mein shamil hain.

AanHazrat (saww) ne Waleed bin Mughaira ke liye Bad-dua ki thi aur Aap (saww) ne kaha tha:

"Khudaya! Ise andha kar aue uske Bete ki Maut ka sadma pahuncha."

(1) Jis zamane mein Waleed Andha nahi hua tha ek bar woh Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke saamne se guzra. Us waqt Hazrat Jibrael Amin (as) bhi AanHazrat (saww) ke saath baithe hue the. Jibrael Amin (as) ne Aap (saww) se kaha: "Ye Waleed bin Mughaira hai aur ye Aapka Mazaaq udane walon mein shamil hai."

Aap(saww) ne farmaya:  " Ji haan."

Phir usne (Waleed bin Mughaira) apne chhote bhai Hashim se kaha ke beta meri chand Wasiyyaten hain unko ghaur se suno. Pehli Wasiyyat ye hai ke tum Abu Dahem Dosi ko Qatl karna, kyonki usne apni beti se meri shadi ki thi, lekin usne phir mujh se meri Biwi chheen li thi, agar meri Biwi mere ghar hoti to usse bhi tujh jaisa beta paida hota.

Bani Khaza'ah ke ek shakhs ki ghalti se mein mar raha hun, lekin unhone mere Qatl ka iraada nahi kiya tha aur mujhe khauf hai ke kahin mere baad tum kisi Azmaish mein na aa jao. Iske bawajood meri Maut ki zimmedari Bani Khaza'ah par hi aayed hoti hai. Meine Bani Saqeef se Sood lena hai, mere baad tum un se Sood lena aur mein Asqaf Najran ka 200 Dinar ka maqrooz hun, tum wo Qarz zaroor ada karna. Iske baad woh mar gaya.

(2) Rabi'a bin Aswad Hazrat Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke paas se guzra. Us waqt Jibrael Amin (as) AanHazrat (saww) ke paas maujood the. Unhone uski Aankhon ki taraf ishaara kiya. Woh Andha ho kar mar gaya..

(3) Aswad bin Abe Yaghoos AanHazrat (saww) ke paas se guzra to Jibrael (as) ne uske Shikam (stomach) ki taraf ishaara kiya. Usko Pyaas ki Bimaari ho gayi. Woh jitna bhi Paani peeta to uski Pyaas na bujhti thi. Paani peete peete akhirkar uska Pet phat gaya aur woh Jahannam raseed hua.

(4) Aas bin Wael AanHazrat (saww) ke paas se guzra. Jibrael (as) ne uske Paaon ki taraf ishaara kiya. Us waqt ek tez dhaar lakdi uske Paaon ke talwe mein chubhi, jo upar wale hisse se baramad hui. Chunanche woh bhi mar gaya.

(5) Ibne Talatah AanHazrat (saww) ke paas se guzra to Jibrael (as) ne uske Chehre ki taraf ishaara kiya. Woh 'Tahama' ke kisi Pahad ki taraf gaya jahan use sakht Loo lagi aur use Pyaas (Dehydration) ka Marz lahaq hua. Akhirkar Paani peete peete uska Pet phat gaya aur woh mar gaya.

Yun Allah Ta'ala ne Apne Habib se Ayat (15:95) ka Waada poora kiya.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

👉🏻

*Wasim Mardood* aur doosre logon ka bhi aisa hi hashr hoga Inshallah.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v6, p725)

      ♦ TABLEEGH-E-ISLAM ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1808)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَٱصۡدَعۡ بِمَا تُؤۡمَرُ وَأَعۡرِضۡ عَنِ ٱلۡمُشۡرِكِینَ * إِنَّا كَفَیۡنَـٰكَ ٱلۡمُسۡتَهۡزِءِینَ * ٱلَّذِینَ یَجۡعَلُونَ مَعَ ٱللَّهِ إِلَـٰهًا ءَاخَرَۚ فَسَوۡفَ یَعۡلَمُونَ.

"Aapko jiska Hukm diya ja raha hai use wazeh taur par suna den aur Shirk karne walon ki parwa na karen. Aapki taraf se Ham Mazaq udane walon ke liye kafi hain, jo Allah ke saath aur Ma'bood ko bhi Khuda qarar de rahe hain. Iska Anjaam woh anqareeb jaan lenge."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 94 - 96)

https://youtu.be/5LlQbPqOkSs

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Aapne dekha ke kis tarah Islam ke Mazaq udane walon ka hashr hua.

Wasim Mardood ke baqool Islam Duniya ka doosra sab se bada mazhab aise hi nahi ho gaya balke ye ek sazish ke tahet Rasool Akram (saww) ne kaam kiya. Is Mardood ko ye nahi pata ke ye Ilahi Deen hai ye koi Insaan ka paida karda nahi. Yehi nazariya Quraish ka tha aur Islam ki Hifazat mein Mohsin e Islam Hazrat  Abu Talib (as) ka ahem kirdar hai.

Tafseer mulaheza farmayen:

Allah Ta'ala ne jab khul kar Ailaan e Nabuwwat ka Hukm diya to Aap (saww) Hajre Ismael par tashreef laye aur farmaya:

"Aye Giroh e Quraish! Aye Giroh e Arab! Mein tumhe Allah ki Tauheed aur apni Risaalat ke Iqraar ki Dawat  deta hun aur mein tumhe hukm deta hun ke tumne Khuda ke jo hamsar (equals) bana rakhe hain aur jin Buton ki Pooja kar rahe ho, unko chhod do aur mein tumse Waada karta hun ke agar tumne meri pairavi ki to Arab o Ajam par tumhari Hukumat hogi aur tum Jannat mein Badshah banoge."

AanHazrat (saww) ki ye guftugu sun kar logon ne Aapka Mazaaq udaya aur kehne lage ke (Nauzobillah) Muhammad (saww) Diwana ho gaya hai. (Wasim ki tarah)

Phir Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ke rob ki wajah se kisi ko AanHazrat (saww) par haath uthane ki jura'at na hui.

Quraish ikatthe ho kar Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ke paas aaye aur unse kaha ke Aap apne bhatije ki khabar len. Ye hamare Aqaed ko Pagalpan se tabeer karta hai aur hamare ma'boodon ko bura bhala kehta hai aur hamare jawano ko gumrah kar raha hai aur hamari jamat mein intishaar paida kar raha hai. Agar use Daulat ki zaroorat hai to ham uske liye itni Daulat jama kar denge ke poore Arab ka Daulatmand shakhs ban jayega. Aur agar woh kisi haseen o jameel Aurat se shaadi karna chahta hai to ham uski shaadi kara dete hain. Ham iska har mutalba poora karne par amada hain, lekin Aap usse kahen ke woh apni Tableegh se baaz aa jaye.

Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ne is baat ka zikr AanHazrat (saww) se kiya to Aap (saww) ne farmaya:

"Chacha jaan! Mein apne Rab ke Farman ki mukhalefat nahi kar sakta."

Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ne farmaya: "Ab Aap (saww) khul kar Tableegh karen. Mein qadam qadam par Aap (saww) ka saath dunga."

🤲🏻

Wasim Mardood par Allah ki La'anat ho

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

 ----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Phir kuchh Din ke baad Quraish ne Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ko lalach bhi diya aur dhamki bhi di.

Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ne unko dhutkara aur karara jawab diya:

Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ne taweel Qaseeda padha:

و لما رأيت القوم لاود بينهم

و قد قطعوا كل العرىٰ و الوسائل

كذبتم و بيت الله يبزى محمد

و لما نطاعن دونه و نناضل

و ننصره حتى نصرع حوله

و نذهل عن ابناننا و الحلائل.

"Jab meine dekha ke Qaum mein Muhabbat nahi rahi aur unhone har tarah ke rishton ko kaat diya hai.

Baitullah ki Qasam! Tumne jhoot kaha hai ke ham Muhammad (saww) ko be sahara chhod denge, abhi to hamne unke saamne na to Teer chalaye hain aur na hi Neze chalaye hain.

Ham Muhammad (saww) ki madad karenge, yahan tak ke apne Beton aur Biwiyon ko faramosh kar denge aur Parwaano ki tarah unke gird kat marenge."

Ye hai wasim Mardood jaise logon ko Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ka karara jawab.

🤲🏻

 ......... فَقَدْ وَفَدْتُ اِلَيْكُمْ اِذْ رَغِبَ عَنْكُمْ اَهْلُ الدُّنْيَا وَ اتَّخَذُوْا اٰيَاتِ اللّٰهِ هُزُوًا وَ اسْتَكْبَرُوْا عَنْهَا۔.....

(Ziyarat-e-Imam Reza (as) - Mafateeh)

      ♦ MOHSIN-E-ISLAM ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1809)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَٱصۡدَعۡ بِمَا تُؤۡمَرُ وَأَعۡرِضۡ عَنِ ٱلۡمُشۡرِكِینَ * إِنَّا كَفَیۡنَـٰكَ ٱلۡمُسۡتَهۡزِءِینَ * ٱلَّذِینَ یَجۡعَلُونَ مَعَ ٱللَّهِ إِلَـٰهًا ءَاخَرَۚ فَسَوۡفَ یَعۡلَمُونَ.*

"Aapko jiska Hukm diya ja raha hai use wazeh taur par suna den aur Shirk karne walon ki parwa na karen. Aapki taraf se Ham Mazaq udane walon ke liye kafi hain, jo Allah ke saath aur Ma'bood ko bhi Khuda qarar de rahe hain. Iska Anjaam woh anqareeb jaan lenge."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 94 - 96)

https://youtu.be/5LlQbPqOkSs

📚📖

👉 Tafseer: (Cont'd)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Tableegh e Islam mein Mohsin e Islam Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ka ahem kirdar hai.

🤝🏻

Phir Quraish ne ek Moaheda (Agreement) likha ke jab tak Bani Hashim Muhammad (saww) ko hamare hawale na karenge us waqt tak unka Ma'asherati (Economical) Boycott kiya jayega.

Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ne Bani Hashim ko jama kiya aur unse farmaya:

"Tumhe Baitullah, Rukn o Maqam aur Mashharul Haraam ki Qasam! Agar Muhammad (saww) ko ek kaanta bhi chubh gaya to mein tumhe maaf nahi karunga."_ Iske baad Hazrat Abu Talib (as) apne Khandaan ko le kar Ghaati mein chale aaye jise Shobe Abi Talib kaha jata hai. Aapne wahan Chaar Saal tak Din Raat Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki hifazat ka fariza sar anjaam diya.

Akhirkar Moaheda ki tehreer khatm ho gayi. Hazrat Abu Talib (as) Rasoole Khuda (saww) ko le kar Ghaati se bahar aaye. Ghaati ke nikalne ke chand roz baad Aapka waqte akhir aa gaya. Rasoole Khuda (saww) Aap (as) ke paas aaye. Us waqt Aap (as) Zindagi ki akheri saanse le rahe the, Aap (saww) ne farmaya:

"Chacha jaan! Allah Ta'ala meri taraf se tumhe Jazae Khair ata farmaye. Aap (as) ne Bachpan mein meri parvarish ki aur Jawani mein meri hifazat ki." 

Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ne Aap (as) ke farman par amal kiya.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

📚

Hazrat Abu Talib (as) Momin e Kamil the. Aap (as) ne AanHazrat (saww) ki hifazat ki gharz se apne Deen ko makhfi rakha. Iman e Abu Talib (as) ke bare etraazat ghalat hain. Hadis wa Riwayat se bhi sabit hai. Allama Amini ne Kitab Al Ghadeer, Vol 7 mein Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ke hawale mufassal zikr kiya hai.

🤲🏻

Wasim Mardood par Allah ki La'anat ho jisne Tauheen e Risaalat ki

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

 ----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Phir kuchh Din ke baad Quraish ne Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ko lalach bhi diya aur dhamki bhi di.

Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ne unko dhutkara aur karara jawab diya:

(Yehi hai wasim Mardood jaise logon ko Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ka karara jawab.)

Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ne taweel Qaseeda padha:

*و لما رأيت القوم لاود بينهم*  

*و قد قطعوا كل العرىٰ و الوسائل*

*كذبتم و بيت الله يبزى محمد*  

*و لما نطاعن دونه و نناضل*

*و ننصره حتى نصرع حوله*

*و نذهل عن ابناننا و الحلائل.*

"Jab meine dekha ke Qaum mein Muhabbat nahi rahi aur unhone har tarah ke rishton ko kaat diya hai.

Baitullah ki Qasam! Tumne jhoot kaha hai ke ham Muhammad (saww) ko be sahara chhod denge, abhi to hamne unke saamne na to Teer chalaye hain aur na hi Neze chalaye hain.

Ham Muhammad (saww) ki madad karenge, yahan tak ke apne Beton aur Biwiyon ko faramosh kar denge aur Parwaano ki tarah unke gird kat marenge."

🤲🏻

 *......... فَقَدْ وَفَدْتُ اِلَيْكُمْ اِذْ رَغِبَ عَنْكُمْ اَهْلُ الدُّنْيَا وَ اتَّخَذُوْا اٰيَاتِ اللّٰهِ هُزُوًا وَ اسْتَكْبَرُوْا عَنْهَا۔.....*

(Ziyarat-e-Imam Reza (as) - Mafateeh)

♦ DUSHMANAN-E-ISLAM KA HASHR ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1810)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَٱصۡدَعۡ بِمَا تُؤۡمَرُ وَأَعۡرِضۡ عَنِ ٱلۡمُشۡرِكِینَ * إِنَّا كَفَیۡنَـٰكَ ٱلۡمُسۡتَهۡزِءِینَ * ٱلَّذِینَ یَجۡعَلُونَ مَعَ ٱللَّهِ إِلَـٰهًا ءَاخَرَۚ فَسَوۡفَ یَعۡلَمُونَ.*

"Aapko jiska Hukm diya ja raha hai use wazeh taur par suna den aur Shirk karne walon ki parwa na karen. Aapki taraf se Ham Mazaq udane walon ke liye kafi hain, jo Allah ke saath aur Ma'bood ko bhi Khuda qarar de rahe hain. Iska Anjaam woh anqareeb jaan lenge."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 94 - 96)

https://youtu.be/5LlQbPqOkSs

📚📖

👉 Tafseer: (Cont'd)

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚 ⁉️

Imam Husain (as):

"Mulke Sham (Syria) se ek Yahoodi Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ke paas aaya aur usne kaha: 'Ham Hazrat Musa (as) ke Pairokar hain aur aap Hazrat Muhammad Mustafa (saww) ke Pairokar hain. Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Musa (as) ko Firaun ki taraf rawana kiya aur unhone Firaun ke saamne Aayat e Kubra pesh ki. Kya tumhare Nabi (saww) ko bhi ye maqam hasil hua?

👉🏻

Hazrat Ali (as) ne farmaya:

"Tumne bilkul sach kaha, lekin suno Hazrat Musa (as) ka muqabile akele Firaun se tha jabke hamare Nabi (saww) ko Abu Jahel bin Hisham, Atba bin Rabia, Shaiba, Abul Bakhtari, Nazar bin Hirs, Ubai bin Khalaf, Manbah wa Baniyah ibne Hajjaj aur Mazaaq udane wale kayi Firauno ka muqabila karna pada tha jin mein Waleed bin Mughaira Makhzoomi, Aas bin Wail Sehmi, Aswad bin And e Yaghoos Zohri, Aswad bin Muttalib aur Haaris bin Talata sare fehrist hain." (Aaj ke daur mein Wasim Rushdie)

"AanHazrat (saww) ne unhe Anfus o Afaaq (Self & Heaven) ki Ayaat dikhlayin, yahan tak ke unke saamne ye baat wazeh ho gayi ke Aapka Paigham Haq par mabni hai."

⁉️

Yahoodi ne kaha ke Allah ne Firaun se inteqaam liya tha, kya tumhare Nabi (saww) ke mukhalefeen se bhi Allah ne inteqaam liya?

Imam Husain (as):

Yahoodi ne kaha ke Allah ne Firaun se inteqaam liya tha, kya tumhare Nabi (saww) ke mukhalefeen se bhi Allah ne inteqaam liya?

👉🏻

Hazrat Ali (as):

"Ji haan! Allah Ta'ala ne Firaun sifat mukhalefeen se bhi inteqaam liya. Allah ne Mazaaq udane walon ke liye farmaya: "Aap ki taraf se ham Mazaaq udane walon ke liye kaafi hain" (15:95) Allah Ta'ala ne Paancho Mazaaq karne walon ko ek hi Din mein mukhtalif asbaab se halaak kiya."

(Ye bayan kar chuke hain)

"(In short) Waleed bin Mughaira Teer ki ani chubhne se halak hua.

Aas bin Wail Sehmi ek Patthar se takra kar Munh ke bal gira aur mar gaya.

Aswad bin Yaghoos ka Ped se takraya aur halaak hua.

Aswad bin Haaris AanHazrat (saww) ki Bad-Dua se Andha ho gaya aur uska Beta mar gaya.

Haaris Bin Talata sakht garmi ki wajah se Habshi ban gaya. Gharwalon ne hi use maar diya.

In sab ne marte waqt yehi kaha 'Mujhe Rabbe Muhammad (saww) ne qatl kiya hai.'

(Ehtejaj e Tabarsi, Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

To kya Wasim Mardood Etaab e Ilahi se bach payega?

🤲🏻

Bare Ilaha Wasim Mardood ka bhi aisa hi Hashr ho jisne Tauheen e Risaalat ki

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

 ----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Quran, Allah ke baad, har shay se afzal hai. Jisne Quran ki izzat ki goya usne Allah ki izzat ki aur jisne Quran ki izzat na ki goya usne Allah ki tauheen ki."

(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v9, p27)

Imam Ali (as):

"Jo shakhs kisi Musalman ke liye tauheen-aamez (insulting) baat kare, Allah use Dozakh mein 'Teenat e Khubaal' (bad-kaar Aurato'n ki Peep) mein qaid karega aur woh us waqt tak waha'n qaid rahega jab tak woh apne alfaaz ki taujih (explanation) pesh na kare."

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p624)

🤲🏻

 *......... فَقَدْ وَفَدْتُ اِلَيْكُمْ اِذْ رَغِبَ عَنْكُمْ اَهْلُ الدُّنْيَا وَ اتَّخَذُوْا اٰيَاتِ اللّٰهِ هُزُوًا وَ اسْتَكْبَرُوْا عَنْهَا۔.....*

(Ziyarat-e-Imam Reza (as) - Mafateeh)

   ♦ SEENA TANGI KA ILAAJ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1811)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَقَدۡ نَعۡلَمُ أَنَّكَ یَضِیقُ صَدۡرُكَ بِمَا یَقُولُونَ * فَسَبِّحۡ بِحَمۡدِ رَبِّكَ وَكُن مِّنَ ٱلسَّـٰجِدِینَ * وَٱعۡبُدۡ رَبَّكَ حَتَّىٰ یَأۡتِیَكَ ٱلۡیَقِینُ.*

"Ham Jaante hain ke jo kuchh ye log baaten bana rahe hain usse Aapke Seene mein tangi mehsoos hoti hai. Aap apne Rab ki Hamd ke saath Tasbeeh karen aur Sajdah guzaron mein shamil ho jayen aur Aap Maut aane tak apne Rab ki Ibaadat karte rahen."

(Surah Al-Hijr: 97 - 99)

https://youtu.be/5LlQbPqOkSs

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

https://shiachannel.in/library/tafseer.html?id=1

📚

Kuffar o Mushrekeen ke taane aur unki aziyyat bhari baaten sun kar AanHazrat (saww) ko Seena mein tangi mehsoos hoti thi.

Aur kyon na ho, aaj har sachche Musalman o Momin Seena o Dil mein tangi mehsoos karta hai jab Kuffar o Zalim Hukumat ke hamnawaon ke taane baane sunta hai. Roz baroz Musalmano ke khilaf bayan aate rehte hain, roz ek naya zeher ugla jata hai. Jisse Muslim wa Non-Muslim ke darmiyan Tafarraqa bazi ki jati hai.

Allah Ta'ala ne Aap (saww) ko iske Ilaaj ke liye 3 Umoor ka Hukm diya:

(1) Apne Rab ki Hamd ke saath Tasbeeh karen.

(2) Namaz padhen. Ayat mein zikr hai ke Aap (saww) Sajdah guzaron mein shamil ho jayen. Iski wajah ye hai ke Sajdah Namaz ka buland tareen Rukn hai.

(3) Maut waarid hone tak Bandagi karte rahen.

"Yaqeen" us Ilm ko kaha jata hai jo Hijab uth jaane ke baad hasil ho, kyonki Maut se bhi Ghaib ke Parde uth jaate hain aur Aalam e Bala ke Haqaiq saamne aate hain. Isiliye Maut ko Lafz "Yaqeen" se tabeer kiya gaya hai.

Ayat وَكُن مِّنَ ٱلسَّـٰجِدِینَ ka mafhoom ye hai ke Aap (saww) Nama guzaron mein shamil rahen. Ibne Abbas ka bayan hai ke Rasoole Khuda (saww) jab bhi pareshan hote to Aap (saww) Namaz padhne lag jate the.

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jo Sabr karta hai to use bhi to thode arse ke liyeapne  Sabr karna padta hai aur jo Be-Sabri karta hai to woh bhi thode arse tak Be-Sabri mein mubtila hota hai, tumhe apne tamam mamelaat mein Sabr se kaam lena chahiye. Allah Ta'ala ne Apne Habib (saww) ko mab'oos farmaya to unhe bhi Sabr aur Namr mizaaji ka Hukm diya."

"AanHazrat (saww) ne Sabr kiya. Logon ne Aap (saww) par badi tohmaten bandhi jisse Aap (saww) ko Seene mein tangi mehsoos hui, tab Allah Ta'ala ne ye Ayat (15:97-99) nazil farmayi."

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

Surah Al-Hijr ki Tafseer Tamam hui.

THE END

🤲🏻

 *اَللّٰهُمَّ طَهِّرْ بِهِ قَلْبِيْ وَ اشْرَحْ بِهِ صَدْرِيْ وَ سَهِّلْ لِيْ بِهِ اَمْرِيْ ۔*

(Ziyarat e Imam Husain (as) - Mafateeh)
